### [1] [Photon-mediated entanglement between spin qubits beyond the dispersive regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12900)
*Andrei Nikitchenko,Guido Burkard*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 该理论研究展示了在Si/SiGe异质结构中，两个通过共享腔体色散耦合的远距离自旋量子比特可以通过实光子交换实现快速纠缠，为共振耦合的半导体自旋量子比特量子门开发铺平道路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索通过共振操作加速远距离量子比特纠缠的可能性，利用实光子交换替代传统的虚光子交换，以提升纠缠速度和鲁棒性。

Method: 采用理论计算方法，分析Si/SiGe异质结构中双量子点内两个电子自旋量子比特与共享腔体组成的复合系统动力学，假设两个自旋量子比特均可调谐至与腔体共振或失谐。

Result: 计算表明，两个自旋量子比特之间的实光子交换能够产生快速纠缠，且这种纠缠对退相干具有鲁棒性，显著优于传统的色散耦合机制。

Conclusion: 该研究为开发基于共振耦合的远距离半导体自旋量子比特（semiconductor spin qubits）的量子门提供了理论基础，展示了实光子交换在量子信息处理中的优势。

Abstract: Dispersively coupled distant qubits in a shared cavity can become entangled through virtual photon exchange with energy-conserving phase evolution of their quantum states. This interaction can potentially be accelerated by operating on resonance, allowing for the exchange of real photons. In this theoretical study, we examine photon-mediated entanglement between two distant spins of electrons confined in double quantum dots formed in a Si/SiGe heterostructure. We calculate the dynamics of the combined system comprised of both spin qubits and the cavity, assuming that both spin qubits can be tuned into and out of resonance with the host cavity. We demonstrate that the exchange of real photons between the two spin qubits can result in rapid entanglement that is robust against decoherence. These results pave the way for the development of quantum gates on resonantly coupled distant semiconductor spin qubits.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.stat-mech'></div>

# cond-mat.stat-mech [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [The Fisher Paradox: Dissipation Interference in Information-Regularized Gradient Flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12285)
*Michael Farmer,Abhinav Kochar,Yugyung Lee*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文揭示了Fisher正则化Wasserstein梯度流中一种先前未被识别的干涉机制：当状态宽度低于临界尺度时，交叉耗散项符号变为正，导致几何Fisher通道暂时阻碍基线自由能泛函下降，形成所谓的Fisher悖论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Fisher正则化Wasserstein梯度流中存在的特殊干涉机制，该机制在状态宽度低于临界尺度时导致交叉耗散项符号反转，从而阻碍自由能泛函下降。

Method: 将流限制在高斯流形上，得到精确的Riccati型方差方程及其闭式轨迹；同时在512点网格上进行有限差分模拟，并在双峰和拉普拉斯初始条件下进行数值实验验证。

Result: 发现了三个由两个临界尺度分隔的动力学区域：sigma=1（交叉耗散符号翻转）和sigma=sqrt(epsilon)（Fisher接管）；方差势V(u)=u^2-2u-epsilon ln(u)包含对数离心势垒，使平衡吸引子偏移Delta sigma≈epsilon/4；干涉持续时间t_cross~D_KL与初始信息距离直接相关。

Conclusion: Fisher正则化Wasserstein梯度流中存在显著的干涉机制，该机制在高斯闭包之外仍然存在，对信息几何耗散动力学具有直接意义；所有解析预测均得到数值验证，平均相对误差在5.21×10^-4以内。

Abstract: We show that Fisher-regularized Wasserstein gradient flows exhibit a previously unrecognized interference mechanism in their dissipation identity: a cross-dissipation term whose sign becomes positive when the state width falls below a critical scale. In this regime the geometric Fisher channel transiently opposes descent of the baseline free-energy functional, producing what we term the Fisher Paradox. Restricting the flow to the Gaussian manifold yields an exact Riccati-type variance equation with a closed-form trajectory, exposing three dynamical regimes separated by two critical scales: sigma = 1 (cross-dissipation sign flip) and sigma = sqrt(epsilon) (Fisher takeover). The variance potential V(u) = u^2 - 2u - epsilon ln(u) contains a logarithmic centrifugal barrier that shifts the equilibrium attractor by Delta sigma approx epsilon/4. The interference persists for a duration t_cross ~ D_KL, linking the dissipation delay directly to the initial information distance. Finite-difference simulations on a 512-point grid confirm all analytical predictions to within 5.21 x 10^-4 mean relative error. Numerical experiments with bimodal and Laplace initial conditions confirm the effect persists beyond Gaussian closure, with direct implications for information-geometric dissipative dynamics.

</details>


### [3] [Impact of currents on non-equilibrium coexistence in chemically driven mixtures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12481)
*E. Meyberg,J. F. Robinson,T. Speck*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在非平衡条件下，分子通过身份切换（identity switching）调控相互作用的自组织过程，推导了广义吉布斯共存判据（generalized Gibbs coexistence criteria），揭示了化学势差与界面电流之间的平衡关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生物功能源于分子在时空中的自组织，但细胞拥挤的非平衡环境使这一过程复杂化。研究旨在揭示大分子在守恒总浓度下通过身份切换（identity switching）调控相互作用的自组织普适原理。

Method: 通过局部细致平衡条件（local detailed balance condition）确保热力学一致性，推导二元混合物稳态共存浓度判据。采用非恒定跃迁速率和锐界面近似（sharp-interface approximation），获得广义吉布斯共存判据的跳跃条件。

Result: 推导的跳跃条件将吉布斯共存判据（Gibbs' coexistence criteria）推广到非平衡情形，表明化学势差与界面区域受限的电流相平衡。这些条件连接了单个物种的化学势差异与其在界面区域的电流。

Conclusion: 研究建立了非平衡条件下分子自组织的理论框架，通过身份切换机制和热力学一致性约束，揭示了广义共存判据如何平衡化学势差与界面电流，为理解细胞环境中的大分子组织提供了新视角。

Abstract: Virtually every biological function emerges through the organization of molecules in time and space. Consequently, a major challenge in statistical physics is to uncover the universal principles governing macromolecular self-organization within the crowded, non-equilibrium environment of the cell. Here, we investigate a class of models where molecules maintain a conserved total concentration but can switch "identities", thereby modulating their intermolecular interactions. By enforcing thermodynamic consistency via the local detailed balance condition, we derive the steady-state criteria determining coexisting concentrations in a binary mixture. For non-constant transition rates and using a sharp-interface approximation, we obtain jump conditions that generalize Gibbs' coexistence criteria of equal pressure and chemical potential. We demonstrate that these jumps balance the chemical potential differences of individual species against their currents, which are confined to the interfacial region.

</details>


### [4] [Out-of-equilibrium percolation transitions at finite critical times after quenches across magnetic first-order transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13127)
*Andrea Pelissetto,Davide Rossini,Ettore Vicari*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究展示了铁磁伊辛（Ising）系统在淬火（quench）跨越一级相变线时会发生非平衡渗流（percolation）转变，其特征时间与磁场强度呈指数依赖关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究铁磁伊辛系统在淬火跨越一级磁相变线后的非平衡动力学行为，特别是探索从亚稳态到稳定态的转变过程中出现的渗流临界现象。

Method: 以二维伊辛系统为范例，通过淬火磁场从负值变为正值来驱动系统跨越低温一级相变线，在纯弛豫动力学下研究系统演化。

Result: 在热力学极限下，系统演化在有限临界时间发生动态转变，表现为正负自旋最大团簇的渗流；该非平衡渗流转变具有有限尺寸标度行为，但临界指数与随机渗流不同且依赖于磁场强度。

Conclusion: 非平衡渗流临界行为与磁化强度在弱磁场极限下的类旋节（spinodal-like）行为相关，导致渗流时间对磁场强度呈现类旋节指数依赖关系。

Abstract: We show that an out-of-equilibrium percolation transition occurs after quenching ferromagnetic Ising-like systems across their magnetic first-order transitions. As a paradigmatic example, we consider a two-dimensional Ising system driven across its low-temperature first-order transition line by a quench of the magnetic field $h$ from $h_i<0$ to $h>0$. In the thermodynamic limit and for finite values of $h$, the post-quench evolution under a purely relaxational dynamics is characterized by a dynamic transition at a finite critical time $t_c(h)$ from the metastable negatively magnetized phase to the positive one, marked by the percolation of the largest clusters of positive and negative spins. This out-of-equilibrium percolation transition displays a finite-size scaling behavior as in the standard random-percolation case. However, while the fractal dimension of the percolating clusters is consistent with the random-percolation value, the exponent controlling the approach to criticality differs and depends on $h$. We also show that the percolation critical behavior is related to the spinodal-like behavior of the magnetization in the small-$h$ limit, which implies that the percolation time $t_c(h)$ exhibits a spinodal-like exponential dependence on $h$.

</details>


### [5] [Towers of quantum many-body scars under stochastic resetting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13165)
*Lorenzo Gotta,Manas Kulkarni,Gabriele Perfetto*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究提出通过随机重置（stochastic resetting）协议来制备量子多体疤痕（quantum many-body scars）的局部性质，将疤痕动力学与向简单非纠缠乘积态（unentangled product states）的随机重置交错进行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子多体疤痕（quantum many-body scars）作为非可积哈密顿量（nonintegrable Hamiltonians）的高度激发本征态，其动力学表现出非热行为（athermal behavior）和持续振荡，但由于其纠缠特性（entanglement content），制备这些态具有挑战性。

Method: 通过将疤痕动力学与向疤痕子空间（scarred subspace）内预定义简单非纠缠乘积态（unentangled product states）的随机重置（stochastic resetting）交错进行，研究推导了保真度（fidelity）和局域可观测量（local observables）时间演化的解析结果。

Result: 重置阻尼了疤痕振荡（scarred oscillations），并在稳态（stationary state）中产生了空间非对角长程序（spatial off-diagonal long-range order）。该稳态的混合度（mixedness）随系统尺寸对数标度（logarithmically），且在稀疏重置极限（sparse-resetting limit）下，其局部等价于由重置态确定的单个纯疤痕本征态（pure scarred eigenstate）。

Conclusion: 该协议为通过重置实验制备相关纠缠态（correlated and entangled states）的局部性质提供了一条可能途径，证明了随机重置能够有效访问疤痕态的局部特性。

Abstract: Towers of quantum many-body scars are sets of highly-excited eigenstates of nonintegrable Hamiltonians whose dynamics shows athermal behavior and persistent oscillations in time. The preparation of such states is, however, challenging due to their entanglement content. In this work, we show that local properties of such states can be prepared by interspersing the scarred dynamics with stochastic resets to much simpler unentangled product states. Stochastic resetting amounts to reinitializing the many-body wavefunction of the system at random times to a predefined state, which we choose to be in the scarred subspace. We derive several analytical results for the ensuing dynamics, e.g., for the time evolution of the fidelity and of local observables. Resetting damps the scarred oscillations and generates spatial off-diagonal long-range order in the ensuing stationary state. The latter shows mixedness that scales logarithmically as a function of the system size, which follows from the structure of the scarred eigenstates. We prove that such stationary states are locally equivalent, in the sparse-resetting limit, to a single pure scarred eigenstate, which is determined by the reset state. This protocol thereby might represent a route to the experimental preparation of the local properties of correlated and entangled states through resetting.

</details>

# physics.data-an [[Back]](#toc)

### [6] [Classifying hadronic objects in ATLAS with ML/AI algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12306)
*Leonardo Toffolin*

Main category: physics.data-an

TL;DR: 该论文总结了ATLAS实验中基于组成粒子（constituent-based）的喷注标记（jet tagging）架构的最新进展，包括图神经网络和基于Transformer的方法，以及它们在模拟和真实数据中的性能表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强子末态的识别对ATLAS实验的物理研究计划至关重要，需要区分夸克和胶子引发的喷注，并识别W玻色子和顶夸克等重粒子的强子衰变。

Method: 采用先进的人工智能算法，特别是基于组成粒子的标记架构，包括图神经网络（GNNs）和基于Transformer的方法，对喷注进行分类。

Result: 总结了这些架构在模拟和真实数据中的性能表现，并探讨了未来发展方向，包括数据驱动的优化和模型无关的标记策略。

Conclusion: 论文概述了ATLAS实验中喷注标记技术的最新进展，强调了基于组成粒子的AI方法在粒子物理分析中的重要性，并指出了未来向数据驱动优化和模型无关策略发展的方向。

Abstract: The identification of hadronic final states plays a crucial role in the physics programme of the ATLAS Experiment at the CERN LHC. Sophisticated artificial intelligence (AI) algorithms are employed to classify jets according to their origin, distinguishing between quark- and gluon-initiated jets, and identifying hadronically decaying heavy objects such as W bosons and top quarks. This contribution summarises recent developments in constituent-based tagging architectures, including graph neural networks (GNNs) and transformer-based approaches, their performance in simulated and real data, and future perspectives towards data-driven optimisation and model-independent tagging strategies.

</details>


### [7] [Recent advances and trends in pattern recognition and data analysis for RICH detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13000)
*Luka Santelj*

Main category: physics.data-an

TL;DR: 本文综述了环形成像切伦科夫（RICH）探测器重建算法的当前发展状况，涵盖传统方法和机器学习应用，并讨论了全球粒子识别策略和生成式机器学习等新兴趋势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 环形成像切伦科夫（Ring Imaging Cherenkov, RICH）探测器是粒子、核物理和天体粒子物理实验中粒子识别系统的关键组件。其最终性能不仅取决于探测器设计和硬件实现，更关键地依赖于用于重建切伦科夫环图像和执行粒子识别的模式识别与数据分析算法的质量。

Method: 本文采用综述方法，回顾了RICH重建算法的当前状态，包括基于似然度（likelihood-based）的方法和霍夫变换（Hough-transform）技术等传统重建方法，以及现代机器学习工具的应用。

Result: 综述展示了近年来在传统重建方法和机器学习应用方面取得的显著进展，突出了运行实验中具有代表性的用例，并分析了当前算法发展的现状。

Conclusion: 本文讨论了包括全球粒子识别策略（global particle identification strategies）和用于快速模拟与重建的生成式机器学习方法（generative machine learning approaches）在内的新兴趋势，为RICH探测器数据处理的未来发展提供了方向。

Abstract: Ring Imaging Cherenkov (RICH) detectors are a key component of particle identification systems in many particle, nuclear and astroparticle physics experiments. Their ultimate performance depends not only on detector design and hardware implementation, but also crucially on the quality of pattern recognition and data analysis algorithms used to reconstruct Cherenkov ring images and to perform particle identification. In recent years, significant advances have been made both in traditional reconstruction approaches, such as likelihood-based methods and Hough-transform techniques, and in the application of modern machine learning tools. This contribution reviews the current state of RICH reconstruction algorithms, highlights representative use cases from operating experiments, and discusses emerging trends including global particle identification strategies and generative machine learning approaches for fast simulation and reconstruction.

</details>


<div id='hep-ph'></div>

# hep-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [8] [All-electron dark matter-electron scattering with random-phase approximation dielectric screening and local field effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12326)
*Cyrus Dreyer,Rouven Essig,Marivi Fernandez-Serra,Megan Hott,Aman Singal*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个全电子框架，用于计算暗物质-电子散射率，该框架在随机相位近似（RPA）级别包含了介电屏蔽效应，特别强调了局部场效应（local field effects）的重要性。以晶体硅为基准，研究表明局部场效应在大动量转移（跨越多个布里渊区）和低动量（近等离激元共振）区域均起关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准确预测固体中暗物质-电子散射需要全电子处理，并超越简单近似来忠实地描述介电屏蔽效应。特别是由电子响应的微观不均匀性引起的局部场效应（local field effects），可以在相关的动量和能量尺度上显著改变散射率。

Method: 研究提出了一个全电子框架（all-electron framework），用于计算暗物质-电子散射率。该框架在随机相位近似（random-phase approximation, RPA）级别纳入了介电屏蔽，并包含了局部场效应。研究以晶体硅（crystalline silicon）为基准材料，并进一步为Ge、GaAs、SiC和金刚石（diamond）提供了包含局部场效应的RPA介电函数。

Result: 研究表明，局部场效应在大动量转移（跨越多个布里渊区，multiple Brillouin zones）和低动量（近等离激元共振，plasmon resonance）区域均扮演重要角色。研究计算了电子反冲谱（electron recoil spectra）和对非相对论性晕暗物质（non-relativistic halo dark matter）以及加速暗物质（boosted dark matter）的预期灵敏度，这些分别对高动量和低动量区域的局部场效应影响敏感。

Conclusion: 该研究开发了一个包含局部场效应的全电子框架，用于精确计算固体中的暗物质-电子散射率。这些进展已实现在开源代码QCDark2中，并为多种靶材料（Ge、GaAs、SiC、金刚石）提供了包含局部场效应的RPA介电函数，实现了跨靶材料的系统性比较。

Abstract: Accurate predictions for dark matter-electron scattering in solids require an all-electron treatment together with a faithful description of dielectric screening beyond simple approximations. In particular, local field effects, arising from microscopic inhomogeneities of the electronic response, can significantly modify scattering rates across relevant momentum and energy scales. We present an all-electron framework for computing dark matter-electron scattering rates that incorporates dielectric screening at the random-phase approximation (RPA) level, including local field effects. Using crystalline silicon as a benchmark, we show that local field effects play an important role both at large momentum transfers, spanning multiple Brillouin zones, and at low momentum near the plasmon resonance. We compute electron recoil spectra and projected sensitivities for non-relativistic halo dark matter and for boosted dark matter or other dark-sector particles, which are sensitive to the impact of local field effects in these high and low momentum regimes, respectively. We further present RPA dielectric functions including local field effects for Ge, GaAs, SiC, and diamond, enabling a systematic comparison across target materials. These developments are implemented in the open source code QCDark2.

</details>


### [9] [Testing the unitarity of the light neutrino mixing matrix](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12385)
*E. Gabrielli,A. Lind,L. Marzola,K. Müürsepp,E. Nardi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在粒子对撞机实验中检验中微子混合矩阵（Pontecorvo-Maki-Nakagawa-Sakata matrix）幺正性的新方法，该方法利用幺正性破坏导致的截面异常能量增长效应，并基于现有和未来对撞机数据给出了模型无关的约束和灵敏度预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在开发一种在粒子对撞机实验中直接检验中微子混合矩阵（PMNS matrix）幺正性的新方法。标准模型扩展中，轻中微子与重态混合可能导致PMNS矩阵的幺正性破坏，而现有实验对此的探测能力有限。

Method: 该方法利用幺正性破坏条件下，t-道中微子交换与s-道规范玻色子贡献的不完全抵消效应，导致散射截面随能量异常增长。通过分析对撞机过程在低于新物理能标时的截面行为，可以提取与模型无关的幺正性破坏约束。

Result: 基于LEP-II数据推导出了对味对角幺正性破坏效应的模型无关约束。进一步展示了未来轻子对撞机和强子对撞机应用此方法的灵敏度预测，证明它们能够有效探测中微子混合矩阵的幺正性。

Conclusion: 所提出的方法为在对撞机实验中检验中微子混合矩阵幺正性提供了有效途径，特别是在过程特征能量低于新物理自由度质量阈值的条件下，该方法能够灵敏地探测标准模型扩展中的幺正性破坏效应。

Abstract: We propose a novel test of the unitarity of the Pontecorvo-Maki-Nakagawa-Sakata (PMNS) mixing matrix at collider experiments. Our approach exploits the incomplete cancellation between $t$-channel neutrino exchange and $s$-channel gauge-boson contributions that arises in the presence of violation of the flavor-diagonal PMNS unitarity conditions, leading to an anomalous growth of the cross section with energy. Such effects are generic in extensions of the Standard Model in which light neutrinos mix with heavier states, and can manifest at colliders as long as the characteristic energy of the process remains below the mass threshold of the new degrees of freedom. After briefly reviewing these scenarios, we employ our strategy to derive model-independent bounds on flavor diagonal unitarity-violating effects using LEP-II data. We then present sensitivity projections for future lepton and hadron colliders, demonstrating that they are well suited to probe the unitarity of the neutrino mixing matrix with this method.

</details>


### [10] [Quantum entanglement and Bell nonlocality in top-quark pair production at a photon linear collider](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12830)
*Seong Youl Choi,Dong Woo Kang,Jae Sik Lee,Chan Beom Park*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了光子直线对撞机（photon linear collider）中顶夸克对（top-quark pair）产生的量子纠缠可观测性，特别关注了碰撞光子偏振（colliding-photon polarization）对纠缠探测的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索光子直线对撞机作为研究量子纠缠的理想平台，该平台通过背散射（backscattered）激光光子产生高能碰撞光子，且光子偏振可通过初始电子束、正电子束和激光光子偏振完全控制。

Method: 方法包括从螺旋度振幅（helicity amplitudes）构建顶夸克对（$t\bar{t}$）双量子比特系统（two-qubit system）的自旋密度矩阵（spin density matrix），以此分析碰撞光子偏振对量子纠缠可观测性的影响。

Result: 研究结果表明，光子直线对撞机是探测量子纠缠和贝尔非定域性（Bell nonlocality）的理想装置，能够在顶夸克对产生过程的广泛相空间（phase space）中进行有效探测。

Conclusion: 结论强调光子直线对撞机通过完全可控的碰撞光子偏振，为研究顶夸克对系统中的量子纠缠和贝尔非定域性提供了优越的实验环境。

Abstract: A photon linear collider, the two-photon collision mode of an $e^+e^-$ linear collider, uses high-energy laser photons backscattered off the incoming electrons and positrons. The colliding-photon polarization is fully controllable through the polarizations of the initial electron and positron beams and laser photons. We investigate the impact of colliding-photon polarization on the observability of quantum entanglement in top-quark pair production at a photon linear collider. Constructing the spin density matrix of the $t\bar{t}$ two-qubit system from the helicity amplitudes, we demonstrate that a photon linear collider is an ideal machine to probe quantum entanglement and Bell nonlocality across the broad phase space of the process.

</details>


### [11] [The Migdal effect in Semiconductors for the Effective Field Theory of Dark Matter Direct Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13052)
*Kim V. Berghaus,Rouven Essig,Megan H. McDuffie*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究将半导体中的米格达尔效应（Migdal effect）与非相对论有效场论（non-relativistic effective field theory）框架结合，计算了所有十种六维算符下的效应，并利用EDELWEISS实验数据推导了新的实验限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在将半导体中的米格达尔效应（即初级核散射事件引发的瞬时电离）与描述暗物质-核相互作用的非相对论有效场论框架系统结合，以全面分析暗物质探测中的这一重要过程。

Method: 采用有效场论方法，将晶体的复杂振动和电子自由度编码为可测量的结构因子，同时使用非相对论有效场论算符系统描述暗物质-核相互作用，并将这两个框架结合进行计算。

Result: 从有效哈密顿量发现，暗物质-核散射与电离和振动激发信号可因子化分离，类似于自由原子情况；利用锗探测器EDELWEISS数据推导了各算符的新实验界限，并与其他直接探测限制进行比较。

Conclusion: 研究发现可访问参数空间受到简单紫外完备理论中重媒介子界限的限制而不利，这些紫外完备理论会产生相应的有效算符。

Abstract: The Migdal effect in semiconductors, prompt ionization from a primary nuclear scattering event, can be described across all kinematic regimes using an effective field theory that encodes the complex vibrational and electronic degrees of freedom of the crystal in measurable structure factors. Simultaneously, general dark matter-nucleus interactions can be systematically described using non-relativistic effective field theory operators. We combine these two effective field theory frameworks to calculate the Migdal effect in semiconductors for all ten dimension-six non-relativistic operators. From the effective Hamiltonian, we find that DM-nucleus scattering factorizes from the ionization and vibrational excitation signal as it does in the free-atom case. Using data from EDELWEISS that was taken with a germanium detector, we derive new experimental bounds on each operator and compare these limits to other direct-detection constraints in the literature. We find the accessible parameter space to be disfavored by bounds on heavy mediators contained in simple UV completions that generate the effective operators.

### [12] [Axion search with telescope for radio astronomy (ASTRA): forecast for observations between 0.5 and 4~GHz](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13194)
*Utkarsh Bhura,David J. E. Marsh,Bradley R. Johnson,Karl van Bibber,Mallory Helfenbein,Bradley J. Kavanagh,Matthew Nelson,Ciaran A. J. O'Hare,Giovanni Pierobon,Gray Rybka,Luca Visinelli*

Main category: hep-ph

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轴子暗物质（axion dark matter）理论预测其在脉冲星（neutron star）磁层中会转化为射电波，这为探测轴子提供了一种新途径。研究旨在评估使用小型射电望远镜探测这种信号的可行性，以探索轴子-光子耦合（axion-photon coupling）的新参数空间。

Method: 研究计划在Fan Mountain Observatory安装5米射电望远镜，在UHF、L和S波段（0.5-4 GHz）进行观测。方法包括建立详细的脉冲星种群模型（neutron star population model）、噪声模型（noise model）和观测策略（observing strategy），重点关注银河系中心（Galactic centre）的脉冲星。

Result: 研究表明，该望远镜在三年观测期内能够探索轴子质量（axion mass）范围2-17 μeV的新参数空间，对轴子-光子耦合（axion-photon coupling）的灵敏度达到g_{aγγ} ≳ 2×10⁻¹² GeV⁻¹，比现有脉冲星观测提高一个数量级以上。如果银河系中心存在暗物质尖峰（DM spike），该搜索对QCD轴子模型（QCD axion model）波段具有敏感性。

Conclusion: 该宽带搜索方法是对同频率范围内其他技术的补充，UHF和L波段观测构成了"轴子射电天文望远镜搜索"（Axion Search with Telescope for Radio Astronomy, ASTRA）项目的探路阶段。未来针对更高质量轴子的发现潜力需要硬件开发以覆盖S、C、X和Ku波段（2-18 GHz）。

Abstract: Axion dark matter (DM) is predicted to convert into radio waves in neutron star magnetospheres. We assess the detectability of this signal using a 5 m radio telescope to be installed at the Fan Mountain Observatory, operating in the UHF, L- and S-bands from 0.5 to 4~GHz. We demonstrate that such a telescope can search new parameter space for axion-like particles over a broad range from $2\,μ\text{eV}<m_a<17\,μ\text{eV}$ for axion-photon couplings $g_{aγγ} \gtrsim 2\times 10^{-12}\text{ GeV}^{-1}$ with a three year observing period assuming the standard halo model -- improving neutron star observations by more than an order of magnitude. The search is broadband and is thus complementary to other techniques in the same frequency range. We describe in detail our neutron star population model, noise model, and proposed observing strategy. Most constraining power comes from neutron stars at the Galactic centre, where the smooth DM halo is densest. If a DM spike exists at the Galactic centre, the search is sensitive in the QCD axion model band. UHF and L-band observations (0.5 to 2~GHz) represent the pathfinder phase of a wider program we call ``Axion Search with Telescope for Radio Astronomy'' (ASTRA). Future higher mass searches aimed at discovery potential for the post-inflation axion require further hardware development to cover S, C, X and Ku bands (2 to 18~GHz).

### [13] [Not So Minimal Warm Inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12856)
*Mar Bastero-Gil,Pedro García Osorio,António Torres Manso*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了轴子类暴胀子与非阿贝尔规范玻色子耦合的暖暴胀模型，重点关注通过sphaleron加热机制维持有限温度的可行性，并分析了观测约束和模型构建限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在重新评估轴子类暴胀子（axion-like inflaton）与非阿贝尔规范玻色子（non-Abelian gauge bosons）耦合的暖暴胀（warm inflation）模型的可行性。即使从冷初始条件开始，这些系统中的sphaleron加热可能产生足够的热摩擦来维持整个暴胀时期的有限温度。

Method: 研究采用最小暖暴胀（Minimal Warm Inflation）框架，坚持移位对称势（shift-symmetric potentials）。重点分析了摩擦率和暴胀子势中出现的衰变常数（decay constants）之间的层次结构，并检验了观测约束和模型构建限制。

Result: 研究发现流行的钟表机制（clockwork mechanism）无法产生所需的层次结构。然而，分波幺正性界限（partial-wave unitarity bounds）允许有效的描述保持与观测一致。

Conclusion: 轴子类暴胀子与非阿贝尔规范玻色子耦合的暖暴胀模型在特定条件下具有可行性，但需要超越钟表机制的机制来实现所需的参数层次，同时满足幺正性约束。

Abstract: An axion-like inflaton coupled to non-Abelian gauge bosons provides a compelling microphysical framework for warm inflation. Starting even from cold initial conditions, in these systems, sphaleron heating may generate thermal friction sufficient to sustain finite temperatures throughout the inflationary epoch. Insisting on shift-symmetric potentials, in this work we revisit the viability of these scenarios under the designation of Minimal Warm Inflation. We examine both observational constraints and model-building limitations on models with a hierarchy between the decay constants appearing in the friction rate and in the inflaton potential. We conclude that the popular clockwork mechanism cannot generate the required hierarchy; however, partial-wave unitarity bounds admit effective descriptions that remain consistent with observations.

### [14] [Factorization Beyond Coherence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12383)
*Thomas Becher,Patrick Hager,Matthias Neubert,Dominik Schwienbacher*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有因子化公式未能充分考虑Glauber胶子诱导的相干性破坏效应，这导致对强子对撞机中N-jettiness等全局LHC可观测量的理论描述存在缺陷。

Method: 推导了包含Glauber胶子和新动量模式的新因子化定理，计算了相干性破坏对数（CVLs）重求和所需的异常维度（anomalous dimensions），并建立了系统性处理相干性破坏的通用框架。

Result: 相干性破坏对数（CVLs）在四环（N≥1）或五环（N=0）阶开始出现，计算了重求和所需的异常维度，并建立了相干性破坏的系统性处理框架。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，大多数现有的LHC全局可观测量的因子化公式必须进行修正，以正确纳入相干性破坏效应。

Abstract: We derive a novel factorization theorem for $N$-jettiness at hadron colliders, which incorporates coherence-violating effects induced by Glauber gluons and several new momentum modes. Their interplay generates coherence-violating logarithms (CVLs) starting at four-loop ($N\ge1$) or five-loop order ($N=0$). We calculate the anomalous dimensions required for the resummation of CVLs and establish a general framework for the systematic treatment of coherence violation. Our findings imply that most existing factorization formulas for global LHC observables must be revised.

### [15] [Probing the chiral and $U(1)$ axial symmetry restoration via meson susceptibilities in holographic QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12911)
*Hiwa A. Ahmed,Danning Li,Mamiya Kawaguchi,Mei Huang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本研究采用软壁全息QCD模型，通过两个参数集（Case I和Case II）研究有限温度下手征对称性和U(1)轴矢量对称性的恢复模式。模型成功再现了平滑的手征交叉转变，但发现U(1)轴矢量对称性恢复温度显著高于手征对称性恢复温度，揭示了模型在描述U(1)轴矢量反常方面的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索有限温度下手征对称性和U(1)轴矢量对称性的恢复模式。当前研究使用软壁全息QCD模型来理解这些对称性在高温下的恢复行为，特别是它们之间的恢复温度差异。

Method: 研究方法采用软壁全息QCD模型，使用两个不同的参数集（Case I和Case II）。两个参数集都经过校准，以再现伪临界温度T_pc ∼ 155 MeV和物理π介子质量。通过分析轻夸克和奇异夸克凝聚的温度依赖性，以及手征伙伴介子（π-σ和η-a_0）的屏蔽质量来研究对称性恢复。

Result: 研究结果显示平滑的手征交叉转变，Case I和Case II的伪临界温度分别为T_pc=0.157 GeV和T_pc=0.154 GeV。手征伙伴介子的屏蔽质量在T_pc附近简并，表明手征对称性恢复。然而，U(1)轴矢量对称性恢复指标χ_π-χ_a_0在T ∼ 0.190 GeV时消失，表明其恢复温度高于手征对称性恢复温度。拓扑敏感性χ_top^{1/4}在T_pc附近急剧下降。

Conclusion: 结论表明，虽然模型在定性上捕捉到了手征转变的已知特征，但与格点QCD相比，模型在U(1)轴矢量反常的定性描述方面存在局限性。研究揭示了手征对称性和U(1)轴矢量对称性在软壁全息框架内具有不同的恢复尺度。

Abstract: We investigate the restoration patterns of chiral and $U(1)$ axial symmetries at finite temperature using a soft-wall holographic QCD model. The study employs two distinct parameter sets (Case I and Case II), both calibrated to reproduce a pseudocritical temperature $T_{\rm pc} \sim 155$ MeV and the physical pion mass. The temperature dependence of the light and strange quark condensates confirms a smooth chiral crossover transition, with pseudocritical temperatures of $T_{\rm pc}=0.157$ GeV and $T_{\rm pc}=0.154$ GeV for Cases I and II, respectively. The screening masses of chiral partner mesons ($π$-$σ$ and $η$-$a_0$) become degenerate near $T_{\rm pc}$, providing a clear signature of chiral symmetry restoration. Analysis of the corresponding meson susceptibilities further supports this conclusion. However, the indicator for $U(1)$ axial symmetry restoration, $χ_π- χ_{a_0}$, vanishes at a temperature $T \sim 0.190 $ GeV, which indicates a distinct restoration scale with chiral symmetry restoration scale within the present holographic framework. The temperature-dependent topological susceptibility $χ_{\rm top}^{1/4}$ is also computed, showing a sharp drop near $T_{\rm pc}$ and a subsequent slight decrease. While the model qualitatively captures established features of the chiral transition, the results highlight a limitation in the qualitative description of the $U(1)$ axial anomaly compared to LQCD in our work.

### [16] [Radiative return meets GVMD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13171)
*Pau Petit Rosàs,Olga Shekhovtsova,William J. Torres Bobadilla*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过将π介子形状因子（pion form factor）纳入费曼规则，改进了辐射回返过程e⁺e⁻→π⁺π⁻γ中π介子-光子相互作用的次领头阶描述，并在Phokhara事件生成器中实现，发现对撞机能量接近π介子形状因子峰值时角微分截面分布存在百分比级别效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在改进辐射回返过程e⁺e⁻→π⁺π⁻γ中π介子-光子相互作用的描述，特别是在次领头阶（next-to-leading order）精度下，通过更准确地纳入π介子形状因子来提升理论预测能力。

Method: 方法包括将π介子形状因子纳入费曼规则，进行新振幅的一般性计算，并开发易于与任何蒙特卡洛生成器（Monte Carlo generator）接口的实现，最终将该框架整合到Phokhara事件生成器中。

Result: 研究发现，在对撞机质心能量接近π介子形状因子峰值时，角微分截面分布出现百分比级别效应；而总截面和电荷偶变量分布仅显示千分比级别效应或无可见差异。通过与KLOE测量的前向-后向不对称性比较评估了改进的预测能力。

Conclusion: 该研究成功实现了π介子形状因子在辐射回返过程中的次领头阶改进，为精确测量提供了重要理论工具，特别是在角分布分析中显示出显著影响，而总截面测量受影响较小。

Abstract: We improve the description of pion-photon interactions in the radiative return process $e^+e^-\to π^+π^-γ$ at the next-to-leading order by including the pion form factor in the Feynman rules. We present a general calculation of the new amplitudes, and provide an implementation easy to interface with any Monte Carlo generator. We incorporate this framework into the event generator $\texttt{Phokhara}$ and study several experimental configurations. Overall, we find percent-level effects appearing in angular differential cross section distributions at colliders whose centre-of-mass energies lie near the peak of the pion form factor. By contrast, total cross sections and distributions in charge-even variables show effects only at the permille level, or no visible differences at all. Finally, we compare the new predictions with KLOE measurements of the forward-backward asymmetry in order to assess the predictive power of the modifications.

# math.PR [[Back]](#toc)

### [17] [Clustering without geometry in sparse networks with independent edges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13159)
*Alessio Catanzaro,Remco van der Hofstad,Diego Garlaschelli*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文证明了一种稀疏随机图模型能够在保持边独立性的前提下产生有限聚类，无需几何约束或高阶依赖。该模型基于节点聚合不变性，通过无限均值节点适应度实现幂律度分布，并展示了网络性质的非自平均现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实世界网络普遍同时表现出稀疏性和聚类性（clustering），但传统稀疏随机图模型需要依赖几何距离或高阶依赖才能产生聚类。这引发了关于聚类是否意味着潜在几何结构的争论，需要探索产生聚类的替代机制。

Method: 研究采用了一种在节点聚合（node aggregation）下保持不变的稀疏随机图模型，该模型具有独立的边。通过数学证明和数值模拟相结合的方法，分析了该模型产生聚类的内在机制。

Result: 该模型能够在保持边独立性的前提下产生有限聚类，无需几何约束或高阶依赖。其核心机制是无限均值节点适应度（infinite-mean node fitness），这同时导致了幂律度分布（power-law degree distribution）。研究还首次严格表征了网络性质的非自平均（breakdown of self-averaging）现象。

Conclusion: 节点聚合不变性（node aggregation invariance）是产生现实网络性质（如聚类和幂律度分布）的一种基本途径，可作为几何约束或高阶依赖的替代机制。这一发现为理解现实世界网络结构提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: The coexistence of sparsity and clustering (non-vanishing average fraction of triangles per node) is one of the few structural features that, irrespective of finer details, are ubiquitously observed across large real-world networks. This fact calls for generic models producing sparse clustered graphs. Earlier results suggested that sparse random graphs with independent edges fail to reproduce clustering, unless edge probabilities are assumed to depend on underlying metric distances that, thanks to the triangle inequality, naturally favour triadic closure. This observation has opened a debate on whether clustering implies (latent) geometry in real-world networks. Alternatively, recent models of higher-order networks can replicate clustering by abandoning edge independence. In this paper, we mathematically prove, and numerically confirm, that a sparse random graph with independent edges, recently identified in the context of network renormalization as an invariant model under node aggregation, produces finite clustering without any geometric or higher-order constraint. The underlying mechanism is an infinite-mean node fitness, which also implies a power-law degree distribution. Further, as a novel phenomenon that we characterize rigorously, we observe the breakdown of self-averaging of various network properties. Therefore, as an alternative to geometry or higher-order dependencies, node aggregation invariance emerges as a basic route to realistic network properties.

</details>


### [18] [Vector spin glasses with Mattis interaction I: the convex case](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12033)
*Hong-Bin Chen,Victor Issa*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文作为两篇系列论文的第一部分，系统研究了包含自旋玻璃部分和一般Mattis相互作用部分的矢量自旋玻璃模型。在自旋玻璃部分满足通常凸性假设的条件下，通过Parisi型公式确定了极限自由能，并证明了平均磁化强度的大偏差原理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在系统研究一类矢量自旋玻璃模型，其能量函数包含自旋玻璃部分和一般Mattis相互作用部分。这是两篇系列论文的第一部分，专注于自旋玻璃部分满足通常凸性假设的模型。

Method: 证明方法显著简化且简短，将Mattis相互作用视为模型参数进行处理。通过Parisi型公式（Parisi-type formula）确定极限自由能，并建立平均磁化强度的大偏差原理（large deviation principle）。

Result: 成功识别了极限自由能，并通过Parisi型公式给出了其表达式。同时证明了平均磁化强度的大偏差原理，为这类矢量自旋玻璃模型提供了严格的数学基础。

Conclusion: 本文为满足凸性假设的矢量自旋玻璃模型建立了完整的理论框架。在配套论文中，将在高温区域（high-temperature regime）对不满足凸性假设的模型建立类似结果。

Abstract: This paper constitutes the first part of a two-paper series devoted to the systematic study of vector spin glass models whose energy function involves a spin glass part and a general Mattis interaction part.
  In this paper, we focus on models whose spin glass part satisfies the usual convexity assumption. We identify the limit free energy via a Parisi-type formula and prove a large deviation principle for the mean magnetization. The proof is remarkably simple and short compared to previous approaches; it relies on treating the Mattis interaction as a parameter of the model.
  In the companion paper, we establish similar results in the high-temperature regime for models whose spin glass part is not assumed to satisfy the usual convexity assumption.

### [19] [Vector spin glasses with Mattis interaction II: non-convex high-temperature models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12034)
*Hong-Bin Chen,Victor Issa*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文证明了在高温条件下，非凸自旋玻璃（spin glass）模型的极限自由能（free energy）可由哈密顿-雅可比型偏微分方程的唯一解描述，并给出了基于临界点的显式表示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究自旋玻璃部分不满足通常凸性假设的矢量自旋玻璃模型。在这种情况下，帕里西公式（Parisi formula）失效，且缺乏完全确定极限自由能的方法。

Method: 作者证明了高温条件下，极限自由能可由哈密顿-雅可比型偏微分方程的唯一解描述这一猜想，并提供了基于临界点的显式自由能表示。同时利用自由能与大偏差原理（large deviation principle）的对偶性进行推导。

Result: 在高温条件下，成功验证了极限自由能可由哈密顿-雅可比型偏微分方程唯一解描述的猜想，并获得了自由能的显式表示。由此推导出平均磁化强度的大偏差原理，以及高温下带有附加马蒂斯相互作用（Mattis interaction）的自旋玻璃模型的自由能表示。

Conclusion: 本文在高温条件下解决了非凸自旋玻璃模型的自由能计算问题，为相关模型提供了理论框架。在系列论文的上一篇中，作者对所有温度下满足凸性假设的模型建立了类似结果。

Abstract: This paper constitutes the second part of a two-paper series devoted to the systematic study of vector spin glass models whose energy function involves a spin glass part and a general Mattis interaction part.
  In this paper, we focus on models whose spin glass part does not satisfy the usual convexity assumption. In this case, the Parisi formula breaks down, and there are no known methods to fully identify the limit free energy. It was suggested in [arXiv:1906.08471] that the limit free energy may be described using the unique solution of a partial differential equation of Hamilton--Jacobi type. In the present paper, we prove the validity of this conjecture in the high-temperature regime and provide an explicit representation for the free energy in terms of critical points.
  Using the duality between the free energy and large deviation principles, one can then easily deduce from the previous result a large deviation principle for the mean magnetization as well as a representation for the free energy of spin glass models with additional Mattis interaction at high temperature.
  In the companion paper, we establish similar results at all temperatures for models whose spin glass part is assumed to satisfy the usual convexity assumption.

</details>

### [20] [Nonequilibrium assembly of Lennard-Jones particles on a sphere](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12360)
*Ivan Yu. Golushko,Olga V. Konevtsova,Daria S. Roshal,Sergei B. Rochal*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过非平衡顺序组装机制模拟了n<72个相同粒子形成球形壳体的过程，揭示了除已知二十面体病毒蛋白壳外，还产生具有正方形-三角形表面序的多种壳体结构，这些结构对应天然或合成蛋白复合物。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究已知球形堆积（spherical packings）背后的物理机制和共同几何原理对于合成纳米容器（synthetic nanocontainers）的理性设计至关重要。需要理解小球形壳体在非平衡条件下的组装过程。

Method: 采用非平衡顺序组装（nonequilibrium and sequential assembly）机制模拟：每一步将新粒子附着在最有利的能量位置，随后系统弛豫。粒子具有自身曲率并通过Lennard-Jones势相互作用，同时使用双极小Lennard-Jones-Gauss势模拟各向异性相互作用。

Result: 该机制不仅生成已知的最小二十面体病毒蛋白壳（icosahedral viral protein shells），还产生广泛具有正方形-三角形表面序（square-triangular surface order）的壳体。这些壳体大多对应具有八面体或四面体对称性的天然或合成蛋白复合物模型。

Conclusion: 研究比较了非平衡组装结构与平衡组装（对应全局能量极小）的结构差异，并考虑了温度依赖的随机组装过程，为理解球形壳体的形成机制提供了新视角。

Abstract: Studying physical mechanisms and common geometric principles underlying known spherical packings is crucial for rational design of synthetic nanocontainers. Here we model the growth of small spherical shells containing n<72 identical particles that have their own curvature and interact with each other via the Lennard-Jones potential. The shell assembly is assumed to be nonequilibrium and sequential: at each step, a new particle is attached to the most energetically favorable position, after which the system relaxes. Along with well-known structures of the smallest icosahedral viral protein shells, the proposed mechanism generates a wide range of shells exhibiting square-triangular surface order. Most of such shells are the models of synthetic or natural protein complexes that have octahedral or tetrahedral symmetries and perform various functions. We compare the obtained structures with those resulting from the equilibrium assembly and corresponding to global energy minima. Also, we consider the temperature-dependent stochastic assembly and use the double-minimum Lennard-Jones-Gauss potential to mimic anisotropic particle interactions.

### [21] [Recent Computational Advances in Dense Suspension Mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12410)
*Orhun Ayar,Bhargav Sriram Siddani,Ishan Srivastava,Abhinendra Singh*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文综述了稠密悬浮液（dense suspensions）多尺度模拟方法的最新进展，重点讨论了整合颗粒接触力学与悬浮液流体动力学的计算框架，旨在建立预测性多尺度模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稠密悬浮液在工业、地球物理过程和软物质非平衡系统中具有重要地位，但其在高颗粒浓度下表现出复杂的应力依赖性流变学行为，包括不连续剪切增稠（discontinuous shear thickening）和剪切堵塞（shear jamming）。这些非线性物理现象源于摩擦接触、界面化学和流体介导的流体动力学之间的相互作用，使得预测建模具有多尺度特性和计算挑战性。

Method: 本文讨论了整合干颗粒材料的接触摩擦力学与悬浮液流体动力学的最先进模拟框架。这些方法包括从颗粒解析（particle-resolved）到连续介质模型（continuum models）的不同保真度模拟，以及研究流动过程中介观尺度组织（mesoscale organization）的模型。

Result: 这些计算方法揭示了稠密悬浮液的分层结构：微观尺度约束产生介观尺度摩擦网络（mesoscale frictional networks），最终控制宏观流动。通过综合计算力学和软物质物理的发展，这些方法为理解稠密悬浮液的流变学提供了预测性见解。

Conclusion: 本文展望了稠密悬浮液多尺度建模框架的发展方向，强调需要建立能够处理真实几何形状和复杂流动环境的预测性模型。通过整合不同尺度的计算方法，可以更好地理解稠密悬浮液的流变行为及其在工业与地球物理过程中的应用。

Abstract: Dense suspensions of particles dispersed in liquids are central to industrial and geophysical processes and serve as model systems for out-of-equilibrium soft matter. At high particle concentrations, they exhibit stress-dependent rheology, including discontinuous shear thickening and shear jamming, arising from frictional contacts. Nonlinear physics arises from the interplay among direct contacts, interfacial chemistry, and fluid-mediated hydrodynamics. The relative importance of these mechanisms depends on particle properties and flow conditions, making predictive modeling inherently multi-scale and, therefore, computationally challenging. Recent advances in computational methods have transformed our ability to simulate the physics of dense suspensions across scales. In this Perspective, we discuss state-of-the-art simulation frameworks that integrate the mechanics of dry granular materials, mediated by contact friction, with suspension hydrodynamics to provide predictive models of dense suspension rheology. We highlight recent computational developments for simulating dense suspensions at varying levels of fidelity, ranging from particle-resolved to continuum models, as well as models that investigate their mesoscale organization during flow. Together, these approaches reveal a hierarchical structure in which microscale constraints give rise to mesoscale frictional networks that ultimately govern macroscopic flow. By synthesizing developments across computational mechanics and soft matter physics, this Perspective highlights emerging directions toward a predictive, multi-scale modeling framework of dense suspensions in realistic geometries and complex flow environments.

</details>


### [22] [Simulation of shear strain at arbitrary angles as a probe of packing instabilities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12457)
*Chloe W. Lindeman,Sidney R. Nagel*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一种可在周期性边界条件下以连续可变角度施加剪切应变的模拟工具，用于分析无序固体中粒子接触失稳的相互作用。研究发现失稳可在相空间中形成广泛的失稳线，并揭示了不同角度和位置失稳之间的相关性，特别是滞后子（hysterons）在失稳消失点附近的行为特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无序固体在足够大的剪切应变下会发生粒子接触失稳和重排，导致材料变形和失效。这些失稳可能在不同位置发生并相互影响，因此需要研究失稳之间的相互作用及其在相空间中的行为特征。

Method: 开发了一种在周期性边界条件下以连续可变角度θ施加剪切应变的模拟工具。通过在不同角度施加应变，研究不同角度和样品不同位置遇到的失稳之间的相关性，特别关注滞后子（hysterons）的行为。

Result: 研究发现失稳可在相空间中形成广泛的失稳线（instability lines）。观察到三种主要失稳行为：相互穿过的失稳、随角度连续变化的失稳、以及幅度平滑减小至零而消失的失稳。对于滞后子，当θ趋近于失稳消失点时，正向和反向失稳的间距缩小为零，导致大量微小滞后子的出现。

Conclusion: 该研究通过开发新的模拟工具揭示了无序固体中剪切诱导失稳的复杂相互作用模式。失稳在相空间中形成连续的结构，而滞后子的行为表明失稳消失点附近存在特殊的临界现象，这为理解无序材料的力学响应提供了新的视角。

Abstract: Disordered solids distort and fail as particle contacts become unstable and rearrange under sufficiently large shear strains. Such instabilities can occur at different locations and, because of their proximity, can interact with one another. We develop a tool for simulations with periodic boundary conditions that allows strains to be applied at a continuously variable angle, $θ$. We show that instabilities can persist over a broad angular ranges of applied shear to form instability lines in phase space. By applying strain at different $θ$, we examine the correlations between the instabilities encountered at different angles and different positions in the sample. We find instabilities that pass through one another, others that change continuously as the angle is varied, and yet others that end by smoothly decreasing their magnitudes to zero as the instability fades away. Examining hysterons, i.e., instabilities that undo themselves upon reversing the direction of shear, we find that as $θ$ is varied towards the point where the instability disappears, the separation between the forward and backward instabilities shrinks to zero so as to produce an enhanced number of very small hysterons.

### [23] [Theory of hybrid defects, with coupled orientational order parameters, on flat and curved surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12474)
*Lincoln Paik,Jonathan V. Selinger*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了具有两种二维取向序（m-atic和n-atic）的物理系统中的缺陷结构，分析了耦合强度对缺陷形态的影响，从弱耦合时的弥散壁网络到强耦合时的缺陷核合并。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多物理系统涉及两种相互耦合的取向序，如铁电向列相液晶（ferroelectric nematic liquid crystals）的极性与向列序耦合，以及倾斜六角相（tilted hexatic phases）的极性与六角序耦合。这些系统中的缺陷结构通常较为复杂，需要深入研究。

Method: 研究模拟了具有两种二维取向序（m-atic和n-atic，其中m和n为不同整数）的相，在两种几何结构中进行：具有强径向锚定（strong radial anchoring）的平面圆盘和球面，因为这些几何结构都需要缺陷的存在。

Result: 当两种序之间的耦合较弱时，缺陷通过弥散壁（diffuse walls）网络连接，系统形成稳定的畴结构。随着耦合增强，畴壁（domain walls）变得更尖锐和更短。在极强耦合下，高阶缺陷会合并到低阶缺陷中，形成拉伸的缺陷核（stretched defect cores）。

Conclusion: 研究表明，两种取向序之间的耦合强度显著影响缺陷结构的形态，从弱耦合的弥散壁网络到强耦合的缺陷核合并，揭示了复杂物理系统中缺陷演化的基本规律。

Abstract: Many physical systems involve two types of orientational order, which are coupled together. For example, ferroelectric nematic liquid crystals have coupled polar and nematic order, and tilted hexatic phases have coupled polar and hexatic order. In these systems, defect structures can be quite complex. Here, we investigate phases with two types of two-dimensional orientational order, $m$-atic and $n$-atic, where $m$ and $n$ are two distinct integers. We simulate these phases in a flat disk with strong radial anchoring, and on a spherical surface, because both of these geometries require the presence of defects. If the coupling between the two types of order is weak, then the defects are connected by a network of diffuse walls, and the system forms a stable domain structure. As the coupling increases, the domain walls become sharper and shorter. For very strong coupling, the higher-order defects merge into the lower-order defects, forming stretched defect cores.

</details>


### [24] [Polymer-Residue Accessibility Shapes Sequence Dependence of Critical Temperatures for Phase Separation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12534)
*J. Pedro de Souza,Benjamin Sorkin,Amala Akkiraju,Athanassios Z. Panagiotopoulos,Howard A. Stone*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于单体可及性（monomer accessibility）的解析微扰理论，通过残基可及性参数（RAP）定量解释生物聚合物相图对序列的依赖性，成功预测了数千种双字母聚合物溶液临界温度的变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生物聚合物（如固有无序蛋白质）在细胞生物学中发挥核心作用，其物理性质和功能由残基序列决定。目前需要理解组合复杂的序列如何影响生物聚合物相图，特别是相分离和生物凝聚体活性的调控机制。

Method: 研究提出了一种解析微扰方法（analytical perturbative approach），现象学地排除两个聚合物质心在相关孔（correlation hole）内的重叠。该理论通过残基可及性参数（residue-accessibility parameter, RAP）计算平均场相互作用强度的修正，该参数考虑了内部单体相互作用的有限可用性。

Result: 尽管方法简单，RAP能够合理解释数千种不同长度和序列的双字母聚合物溶液（two-letter polymer solutions）在广泛蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte-Carlo simulations）中发现的临界温度变化。RAP有效揭示了单体可及性对配对相互作用强度的决定性作用。

Conclusion: 残基可及性参数（RAP）可有效解析给定任何聚合物长度、单体类型集合和聚合物混合物条件下，聚合物相图对序列的依赖性。该方法为理解生物聚合物相分离的序列特异性提供了定量理论框架。

Abstract: Biological polymers, such as intrinsically disordered proteins, play a central role in cellular biology, including mediating phase separation and controlling activity of biological condensates. The physical properties and functions of biopolymers are determined by their residue sequence. Recently, significant computational and theoretical efforts have been devoted to characterizing the combinatorially complex sequence dependence of biopolymer phase diagrams. Here, we quantitatively show that monomer accessibility is central to determining the strength of pair interactions. We formulate an analytical perturbative approach, phenomenologically precluding two polymers' centers of mass from overlapping within a correlation hole. This theory yields the correction to the strength of mean-field interactions in terms of a residue-accessibility parameter (RAP), which accounts for the limited availability of inner monomers to interactions. Despite the simplicity of the approach, RAP rationalizes the variations in critical temperatures found in extensive Monte-Carlo simulations for thousands of two-letter polymer solutions of varying length and sequence. RAP may thus be effective for deciphering the polymer-sequence dependence of phase diagrams given any polymer length, set of monomer types, and polymer mixtures.

### [25] [Memory-aware acceleration of orientational dynamics in nanoparticle suspensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12689)
*Miguel Ibáñez,Raúl A. Rica-Alarcón,María L. Jiménez*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过纳米粒子电取向实验展示了Kovacs型非单调弛豫现象，揭示了多分散性导致的多尺度弛豫记忆效应，并设计了通过顺序抑制最慢弛豫模式来加速动力学的控制策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机系统在突然扰动后的弛豫过程受速度极限约束，且常伴随阻碍动力学加速的记忆效应。研究旨在探索非球形纳米粒子电取向中的Kovacs型非单调弛豫现象，并理解这种记忆效应对简单加速协议的限制。

Method: 实验上通过场致双折射光学监测取向动力学，该信号与向列序参数成正比。理论框架基于取向概率密度的Smoluchowski方程，在高频交流电场区域，取向弛豫由诱导偶极子主导。

Result: 当采用匹配两步协议时，弛豫过程呈现特征性的Kovacs肩部。观察到的记忆效应源于多分散性产生的旋转扩散系数谱，从而导致多尺度弛豫。通过顺序抑制最慢活性弛豫模式，设计的协议显著降低了弛豫时间。

Conclusion: 研究阐明了当使用单一控制参数引导多个自由度时记忆效应的产生机制，并为控制多尺度随机动力学提供了实验可行的策略。在NaMt悬浮液实验中，相比单次淬灭和匹配两步协议，实现了弛豫时间的显著减少。

Abstract: The relaxation of stochastic systems after sudden perturbations is constrained by speed limits and often reveals memory effects that hinder attempts to accelerate their dynamics. Here we demonstrate Kovacs-type nonmonotonic relaxation in the electro-orientation of non-spherical nanoparticles and show how this memory effect limits simple acceleration protocols. Experimentally, the orientational dynamics is monitored optically through field-induced birefringence, which is proportional to the nematic order parameter. When an AC electric field is first set to an extreme value until the birefringence reaches its target and is then switched to the target field (matched two-step protocol), the relaxation exhibits a characteristic Kovacs shoulder. We interpret this behavior within a theoretical framework based on the Smoluchowski equation for the orientational probability density. In the high-frequency AC regime, orientational relaxation is governed by induced dipoles, and the observed memory effect originates from polydispersity, which generates a spectrum of rotational diffusion coefficients and hence multiscale relaxation. Building on this insight, we design protocols that mitigate the detrimental effect of memory by sequentially suppressing the slowest active relaxation mode. Experiments on nanoparticle suspensions with different properties confirm these mechanisms, and we demonstrate substantial reductions in relaxation time compared with single quenches and matched two-step protocols with NaMt suspensions. More broadly, these results illustrate how memory effects emerge when many degrees of freedom are steered with a single control parameter and provide an experimentally accessible strategy for controlling multiscale stochastic dynamics.

### [26] [Cell-induced wrinkling patterns on soft substrates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12839)
*Aleksandra Ardaševa,Varun Venkatesh,Daiki Matsunaga,Shinji Deguchi,Amin Doostmohammadi*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一个基于Föppl-von Kármán方程薄板弹性框架与细胞相场模型耦合的理论框架，用于描述细胞在软基底上诱导的褶皱现象，预测了不同褶皱形态的转变及其与细胞力的定量关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 细胞在柔性基底上施加牵引力时会引起表面失稳，表现为特征性的褶皱图案。现有研究需要建立机械描述框架来理解细胞诱导褶皱的机制，并连接观察到的表面图案与潜在的细胞力。

Method: 采用基于Föppl-von Kármán方程的薄板弹性框架，耦合单细胞的相场模型（phase-field model）。模型包含由细胞活动驱动的面内收缩应力，研究其大小、空间分布和对称性如何决定褶皱的发生和图案选择。

Result: 理论预测了不同形态之间的转变，如径向、周向和各向异性褶皱排列，并提供了褶皱波长和振幅作为弹性参数与施加细胞力的函数的标度关系。与柔性凝胶上细胞驱动褶皱的实验观察结果比较，在定性图案类别和定量波长趋势方面均显示出良好一致性。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一个最小建模框架来解释褶皱实验，并将观察到的表面图案与潜在的细胞力联系起来。该框架有助于理解细胞-基底相互作用的力学机制。

Abstract: Cells exert traction forces on compliant substrates and can induce surface instabilities that appear as characteristic wrinkling patterns. Here, we develop a mechanical description of cell-induced wrinkling on soft substrates using a thin film elastic framework based on the Föppl-von Kármán equations coupled to a phase-field model of a single cell. We model in-plane contractile stresses driven by cellular activity and study how their magnitude, spatial distribution, and symmetry determine the onset of wrinkling and the resulting pattern selection. The theory predicts transitions between distinct morphologies, such as radial, circumferential, and anisotropic wrinkle arrangements, and provides scaling relations for wrinkle wavelength and amplitude as functions of elastic parameters and imposed cellular forcing. We compare these predictions with available experimental observations of cell-driven wrinkling on compliant gels and find good agreement for both qualitative pattern classes and quantitative wavelength trends. Our results offer a minimal modelling framework to interpret wrinkling assays and connect observed surface patterns to underlying cellular forces.

</details>


### [27] [Electrohydrodynamic Stresses from Hydrogen-Bond Network Dynamics in Water](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12941)
*Pramodt Srinivasula*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究结合非平衡热力学框架与晶格气体模型，建立了连接分子尺度氢键网络动力学与宏观电水动力学流动的统一连续介质理论，定量解释了实验测量的粘电系数和电致伸缩压力贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在揭示氢键网络对水环境中流动的阻力如何产生粘电应力（viscoelectric stresses）并贡献于电致伸缩压力（electrostrictive pressure），从而理解氢键动力学影响电水动力学流动的微观机制。

Method: 采用昂萨格（Onsager）非平衡热力学框架，将水电解质的晶格气体描述（lattice-gas description）与氢键分子网络的粗粒化流体动力学表示相结合，其中粘性耗散通过能量等效的布朗实体建模。

Result: 该理论框架成功连接了实验和分子动力学的分子结构信息，形成了统一的偶极泊松-能斯特-普朗克-斯托克斯（dipolar Poisson-Nernst-Planck-Stokes, dPNP-S）连续介质理论，定量再现了Jin等人（PNAS 2022）测量的粘电系数以及对电致伸缩压力的贡献。

Conclusion: 研究结果识别了氢键动力学影响电水动力学流动的微观机制，建立了从分子尺度到宏观连续介质尺度的理论桥梁，为理解水环境中电驱动流动现象提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: The resistance of hydrogen-bond networks to ambient flow in water produces viscoelectric stresses and contributes to electrostrictive pressure. Within Onsager's nonequilibrium thermodynamic framework, a lattice-gas description of aqueous electrolytes is combined with a coarse-grained hydrodynamic representation of hydrogen-bonded molecular networks, where viscous dissipation is modeled through energetically equivalent Brownian entities. This formulation connects molecular structural information from experiments and molecular dynamics to a unified dipolar Poisson-Nernst-Planck-Stokes (dPNP-S) continuum theory, quantitatively reproducing the measured viscoelectric coefficient of Jin et al. (PNAS 2022) and contributions to electrostrictive pressure. These results identify a microscopic mechanism by which hydrogen-bond dynamics influence electrohydrodynamic flow.

</details>


### [28] [Large dilatational hyperelasticity of glasses en route to cavitation failure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12964)
*Pawandeep Kaur,Noam Ottolenghi,Edan Lerner,David Richard,Eran Bouchbinder*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了玻璃材料在接近失效时的弹塑性变形行为随应力三轴度（stress triaxiality）水平不同而发生质变：高应力三轴度下呈现强超弹性响应与微塑性，而低应力三轴度下行为显著不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 材料在各种加载条件下发生弹塑性变形并最终失效，通常用应力三轴度（即静水应力与偏应力的比值）来量化。然而，玻璃材料在接近失效时的弹塑性变形行为如何随应力三轴度变化尚不清楚，需要系统研究不同应力三轴度极限下的变形机制差异。

Method: 研究通过对比分析玻璃在不同应力三轴度极限条件下的变形行为，重点关注高应力三轴度下玻璃的超弹性响应、非仿射弹性变形（nonaffine deformation）以及微空洞形成机制，并与低应力三轴度极限下的行为进行对比。

Result: 在高应力三轴度极限下，玻璃表现出强烈的超弹性响应和微小的塑性变形，且几乎不受淬火速率影响；玻璃无序性导致显著的非仿射弹性变形并伴随微空洞形成。少量微空洞在卸载后不可逆，可能作为大规模空化失效的成核位点，导致玻璃承载能力显著下降。

Conclusion: 玻璃的弹塑性变形和失效行为在高低应力三轴度极限下存在本质差异，这种差异在不同玻璃形成物中具有普适性。研究结果对于理解实际应力条件下玻璃的变形和失效机制具有重要意义。

Abstract: Materials deform elasto-plastically and fail under various loading conditions, typically quantified by the stress triaxiality, which is the ratio between the dilatational (hydrostatic) stress and the deviatoric (shear-like) one. We show that the elasto-plastic deformation of glasses approaching failure qualitatively differ for large and small stress triaxiality levels. Specifically, in the former limit, glasses reveal a strong hyperelastic (nonlinear elastic) response with minute plasticity, largely independently of the quenching rate across the glass transition. Yet, glassy disorder gives rise to significant elastic (reversible) nonaffine deformation, accompanied by the formation of micro-cavities. A small fraction of the latter is irreversible, i.e., survives unloading prior to the onset of failure, and may serve as nucleation sites for failure in the form of large-scale cavitation, upon which the glass loses a significant fraction of its load-bearing capacity. These results are contrasted with glass behavior in the limit of vanishing stress triaxiality and their universality across different glass formers is demonstrated. Finally, the implications of our findings for understanding glass deformation and failure under realistic stress conditions are discussed.

</details>


### [29] [Boundary-Mediated Phases of Self-Propelled Kuramoto Particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13001)
*Francesco Arceri,Vittoria Sposini,Enzo Orlandini,Fulvio Baldovin*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了活性粒子（active agents）在受限环境中通过集体运动产生能量传递时，微观驱动机制（自推进与速度对齐）如何选择不同的聚集模式，形成分散或紧凑的簇状态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 活性粒子可通过集体运动向环境传递能量，在受限障碍物附近形成聚集模式。研究旨在探究微观驱动机制（自推进或速度对齐）如何选择不同的聚集模式，导致分散或紧凑的簇状态。

Method: 首先在完美反射或光滑边界条件下表征两种驱动机制相互作用产生的动力学状态。随后引入边界摩擦（boundary friction），观察其对聚集模式的显著改变，并识别出先前情况下不存在的新动力学相。

Result: 研究发现边界摩擦会显著改变聚集模式，产生先前情况下不存在的新动力学相。通过将涌现的宏观结构与底层微观相互作用联系起来，该工作建立了推断主导边界介导集体行为相互作用的实用途径。

Conclusion: 该研究通过连接涌现的宏观结构与底层微观相互作用，为推断主导边界介导集体行为的相互作用提供了实用途径，其应用范围涵盖单细胞迁移到仿生机器人学（bio-inspired robotics）。

Abstract: Active agents can transfer energy to their environment through collective motion, generating accumulation patterns near confining obstacles. Here we investigate how the nature of the microscopic drive-self-propulsion or velocity alignment-selects distinct accumulation patterns, leading to either delocalized or compact clustered states. We first characterize the dynamical regimes emerging from the interplay of these two driving mechanisms under perfectly reflective or smooth boundary conditions. We then introduce boundary friction and observe a drastic change in the accumulation patterns, with new dynamical phases that are absent in the previous case. By connecting emergent macroscopic structures to their underlying microscopic interactions, this work provides a practical route to infer the dominant interaction ruling boundary-mediated collective behavior, with applications ranging from single-cell migration to bio-inspired robotics.

</details>

### [30] [Dipolar solvent contributions for transient nanoscale electroosmotic flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13021)
*Pramodt Srinivasula*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本研究将偶极溶剂物理（包括介电饱和和粘电效应）整合到Poisson-Nernst-Planck-Stokes（PNP-S）框架中，揭示了纳米尺度弱电解质电流体动力学流动中溶剂分子结构对电动现象的重要影响，电渗迁移率最大可降低50%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纳米尺度弱电解质的电流体动力学（electrohydrodynamic）流动显著受到双电层（electric double layer, EDL）内水类极性溶剂分子结构的影响。在这些尺度下，EDL演化时间尺度常与流体现象相当，而传统连续介质模型通常假设恒定的介电和粘性溶剂背景，忽略了偶极溶剂物理效应。

Method: 本研究将偶极溶剂物理（dipolar solvent physics），特别是介电饱和（dielectric saturation）和粘电效应（viscoelectric effect）共同整合到Poisson-Nernst-Planck-Stokes（PNP-S）框架中。分别采用Langevin-Bikerman溶剂介电常数分布和经验粘电系数，在一维几何中进行数值模拟。

Result: 数值模拟揭示了EDL演化过程中电流体动力学体积力密度和瞬态电渗迁移率（electroosmotic mobility）的显著改变。这些修正的幅度和时间演化在参数范围内表现出系统性偏离标准恒介电常数和恒粘度模型，电渗迁移率最大可降低50%，受一个特征无量纲参数控制。

Conclusion: 研究结果为瞬态纳米尺度电渗流动提供了一个溶剂一致的连续介质框架，并量化了分子溶剂结构对电流体动力学输运的影响，这对现代纳米流体应用具有重要意义。

Abstract: Electrohydrodynamic flows of weak electrolytes at the nanoscale are significantly influenced by the molecular structure of water-like polar solvents within the electric double layer (EDL). Moreover, unlike in microfluidics, at these length scales the time scale of evolution of EDL often becomes comparable to the consequent fluidic phenomena of interest. While continuum descriptions to model such phenomena typically assume a constant dielectric and viscous solvent background, this study incorporates dipolar solvent physics, specifically both dielectric saturation and the viscoelectric effect together, into a Poisson-Nernst-Planck-Stokes (PNP-S) framework, using the Langevin-Bikerman solvent permittivity distribution and empirical viscoelectric coefficients, respectively. Numerical simulations in a one-dimensional geometry reveal substantial modifications to the electrohydrodynamic body force density and transient electroosmotic mobility during EDL evolution. The magnitude and temporal evolution of these corrections are characterized across parametric regimes, revealing systematic departures from standard constant-permittivity and constant-viscosity models, with electroosmotic mobility reductions of up to 50% governed by a characteristic dimensionless parameter. The results provide a solvent-consistent continuum framework for transient nanoscale electroosmotic flows and quantify the impact of molecular solvent structure on electrohydrodynamic transport relevant to modern nanofluidic applications.

</details>

### [31] [Forward Self-Similar Solutions to the 2D Hypodissipative Navier-Stokes Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12497)
*Thomas Y. Hou,Peicong Song*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了二维亚耗散Navier-Stokes方程在分数阶扩散下的前向自相似解，证明了对于任意大的齐次初值存在弱解，并在特定参数范围内证明了弱解的光滑性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究二维亚耗散（hypodissipative）Navier-Stokes方程在分数阶扩散（fractional diffusion）$(-Δ)^α$下的前向自相似解（forward self-similar solutions），其中参数范围$\frac{1}{2}<α<1$。关注这类方程解的存在性与正则性。

Method: 首先证明对于任意大的$(1-2α)$-齐次（homogeneous）且局部Lipschitz的初值，存在至少一个弱解（weak solution），其轮廓与分数阶热方程的自相似轮廓相差一个$H^α(\mathbb{R}^2)$空间元素。当$α\in(\frac{2}{3},1)$时，进一步证明任何此类弱解实际上是光滑的（smooth），从而成为强解（strong solution）。

Result: 对于$\frac{1}{2}<α<1$，证明了任意大齐次初值下弱解的存在性；对于$α\in(\frac{2}{3},1)$，证明了弱解的光滑性，即所有弱解都是强解，并满足特定的远场衰减估计（far field decay estimates）。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了二维亚耗散Navier-Stokes方程在分数阶扩散下自相似解的存在性与正则性理论，特别在参数范围$α\in(\frac{2}{3},1)$内证明了弱解的光滑性，为这类方程的解行为提供了重要理论保证。

Abstract: We study the forward self-similar solutions to the $2$D hypodissipative Navier-Stokes equation with fractional diffusion $(-Δ)^α$ for $\frac{1}{2}<α<1$. We first show that for arbitrarily large $(1-2α)$-homogeneous initial data which are locally Lipschitz, there exists at least one weak solution whose profile differs from the self-similar profile of the fractional heat equation by an element of $H^α(\mathbb{R}^2)$. Moreover, when $α\in(\frac{2}{3},1)$ we show that any such weak solution is actually smooth, hence a strong solution, and satisfies certain far field decay estimates.

</details>

### [32] [Zero-field superconducting vortices and Majorana zero modes pinned by magnetic islands in correlated Rashba systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12338)
*Panagiotis Kotetes,Brian M. Andersen*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索在零磁场条件下稳定超导涡旋的新途径，特别是在具有磁性岛和Rashba自旋轨道耦合的系统中，为实验上实现复合涡旋-马约拉纳激发提供理论基础。

Method: 方法基于将超导体与具有面外磁矩的磁性岛交换耦合，利用Rashba自旋轨道耦合效应，考虑具有磁性关联但无长程磁有序的超导体，通过磁性梯度产生非零涡度。

Result: 结果表明，磁性梯度产生的涡度使超导涡旋在能量上稳定，电子磁化能的降低提供了稳定机制，并预测了在超导拓扑绝缘体表面和平面Rashba超导体中零场涡旋和马约拉纳零模的出现。

Conclusion: 该理论揭示了一种非标准的路径，用于在实验可达的系统中捕获复合涡旋-马约拉纳激发，为零磁场下稳定超导涡旋和马约拉纳零模提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We propose a route for pinning zero-field superconducting vortices in systems which are exchange-coupled to magnetic islands and feature Rashba spin-orbit coupling. We consider islands with sizes which greatly exceed those of the vortex cores and possess out-of-plane magnetic moments. A crucial ingredient of our approach is that it considers superconductors which are governed by magnetic correlations without, however, exhibiting long range magnetic order. The arising total magnetization is inhomogeneous and its gradients generate a nonzero vorticity in the superconducting phase. Vortices become energetically stable due to the energy reduction brought about from the generation of electronic magnetization. Using our developed framework, we make concrete predictions for the emergence of zero-field vortices and Majorana zero modes in superconducting topological insulator surfaces and planar Rashba superconductors. Our theory uncovers a nonstandard path for trapping composite vortex-Majorana excitations in systems which appear to be within experimental reach.

### [33] [Ambient-pressure 151-K superconductivity in HgBa2Ca2Cu3O8+δ via pressure quench](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12437)
*Liangzi Deng,Thacien Habamahoro,Artin Safezoddeh,Bishnu Karki,Sudaice Kazibwe,Daniel J. Schulze,Zheng Wu,Matthew Julian,Rohit P. Prasankumar,Hua Zhou,Jesse S. Smith,Pavan R. Hosur,Ching-Wu Chu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导研究的主要驱动力是提高超导转变温度（Tc），因其在能源效率和量子技术方面的巨大应用潜力。然而，自1993年以来常压Tc记录一直停滞不前，后续进展仅限于高压条件下，限制了超导技术的实际应用。

Method: 研究团队开发了压力淬火协议（PQP）来稳定常压下的压力诱导/增强超导态。该方法应用于铜酸盐HgBa2Ca2Cu3O8+δ，并通过同步辐射X射线衍射测量以及声子和电子结构计算提供实验支持。

Result: 通过PQP在铜酸盐HgBa2Ca2Cu3O8+δ中实现了151K的创纪录常压超导转变温度（Tc），这是自1993年以来常压Tc的重大突破。

Conclusion: 这一突破为稳定和探索常压高温超导态及其他先前仅在高压下可及的量子态开辟了新途径，为高温超导及其他领域的深入理解和实际应用铺平了道路。

Abstract: Superconductivity has been a vigorously researched topic since its discovery in 1911. Raising the superconducting transition temperature (Tc) has been the main driving force behind such long-sustained efforts due to its potential for impacting humanity and the fundamental knowledge gained from understanding this macroscopic coherent quantum state at high temperatures. The successful development of high-Tc superconductivity will make possible extraordinarily efficient generation, delivery, and utilization of energy, and could also enable the development of controlled fusion while impacting other burgeoning fields like quantum computation and quantum electronics. However, progress has been hindered by a longstanding plateau in the record ambient-pressure Tc, unchanged since 1993. Subsequent significant advancements in Tc have been achieved only under high pressures, preventing the realization of superconductivity's full potential. To directly address this challenge, we developed a pressure-quench protocol (PQP) to stabilize pressure-induced/-enhanced superconducting states at ambient pressure. Here we achieve a record ambient-pressure Tc of 151 K in the cuprate HgBa2Ca2Cu3O8+δ via PQP. The experimental results are further supported by synchrotron X-ray diffraction measurements and phonon and electronic structure calculations. This breakthrough opens new avenues for stabilizing and exploring ambient-pressure high-Tc superconducting states and other quantum states that have been previously only accessible under pressure, paving the way for deeper understanding and practical applications of high-Tc superconductivity and beyond.

### [34] [Real-time detection of critical slowing-down at the superconducting phase transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12473)
*Guillermo Nava Antonio,Théo Courtois,Corentin Pfaff,KM Shivangi Shukla,Asle Sudbø,Stéphane Mangin,Thomas Hauet,Chiara Ciccarelli*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究利用光学泵浦-太赫兹探测光谱技术，在宽激发通量范围内观测NbN中超导性被抑制的超快过程，发现当吸收光能接近超导体凝聚能时，超导淬灭时间显著延长，这构成了临界慢化的非平衡类似现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在实时观测超导体在非平衡条件下的临界动力学行为，特别是探索接近临界点时超导性动力学的慢化现象，为研究非平衡临界现象开辟新途径。

Method: 采用光学泵浦-太赫兹探测光谱技术（optical pump-THz probe spectroscopy）对NbN进行宽激发通量范围的测量，并结合时间依赖的Ginzburg-Landau模拟分析超导动力学行为。

Result: 实验发现当吸收光能接近超导体凝聚能（condensation energy）时，超导淬灭时间显著延长，这一现象被解释为动态相变边界处自由能景观平坦化导致的临界慢化（critical slowing-down）非平衡类似现象。

Conclusion: 该研究首次实时观测到接近临界点时超导动力学的慢化现象，证实了时间依赖Ginzburg-Landau模拟的预测，为利用时间分辨太赫兹光谱研究非平衡临界现象开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We employ optical pump-THz probe spectroscopy to chart the ultrafast superconductivity suppression in NbN over a broad range of excitation fluences. Our measurements uncover a pronounced lengthening of the superconductivity quenching time when the absorbed optical energy is close to the condensation energy of the superconductor, which constitutes a non-equilibrium analog of critical slowing-down on a timescale comparable to that of superconducting fluctuations. Time-dependent Ginzburg-Landau simulations reproduce this behavior and ascribe it to the flattening of the free energy landscape at the dynamical phase transition boundary. Our findings represent a direct observation in real time of slowed-down superconductivity dynamics in proximity to a critical point and open a pathway for investigating out-of-equilibrium critical phenomena with time-resolved THz spectroscopy.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用扫描隧道显微镜和谱学（scanning tunneling microscopy and spectroscopy）技术，该方法能够以晶格尺度分辨率直接获取局域态密度（local density of states），满足对实空间成像与局域谱学结合的需求。

Result: 综述总结了利用该技术研究多个代表性非常规超导体（unconventional superconductors）的最新进展，重点关注对高温超导面（high-temperature superconducting planes）、对密度波（pair-density waves）以及人工异质结构和本征材料中拓扑超导性（topological superconductivity）的直接表征。

Conclusion: 基于微观洞察（microscopic insights），文章最后概述了当前面临的挑战和未来的研究方向，强调了扫描隧道显微术在揭示二维超导体系复杂量子现象中的关键作用。

Abstract: Two-dimensional superconductivity has become a major frontier in condensed matter physics. It holds the key to the mechanism of high-temperature superconductors and offers an exceptional arena to stabilize emergent quantum states enabled by enhanced electron correlations in reduced dimensionality. These states are frequently characterized by spatial modulations and intertwined with competing orders, calling for studies that combine real-space imaging with local spectroscopy. Scanning tunneling microscopy and spectroscopy meets this need by directly accessing local density of states with lattice-scale resolution. In this review, we summarize recent advances of the study on several representative unconventional superconductors using this technique, focusing on direct characterization of high-temperature superconducting planes, pair-density waves, and topological superconductivity in both artificial heterostructures and intrinsic materials. We conclude by outlining current challenges and future directions motivated by the microscopic insights.

### [36] [Finite-momentum superconductivity with singlet-triplet mixing in an altermagnetic metal: A pairing instability analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12897)
*Hui Hu,Zhao Liu,Jia Wang,Xia-Ji Liu,Yoji Ohashi*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于分析反铁磁金属（altermagnetic metal）在吸引相互作用下的配对不稳定性，特别关注反铁磁自旋劈裂如何影响配对机制和超导相的形成。

Method: 研究方法基于方晶格模型，采用最近邻吸引相互作用分析多种配对通道，包括偶宇称扩展s波和d波态，以及两个奇宇称p波通道。研究考察了不同形式的反铁磁性，特别是dxy波和dx2-y2波反铁磁耦合。

Result: 研究结果显示反铁磁自旋劈裂导致不同自旋电子间的有限动量配对，这种配对通常以混合宇称的多通道形式出现，形成具有单重态-三重态混合的多分量FFLO超导相。相同自旋的三重态配对则发生在零质心动量下，且在弱反铁磁耦合和低电子填充时不利。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明反铁磁金属中的配对不稳定性会产生具有混合宇称多分量的有限动量FFLO超导相，同时探讨了在位吸引相互作用对混合宇称配对的影响。

Abstract: We analyze the pairing instability of an altermagnetic metal on a square lattice driven by an attractive nearest-neighbor interaction. This interaction enables multiple pairing channels, including even-parity extended $s$-wave and $d$-wave states, as well as two odd-parity $p$-wave channels. We verify that altermagnetic spin-splitting in the single-particle dispersion gives rise to finite-momentum pairing between electrons with unlike spins, in agreement with earlier predictions. Quite unexpectedly, this pairing typically emerges across multiple channels with mixed parity. Consequently, the resulting finite-momentum Fulde--Ferrell--Larkin--Ovchinnikov (FFLO) superconducting phase is expected to exhibit a multi-component order parameter featuring singlet-triplet mixing. We examine several forms of altermagnetism, specifically $d_{xy}$-wave and $d_{x^{2}-y^{2}}$-wave altermagnetic couplings, and present the corresponding phase diagrams. Additionally, we investigate the triplet pairing between electrons with identical spins, and find that it consistently occurs at zero center-of-mass momentum and is unfavorable at weak altermagnetic coupling and low electron filling. The influence of on-site attractive interactions on mixed-parity pairing is also explored.

### [37] [Looking for non-gaussianity in Pulsar Timing Arrays through the four point correlator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12311)
*Adrien Kuntz,Clemente Smarra,Massimo Vaglio*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究计算了脉冲星计时阵列中随机引力波背景的四点关联函数，作为探测非高斯特征的主要工具，并提出了将非高斯效应纳入参数估计流程的边际化似然方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 脉冲星计时阵列近期报告了随机引力波背景的有力证据。标准分析假设傅里叶系数服从高斯统计，但若背景源于有限数量的超大质量黑洞双星并合，则可能出现非高斯特征，使得高阶关联函数的确定至关重要。

Method: 本研究计算了任意四个脉冲星位置下随机引力波背景傅里叶系数的完整四点关联函数，将其识别为探测非高斯性的主要探针。结果分为高斯贡献（与两点函数的平方成正比）和真正的非高斯连通分量，其非平凡角度依赖性将Hellings和Downs关联推广到四个脉冲星。

Result: 四点关联函数的角度结构仅依赖于天线模式函数乘积的平均值，因此预计与背景的具体物理起源无关。研究进一步提出了通过推导边际化似然来将四点关联函数纳入参数估计流程，该方法微扰地考虑了非高斯效应。

Conclusion: 该结果为在脉冲星计时阵列数据中搜索非高斯特征提供了理论框架，为更完整地刻画引力波背景特性开辟了道路。

Abstract: Pulsar Timing Arrays have recently reported strong evidence for a stochastic gravitational wave background. In standard analyses, it is modeled through pulsar-dependent Fourier coefficients assumed to follow gaussian statistics, so that the signal is fully characterized by its two-point function. However, if the background arises from a finite population of inspiralling supermassive black hole binaries, non-gaussian features may emerge, making the determination of higher-order correlators essential. In this work, we compute the complete four-point correlator of the stochastic gravitational wave background Fourier coefficients for four arbitrary pulsar positions, identifying it as the leading probe of non-gaussianity. The result separates into a gaussian contribution, proportional to the square of the two-point function, and a genuinely non-gaussian connected component, whose non-trivial angular dependence generalizes the Hellings and Downs correlation to four pulsars. This angular structure depends only on averages of products of antenna pattern functions, and is therefore expected to be independent of the specific physical origin of the background. We further propose to incorporate the four-point correlator into the parameter-estimation pipeline by deriving a marginalized likelihood that perturbatively accounts for non-gaussian effects. Our results provide the theoretical framework to search for non-gaussian features in pulsar timing array data, opening the way to a more complete characterization of gravitational-wave backgrounds.

</details>


### [38] [Dynamical Tidal response of compact stars -- An EFT approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12331)
*Gregory Jarequi,Soumodeep Mitra,Varun Vaidya*

Main category: gr-qc

Method: 采用点粒子有效场论（EFT）方法，结合黑洞微扰理论（Black Hole Perturbation Theory, BPHT）计算任意非旋转致密星体的散射振幅。使用Mano-Suzuki-Takasugi（MST）方法处理非零表面反射率，并将结果与点粒子EFT在低频展开中逐阶匹配。

Result: 建立了提取静态和动力学潮汐洛夫数（TLNs）的系统框架，可计算多极展开中的任意阶项。具体计算了非粘性中子星以及混合玻色子或费米子暗物质的中子星的次次领头阶（Next-to-Next-to Leading Order）潮汐洛夫数，并推导了其重整化群（Renormalization Group）方程。

Conclusion: 该研究成功将点粒子有效场论方法系统应用于致密星体，建立了计算潮汐洛夫数的通用框架。所发展的技术能够处理包含暗物质成分的中子星，为研究致密天体的潮汐响应提供了系统化的理论工具。

Abstract: We apply the point particle EFT approach to a compact star to systematically compute dynamical tidal love numbers for various non-rotating compact objects, extending the treatment of {arXiv:2307.10391[hep-th], arXiv:2407.08327 [gr-qc]}. We calculate the scattering amplitude in Black Hole Perturbation Theory(BPHT) for \textit{arbitrary} non-rotating compact stars using the Mano-Suzuki-Takasugi(MST) method with non zero surface reflectivity and match it with that obtained from point particle EFT order by order in the low frequency expansion. This sets up a systematic framework for extracting the static and dynamical tidal love numbers(TLNs) to any order in the multipole expansion. In this paper, we employ the technique to compute the Next-to-Next-to Leading Order TLN upto a universal constant and its Renormalization Group equation for non-viscous Neutron stars and Neutron stars admixed with Bosonic or Fermionic dark matter.

### [39] [Synthetic gravitational lens image of the Sagittarius A${}^*$ black hole with a thin disk model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12402)
*Ezequiel F. Boero,Osvaldo M. Moreschi*

TL;DR: 本文通过构建不同配置的简单吸积盘模型，模拟了人马座A*（Sgr A*）的图像，并与事件视界望远镜（EHT）合作组发布的观测图像进行对比。研究发现，尽管EHT合作组倾向于排除2017年4月6日的图像，但作者的最佳模拟图像与该日期的Themis处理流程输出结果相似，从而支持了吸积盘近侧向（edge-on）的几何构型。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者构建了一个简单的吸积盘模型，该模型在先前工作中已成功再现M87*的主要观测特征。他们生成了两种主要配置的图像：第一种基于EHT最佳图像（倾斜盘面，具有三个亮区）；第二种则详细探索了近侧向（edge-on）的取向。模拟采用了高效的射线追踪（ray tracing）和测地线偏离（geodesic deviation）方法，以考虑形变、相对论效应和放大效应。

Result: 模拟图像与EHT使用2017年4月6日和7日数据重建的图像进行了比较。研究发现，尽管EHT合作组似乎排除了4月6日的图像，但作者的最佳建议图像与4月6日Themis处理流程的输出结果相似。这一相似性为吸积盘的近侧向（edge-on）几何配置提供了支持。

Conclusion: 基于模拟图像与观测数据的对比，本文得出结论：近侧向（edge-on）的吸积盘几何构型能够更好地解释EHT观测到的人马座A*图像特征，特别是与2017年4月6日Themis处理流程的输出结果的一致性，为该构型提供了证据。

Abstract: The images of Sagittarius A${}^*$ published by the Event Horizon Telescope (ETH) Collaboration in 2022 present features that were associated with an emission ring consistent with what is expected from an accretion disc surrounding the supermassive black hole at the center of our Galaxy. Here, we generate images of Sgr~A${}^*$ across different configurations of a simple accretion disc model that became successful, in our previous work, in reproducing the main features observed in M87*. Their best image, here reproduced in Fig. 1, suggests a geometric configuration of an inclined disk with three bright regions; which we have considered as our first configuration. Since we were not convinced with the results of this first configuration, we also explore in detail the case of nearly edge-on orientations which are a priori the expected geometry for a relaxed disc, as seen from the plane of the galaxy. We have produced simulated images using an efficient ray tracing and geodesic deviation methodology that allows to account for deformation, relativistic and magnification effects. We compare our synthetic images with the EHT images reconstructed with data from April 6 and 7 of 2017. We found that, although the EHT Collaboration seems to discard the image from April 6, our best suggested image resembles the output from the {\sc Themis} pipeline for April 6; which for us gives support for the edge-on configuration.
