### [40] [An efficient higher-order WKB code for quasinormal modes and greybody factors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12466)
*Roman A. Konoplya,Jerzy Matyjasek,Alexander Zhidenko*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文介绍了高阶WKB（Wentzel-Kramers-Brillouin）准正规模计算代码的更新优化版本，通过将有效势能在其最大值处展开为泰勒级数而非直接计算完整解析表达式，显著减少了计算时间，尤其对于涉及非有理函数的复杂势能，速度提升可达数个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过去几年中，经过高阶扩展和Padé重求和（Padé resummation）显著提升精度的高阶WKB Mathematica代码已在众多研究中广泛应用。本文旨在提供该代码的更新优化版本，以解决计算效率问题。

Method: 主要改进在于将有效势能（effective potential）在其最大值处展开为泰勒级数（Taylor series），而不是为每个特定势能计算完整的WKB公式解析表达式。这种方法保留了方法的准确性。

Result: 该方法实现了计算时间的大幅减少。当有效势能复杂且涉及非有理函数（non-rational functions）时，速度增益可达数个数量级，同时保持了方法的计算精度。

Conclusion: 通过将有效势能展开为泰勒级数的优化方法，显著提升了高阶WKB准正规模计算代码的计算效率，为复杂势能系统的研究提供了更高效的工具。

Abstract: The higher-order WKB Mathematica code for computing quasinormal modes, whose accuracy was significantly enhanced through extensions to higher orders and, in particular, through the use of Padé resummation, has been widely employed in numerous studies over the past several years. In this work, we present an updated and optimized version of the code. The main improvement consists in expanding the effective potential in a Taylor series around its maximum, rather than evaluating the full analytic expression of the WKB formula for each specific potential. This modification leads to a substantial reduction in computation time. In cases where the effective potential is complicated and involves non-rational functions, the speed gain can reach several orders of magnitude, while preserving the accuracy of the method.

</details>


### [41] [Thermodynamics and information recovery of Schwarzschild AdS black holes in Cotton gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12524)
*Yahya Ladghami,Brahim Asfour,Francisco S. N. Lobo,Taoufik Ouali*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了Cotton引力中的Schwarzschild AdS黑洞，分析了其热力学性质及通过岛屿公式（island formula）的信息恢复。研究发现Cotton参数显著影响相结构，正参数时存在类范德瓦尔斯临界性（Van der Waals-like criticality），负参数时则无；岛屿公式可恢复Page曲线（Page curve），晚期熵饱和于两倍Bekenstein-Hawking值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Cotton引力中Schwarzschild AdS黑洞的热力学性质与量子信息恢复之间的联系。将宇宙学常数视为压力，Cotton参数作为独立变量，探索修正引力理论中黑洞相结构对信息恢复过程的影响。

Method: 采用Cotton引力理论框架，将宇宙学常数处理为压力，Cotton参数作为独立变量。使用岛屿公式（island prescription）计算Hawking辐射的纠缠熵（entanglement entropy），分析有无岛屿情况下的熵演化。

Result: Bekenstein-Hawking面积定律成立，但Cotton参数显著影响相结构：正参数时存在极值极限和类范德瓦尔斯临界性（Van der Waals-like criticality），伴随一阶和二阶相变；负参数时无极值极限或临界性。无岛屿时纠缠熵无限增长违反幺正性（unitarity），包含岛屿后恢复Page曲线，晚期熵饱和于两倍Bekenstein-Hawking值。Page时间可表示为热力学量，正Cotton参数时显示临界行为，负Cotton引力中小黑洞信息恢复快而大黑洞慢，压力可减少Page时间。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了黑洞热力学、量子信息恢复与修正引力理论之间的直接联系。Cotton参数对相结构和信息恢复过程具有决定性影响，岛屿机制能有效恢复幺正性，Page时间与热力学性质密切相关。

Abstract: We study Schwarzschild AdS black holes in Cotton gravity, focusing on their thermodynamics and information recovery via the island formula. Treating the cosmological constant as pressure and the Cotton parameter as an independent variable, we find that the Bekenstein-Hawking area law holds, while the Cotton parameter dramatically affects phase structure. For a positive Cotton parameter, black holes admit an extremal limit and exhibit Van der Waals-like criticality with first and second order phase transitions; for a negative Cotton parameter, no extremal limit or criticality occurs. Using the island prescription, we show that without islands, the entanglement entropy of Hawking radiation grows unboundedly, violating unitarity, while including islands after Page time restores the Page curve, with late-time entropy saturating at twice the Bekenstein-Hawking value. Page time can be expressed in terms of thermodynamic quantities, displaying critical behavior for positive Cotton parameter, whereas in negative Cotton gravity small black holes recover information rapidly and large ones more slowly, with pressure reducing Page time. Our results reveal a direct link between black hole thermodynamics, quantum information recovery, and modified gravity

</details>


### [42] [Traversable Wormholes induced by Thomas-Fermi energy density](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12527)
*Remo Garattini,Francisco S. N. Lobo,Kirill Zatrimaylov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了由现实暗物质晕支持的球对称静态可穿越虫洞，基于Thomas-Fermi型密度分布构建了显式形状函数，分析了径向和切向压力，并建立了独立于显式度规函数的物质分布分析框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索由物理上合理的暗物质能量密度分布支持的可穿越虫洞（traversable wormholes），重点关注如何利用现实暗物质晕（dark matter halos）构建物理一致的虫洞几何结构。

Method: 采用Thomas-Fermi型分布构建显式形状函数$b(r)$，分析径向和切向压力，处理喉部（throat）的flare-out条件和无视界要求；探索零潮汐力配置（zero-tidal-force configurations）和非均匀状态方程（inhomogeneous equations of state），在有限半径处实施边界条件以确保能量密度和压力消失。

Result: 通过适当选择径向压力，获得了在整个时空中有限且行为良好的红移函数；推导了渐近展开式以表征暗物质晕边缘附近的度规和物质行为；将爱因斯坦场方程完全用能量密度、径向和切向压力及其导数重新表述，提供了独立于显式度规函数的物质分布分析框架。

Conclusion: 研究结果为构建由现实暗物质晕支持的物理一致虫洞几何提供了系统方法，突出了物质分布、状态方程和几何约束之间复杂的相互作用，为暗物质支持的虫洞结构分析建立了理论框架。

Abstract: We investigate spherically symmetric and static traversable wormholes supported by exotic matter, focusing on solutions sourced by physically motivated dark matter energy density profiles. Considering the Thomas-Fermi-type distribution, we construct explicit forms of the shape function $b(r)$ and analyze the resulting radial and tangential pressures, carefully addressing the requirements of the flare-out condition at the throat and the absence of horizons. We explore zero-tidal-force configurations as well as inhomogeneous equations of state, demonstrating how appropriate choices of the radial pressure allow for finite and well-behaved redshift functions throughout the spacetime. Boundary conditions at a finite radius are implemented to ensure vanishing energy density and pressures, and asymptotic expansions are derived to characterize the behavior of the metric and matter content near the edge of the dark matter halo. Additionally, we reformulate the Einstein field equations entirely in terms of the energy density, radial and tangential pressures, and their derivatives, providing a framework to analyze the matter distribution independently of the explicit metric functions. Our results offer a systematic methodology to construct physically consistent wormhole geometries supported by realistic dark matter halos, highlighting the intricate interplay between matter profiles, equations of state, and geometric constraints.

</details>


### [43] [Shaving off soft hairs and the black hole image memory effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12670)
*Shaoqi Hou,Zong-Hong Zhu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了软毛（soft hair）克尔黑洞（Kerr black hole）的成像特征，发现软毛会导致黑洞图像在观测者视场中发生旋转、膨胀和漂移，产生"图像记忆效应（image memory effect）"，这为软毛存在提供了关键证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞软毛是与广义邦迪-梅茨纳-萨克斯（Bondi-Metzner-Sachs）对称性相关的诺特荷（Noether charges）。研究旨在探索软毛如何影响克尔黑洞的观测图像，特别是寻找能够证实软毛存在的可观测效应。

Method: 通过理论分析研究软毛克尔黑洞的成像特性，比较其与无毛（bald）黑洞图像的差异。具体方法包括分析图像在天空平面（celestial plane）上的几何变换，并估算大质量旋转黑洞伴随较小黑洞时的图像记忆效应幅度。

Result: 软毛克尔黑洞图像相对于无毛黑洞发生旋转、膨胀和以恒定速度沿固定方向漂移。这些效应均具有角度依赖性。当黑洞软毛因视界附近物理过程发射引力波或电磁波而改变时，图像会在观测者视场中漫游，产生图像记忆效应。该效应幅度与大型黑洞质量成正比，随其自旋增加而增大，但随质量比减小而降低。

Conclusion: 图像记忆效应是软毛存在的关键证据（smoking gun），但受限于当前及未来探测器的角分辨率（angular resolution），且忽略宇宙膨胀影响时，该效应难以被探测到。

Abstract: Soft hairs of black holes are the Noether charges associated to the generalized Bondi-Metzner-Sachs symmetries. In this work, the images of soft-haired Kerr black holes were studied. For an eternal black hole, the image is rotated, dilated and drifting compared to that of the bald counterpart in the celestial plane. The rotation and the dilation are independent of the time, while the drifting is at a constant speed and in a fixed direction. These effects all depend on angular directions. The soft hair of an astronomical black hole can change due to the emission of the gravitational or electromagnetic wave from the various physical processes occurring in the vicinity of the horizon. Then, the image roams in the observer's view, causing the image memory effect, the smoking gun for the existence of the soft hair. The magnitude of the image memory effect of a huge, spinning black hole accompanied by a much smaller one was estimated. It turns out that this effect is proportional to the mass of the large black hole, increases with its spin, but descreases with the mass ratio. Due to the limited angular resolution of the current and the future detectors, this effect is hard to be detected, if the impact of the cosmological expansion is ignored.

</details>


### [44] [Third type of spacetime with the coexistence of integrability and non-integrability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12674)
*Junjie Lu,Xin Wu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文发现了一种新型时空（第三类时空），其类时测地线（timelike geodesics）具有不可积动力学，而类光测地线（null geodesics）保持可积性。这通过共形变换（conformal transformations）等方法实现，共形克尔度规（conformal Kerr metric）等是具体实例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，时空的可积性（integrability）通常指类时和类光测地线运动是否可积。标准黑洞时空（如史瓦西和克尔度规）属于第一类（两者皆可积），而梅尔文型时空（Melvin type spacetimes）属于第二类（两者皆不可积）。本文旨在探索是否存在第三类时空，其类时与类光测地线动力学具有不同的可积性。

Method: 主要方法包括共形变换（conformal transformations），该变换可将第一类时空解转化为第三类时空。此外，论文也探索了非共形解的其他途径，如克尔-贝托蒂-罗宾逊黑洞度规（Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson black hole metric）和加速史瓦西时空（accelerating Schwarzschild spacetime）。

Result: 论文成功发现了第三类时空的存在。共形变换通过共形因子（conformal factors）阻止了哈密顿-雅可比方程（Hamilton-Jacobi equation）的变量分离，导致类时测地线运动缺少第四个运动常数（constant of motion），从而不可积。然而，类光测地线不受共形因子影响，保持可积性。

Conclusion: 时空的可积性分类可扩展为三类：第一类（类时与类光测地线皆可积）、第二类（两者皆不可积）、第三类（类时不可积而类光可积）。共形克尔度规是第三类时空的典型例子，且存在非共形解也能产生此类时空。

Abstract: The integrability or non-integrability of a spacetime usually refers to whether the motion of massive or massless particles in the spacetime is integrable or not. The standard black hole spacetimes such as the Schwarzschild and Kerr metrics are always integrable for both timelike and null geodesics. They belong to a first type of spacetime. However, the Melvin type spacetimes as a second type of spacetime are non-integrable, regardless of whether they are for massive or massless particle motion. In this paper, we discover the possibility of a third type of spacetime with non-integrable dynamics of timelike geodesics and integrable dynamics of null geodesics. In fact, conformal transformations may transform type one solutions into type three. This is due to the conformal factors preventing the separation of variables from the Hamilton-Jacobi equation and leading to the absence of a fourth constant of motion for the massive particle dynamics. Nevertheless, the massless particle motion still remains integrable in these metrics for any conformal factors because the conformal factors have no effect on the null geodesics whatsoever. The conformal Kerr metric is an example of the third type of spacetime. In addition to the conformal transformation method, other paths may yield the third type of spacetime. The Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson black hole metric and the accelerating Schwarzschild spacetime are two examples of non-conformal solutions that are also of type three.

</details>


### [45] [Rotating wormholes in five dimensions with equal angular momenta: large asymmetry regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12748)
*Keiya Uemichi,Yasutaka Koga,Daiki Saito,Chul-Moon Yoo,Daisuke Yoshida*

Main category: gr-qc

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在澄清五维时空中具有等角动量的旋转虫洞解中旋转与能量条件之间的关系，特别是针对虫洞两侧存在较大不对称性的情况。先前Dzhunushaliev等人的研究表明，由于旋转效应，零能量条件（null energy condition）的违反可以变得任意小。

Method: 研究基于爱因斯坦方程与幻影场（phantom field）耦合的五维时空中的旋转虫洞解，特别关注具有等角动量的情况。通过分析虫洞两侧的不对称性（即两个渐近区域的质量差异）对能量条件违反程度的影响，探讨旋转与能量条件之间的关系。

Result: 研究发现零能量条件（null energy condition）的违反程度主要由角动量决定，而对不对称性（即两个渐近区域的质量差异）的依赖性很小。此外，在角动量较大的极限下，虫洞时空几何渐近于极端Myers-Perry时空，而非极端黑洞几何在任何极限下都无法重现。

Conclusion: 旋转虫洞解中零能量条件（null energy condition）的违反主要受角动量控制，而非虫洞两侧的不对称性。虫洞时空在角动量较大时趋近于极端Myers-Perry黑洞几何，但无法重现非极端黑洞几何。

Abstract: We clarify the relationship between rotation and the energy condition for stationary rotating wormhole solutions of the Einstein equations coupled to a phantom field in five-dimensional spacetime with equal angular momenta, particularly with large asymmetry between the two sides. It was shown by Dzhunushaliev et al. that the violation of the null energy condition can become arbitrarily small due to rotation. We find that the degree of violation of the null energy condition is essentially determined by the angular momentum and shows little dependence on asymmetry, that is, the mass difference between the two asymptotic regions. We also discuss the relation between the wormhole spacetime and the Myers-Perry black hole. We find that the geometry asymptotes to the extremal Myers-Perry spacetime in the limit of large angular momentum, while the non-extremal black hole geometry cannot be reproduced in any limit.

Abstract: In this paper, we study the effect of the modified dispersion relation (MDR) on the thermodynamics of the Kerr-Newman black hole surrounded by quintessence and a cloud of string. The thermodynamic properties of the Kerr-Newman black hole are shown to rely not only on the black hole's properties but also on the parameters associated with the modified dispersion relation, quintessence, and the cloud string. Additionally, the equation of state is impacted by these parameters. The remnant and the stability of the black hole are also discussed under the correction of MDR, quintessence, and a cloud of string. In addition, the null geodesic structure of the spacetime is studied using the Hamilton--Jacobi formalism. The effective potential for photon motion is obtained, and the radii of the prograde and retrograde circular photon orbits are determined. The instability of these circular photon orbits is further characterized by the Lyapunov exponent.

### [47] [Kerr-Newman black hole surrounded by quintessence under quantum gravity effects and gravity's rainbow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12784)
*Aheibam Boycha Meitei,Irom Ablu Meitei,Telem Ibungochouba Singh,Kangujam Yugindro Singh*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究方法包括：1) 将广义不确定原理（Generalized Uncertainty Principle, GUP）应用于标量粒子的Klein-Gordon方程和费米子的Dirac方程；2) 求解广义Klein-Gordon方程和Dirac方程；3) 使用修正的Hamilton-Jacobi方程（即修正的Rarita-Schwinger方程）研究费米子隧穿；4) 在彩虹引力（gravity rainbow）框架下使用彩虹函数（rainbow functions）分析黑洞热力学。

Result: 研究结果表明：1) 被quintessence包围的Kerr-Newman黑洞的修正霍金温度不仅依赖于黑洞性质，还依赖于发射粒子的量子数和quintessence参数；2) 在彩虹引力框架下，霍金温度、热容、状态方程参数和熵都受到quintessence和彩虹引力的共同影响。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the quantum gravity effects on the tunneling of particles and gravity's rainbow across the event horizon of Kerr-Newman black hole (KNBH) surrounded by the quintessence. The aspect of quantum gravity has been introduced by applying the Generalized Uncertainty Principle (GUP) to the Klein-Gordon equation and the Dirac equation of scalar and fermion particles. By solving the Generalized Klein-Gordon and Dirac equations obeyed by scalar and fermion particles, corrections to the Hawking temperature of the KNBH in the presence of quintessence is discussed. The tunneling of fermions is also examined using the modified Hamilton-Jacobi equation also known as modified Rarita-Schwinger equation, and the corrected Hawking temperature is determined. The corrected Hawking temperature of the KNBH surrounded by quintessence is found to be dependent not only on the properties of the black hole but also on the quantum numbers of the emitted particles and quintessence. Then, we explored the KNBH surrounded by quintessence within the framework of gravity rainbow using rainbow functions. In the context of rainbow functions in loop quantum gravity, we derive the Hawking temperature, heat capacity, equation of state parameters, and entropy for the KNBH surrounded by quintessence. It is found that these quantities are influenced by both the quintessence and the rainbow gravity.

### [48] [Investigating quark star properties through baryon number density $(n)$ within the framework of $f(Q)$ gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12907)
*Sourav Biswas,Debadri Bhattacharjee,Pradip Kumar Chattopadhyay,Nawal H. Siddig,Euaggelos E. Zotos*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: In this paper, we construct a viable strange star model in the framework of MIT bag model equation of state, $p_r=\frac{1}{3}(ρ-4B)$, where $B$ is the bag constant. We have determined the possible range of baryon number density ($n$) for stable quark matter inside the star and calculated the corresponding range of $B$. By solving TOV equations, we obtain possible maximum mass and radius considering MIT bag model equation of state with baryon number density dependent $B$. All the physical parameters such as $ρ,~p_r,~p_t$ and anisotropy parameter ($Δ$) have been analysed in this model to established the physical viability as well as acceptability of the model. Then, we study the stability of the model by analysing the causality conditions, energy conditions, generalised TOV equation, Herrera cracking condition and radial variation of adiabatic index. Within the parameter space used here to construct the model, we have predicted the radii of few compact stars and it is found that the model is suitable in predicting the radii of stars where masses lie below the $2.46~M\odot$ and the predicted radii from model are nearly equal to the values obtained from recent observations. It is significant to observe that up to $2.01~M\odot$, it maybe treated as Strange Star (SS). On the other hand, maximum mass above $2.01~M\odot$ and up to $2.46~M\odot$ may be treated as di-quark stars.

### [49] [Perturbative Renormalisation Group Improved Black Hole Solution and its Quasinormal Modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12919)
*Rupam Jyoti Borah,Umananda Dev Goswami*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于重整化群改进构建了微扰黑洞解，研究了其在SdS和SAdS时空下受标量场扰动时的准正规模特性，并比较了不同计算方法的结果一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于重整化群改进（renormalization group improvement）启发的微扰黑洞解，旨在探究此类黑洞在标量场扰动下的准正规模（quasinormal modes）特性，特别是在Schwarzschild-de Sitter（SdS）和Schwarzschild-anti-de Sitter（SAdS）背景下的行为。

Method: 对于SdS时空采用6阶Padé平均WKB近似方法计算准正规模，对于SAdS背景则使用直接射击法（direct shooting method）。同时分析标量场扰动的时间演化，使用时域分析提取准正规模频率，并采用矩阵铅笔法（matrix pencil method）从时域数据中提取准正规模。

Result: 研究发现准正规模频率对解的自由参数具有依赖性。从时域数据提取的准正规模频率重建的波形与原始时域剖面吻合良好。在SdS背景中，6阶Padé平均WKB方法与时域分析得到的准正规模频率高度一致；在SAdS时空中，直接射击法与时域分析的结果也显示出很好的一致性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，基于重整化群改进构建的微扰黑洞解在不同计算方法下得到的准正规模频率具有很好的一致性，验证了计算方法的可靠性，并为理解此类黑洞的扰动特性提供了重要参考。

Abstract: In this work, we construct a perturbative black hole (BH) solution motivated by renormalization group (RG) improvement and investigate the quasinormal modes (QNMs) of the BH under scalar field perturbations in both Schwarzschild-de Sitter (SdS) and Schwarzschild-anti-de Sitter (SAdS) backgrounds. To compute the QNMs in the SdS spacetime, we employ the 6th-order Padé-averaged WKB approximation method, while for the SAdS background we utilize the direct shooting method. We examine the dependence of the QNM frequencies on the free parameter of the solution. Furthermore, we analyze the time evolution of a scalar field perturbation around the BH and present the corresponding time-domain profiles. The QNMs are also extracted from the time-domain data using the matrix pencil method. Using the extracted QNM frequencies, we reconstruct the waveform and compare it with the original time-domain profile, finding good agreement between the two. The QNM frequencies obtained from the 6th-order Padé-averaged WKB method and the time-domain analysis in the SdS background, as well as those obtained from the direct shooting method and time-domain analysis in the SAdS spacetime, show very good consistency.

### [50] [The Bianchi IX Attractor in Modified Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13104)
*Ester Beatriz,Everaldo Bonotto,Phillipo Lappicy*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明了在修正引力理论（如Hořava-Lifshitz、λ-R或f(R)引力）中，对于超临界参数范围v∈(1/2,1)，所有Bianchi IX型解都收敛于Mixmaster吸引子，这与广义相对论中的Ringström吸引子定理类似但存在重要差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究修正引力理论（modified gravity theories）中真空各向异性空间均匀模型的动力学行为，这些模型预期能描述这些理论中的类空奇点（spacelike singularities）。通过引入参数v∈(0,1)扰动广义相对论中的Bianchi模型，探索超临界理论中的吸引子行为。

Method: 分析修正引力理论（包括Hořava-Lifshitz、λ-R和f(R)引力）中的Bianchi IX型真空各向异性空间均匀模型。通过参数v扰动广义相对论的Bianchi模型，其中v=1/2对应广义相对论恢复。重点研究超临界范围v∈(1/2,1)的动力学行为。

Result: 证明了超临界理论中的吸引子定理：对于任何v∈(1/2,1)，所有Bianchi IX型解都收敛于Mixmaster吸引子的类似物，该吸引子由Bianchi I型解（Kasner状态）和Bianchi II型解的异宿链组成。与广义相对论不同，没有解会收敛到Mixmaster以外的其他集合。

Conclusion: 修正引力理论中的超临界模型表现出与广义相对论中Ringström吸引子定理类似但更简单的动力学行为：所有Bianchi IX型解都必然收敛于Mixmaster吸引子，排除了收敛到局部旋转对称解等其他集合的可能性。

Abstract: We consider vacuum anisotropic spatially homogeneous models in certain modified gravity theories (such as Hořava-Lifshitz, $λ$-$R$ or $f(R)$ gravity), which are expected to describe generic spacelike singularities for these theories. These models perturb the well-known Bianchi models in general relativity (GR) by a parameter $v\in (0,1)$ with GR recovered at $v=1/2$. We prove an analogue of the well-known Ringström attractor theorem in GR to the supercritical theories: for any $v\in (1/2,1)$, all solutions of Bianchi type $\mathrm{IX}$ converge to an analogue of the Mixmaster attractor, consisting of Bianchi type I solutions (Kasner states) and heteroclinic chains of Bianchi type II solutions. In contrast to GR, there are no solutions that converge to a different set other than the Mixmaster (such as the locally rotationally symmetric solutions in GR).

</details>


### [51] [On Radiative Fluxes and Coulombic Charges in the Balance Law for Black Hole Evaporation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13120)
*Eugenio Bianchi,Daniel E. Paraizo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文研究了渐近平坦时空中标量场的辐射能量通量及其与黑洞蒸发的平衡定律，发现邦迪质量（Bondi mass）的量子修正依赖于霍金辐射的纠缠熵，且重整化辐射通量期望值为正，不同于标准的富林-戴维斯公式（Fulling-Davies formula）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在渐近平坦时空中，辐射通量与库仑电荷存在明确区分，二者的关系由平衡定律编码。论文旨在经典层面识别3+1维最小耦合无质量标量场的辐射能量通量，并研究黑洞蒸发中邦迪质量的平衡定律。

Method: 首先在经典层面识别3+1维最小耦合无质量标量场的辐射能量通量，然后在通常的球对称模型中研究半经典平衡定律。通过分析辐射通量的平衡定律，推导邦迪质量的量子修正。

Result: 在半经典平衡定律中，邦迪质量获得依赖于霍金辐射纠缠熵的量子修正。重整化辐射通量期望值明显为正，且与标准富林-戴维斯公式不一致。论文澄清了这一结果与Ashtekar-Taveras-Varadarajan关于2维膨胀黑洞提议的关系。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了邦迪质量在黑洞蒸发过程中的量子修正机制，强调了纠缠熵在平衡定律中的关键作用。这一发现对理解3+1维黑洞蒸发具有重要启示，表明辐射通量的重整化期望值呈现正定性特征。

Abstract: In asymptotically-flat spacetimes, there is a clear distinction between radiative fluxes and Coulombic charges, and their relation is encoded in balance laws. In this paper, we first identify at the classical level the radiative energy flux for a minimally-coupled massless scalar field in 3+1 dimensions, and then investigate the balance law for the Bondi mass in black hole evaporation. In the usual spherically-symmetric model, the semiclassical balance law for the radiative flux implies that the Bondi mass receives a quantum correction which depends on the entanglement entropy of the Hawking radiation. Furthermore, the renormalized expectation value of the radiative flux turns out to be manifestly positive and does not coincide with the standard Fulling-Davies formula. We clarify the relation of this result to the Ashtekar-Taveras-Varadarajan proposal for 2d dilatonic black holes, and discuss its implications for black hole evaporation in 3+1 dimensions.

</details>


### [52] [Challenging the Weak Cosmic Censorship with Phantom Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13210)
*Giovanni Caridi,Fabrizio Corelli,Paolo Pani*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟研究幻标量场（phantom scalar field）的球对称坍缩，该场违反主导能量条件（dominant energy condition），旨在检验彭罗斯弱宇宙监督猜想（weak cosmic censorship conjecture）在能量条件被违反时的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 彭罗斯弱宇宙监督猜想认为引力坍缩产生的时空奇点通常被事件视界隐藏，从而保持外部区域的可预测性。本研究旨在检验当主导能量条件被违反时（通过考虑具有负能量密度的幻标量场坍缩），该猜想是否仍然成立，以评估宇宙监督的鲁棒性。

Method: 采用基于四阶有限差分格式的高精度数值相对论模拟，从表示规则幻标量波包的平滑、渐近平坦初始数据出发，跟踪其通过坍缩或色散的全非线性演化过程。

Result: 与普通正能标量场在黑洞形成阈值处表现出标准Choptuik临界行为不同，幻标量场显示出质的不同动力学特性。在所有考虑的振幅下，未发现俘获面、裸奇点或替代稳态终态的证据；幻标量场总是色散，表明即使存在负能物质，宇宙监督仍动态保持。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，即使违反主导能量条件，宇宙监督猜想仍可能保持动态有效性，幻标量场坍缩不会产生裸奇点，而是始终色散，支持了宇宙监督的鲁棒性。

Abstract: Penrose's weak cosmic censorship conjecture asserts that spacetime singularities produced by gravitational collapse are generically hidden behind event horizons, thus preventing them from causally influencing distant observers and preserving the predictability of the exterior region. In this work, we probe this conjecture in a setup that deliberately violates one of its central assumptions - the dominant energy condition - by considering the spherical collapse of a phantom scalar field with negative energy density. In principle, such a field could produce a Schwarzschild geometry with negative mass and therefore no event horizon. Our aim is to assess whether, once the dominant energy condition is abandoned, the fully coupled evolution of matter and geometry can dynamically generate or expose naked singularities, thereby probing the robustness of cosmic censorship. To this end, we perform high-accuracy numerical relativity simulations based on fourth-order finite-difference schemes. Starting from smooth, asymptotically flat initial data representing regular phantom scalar wave packets, we follow their fully nonlinear evolution through collapse or dispersion. While an ordinary (positive-energy) scalar field exhibits the standard Choptuik critical behavior at the threshold of black-hole formation, the phantom field displays qualitatively different dynamics. For all amplitudes considered, we find no evidence for trapped surfaces, naked singularities, or alternative stationary end states. Instead, the phantom scalar field always disperses, suggesting that cosmic censorship remains dynamically preserved even in the presence of negative-energy matter.

</details>

### [53] [Reheating with Axion-SU(2) and Gravitational Chern-Simons Couplings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12339)
*Tatsuya Daniel,Vahid Kamali*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究分析了暴胀子加旁观轴子-SU(2)系统中振荡再加热早期阶段，包含轴子-规范Chern-Simons耦合和引力Chern-Simons耦合，发现引力Chern-Simons项导致张量功率谱的手征增强，可能产生窄带随机引力波特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索暴胀子加旁观轴子-SU(2)系统中振荡再加热早期阶段的物理过程，特别关注轴子-规范Chern-Simons耦合 $χF\tilde{F}$ 和引力Chern-Simons耦合 $χR\tilde{R}$ 的共同作用对张量扰动的影响。

Method: 采用各向同性SU(2)背景配置的色自然型（chromo-natural type）和二次势能，在再加热的第一个e-fold期间数值求解耦合的背景和张量扰动方程，分析引力Chern-Simons项对张量动力学系数的修正效应。

Result: 引力Chern-Simons项诱导了张量动力学系数的螺旋度依赖修正，导致张量功率谱的手征增强（chiral enhancement），在代表性基准下增强幅度约为数十个百分点，这种早期增强可能映射为现今随机引力波谱中的窄带特征。

Conclusion: 引力Chern-Simons耦合在再加热早期阶段能显著增强张量扰动，产生可观测的窄带引力波特征，但峰值尺度的完全自洽确定需要扫描共动波数并指定再加热历史，这对未来空间探测器的观测具有潜在意义。

Abstract: We study the early stages of an oscillatory reheating phase in an inflaton plus spectator axion-SU(2) system, including both an axion-gauge Chern-Simons coupling $χF\tilde{F}$ and a gravitational Chern-Simons coupling $χR\tilde{R}$. Assuming an isotropic SU(2) background configuration of chromo-natural type and quadratic potentials, we numerically solve the coupled background and tensor perturbation equations during the first e-fold of reheating. The gravitational Chern-Simons term induces a helicity-dependent modification of the tensor kinetic coefficient, yielding a chiral enhancement of the tensor power spectrum on the order of tens of percent for a representative benchmark. We illustrate how such an early-time enhancement can map to a narrow feature in the present-day stochastic gravitational wave spectrum, potentially relevant for upcoming and proposed space-based detectors, while a fully self-consistent determination of the peak scale requires scanning comoving wavenumbers and specifying the reheating history.

</details>


### [54] [Sound Speed Resonance in the Gravitational Wave Background as a probe for non-standard early universe cosmologies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12580)
*Igor de O. C. Pedreira,Amara Ilyas,Ziwei Wang,Leila L. Graef,Yi-Fu Cai*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该论文探讨了引力波（gravitational waves）如何作为探测基础引力理论的有力工具，特别是在广义相对论（general relativity）扩展理论中，标量场（scalar fields）等额外自由度可能通过改变有效摩擦项和传播速度来修改引力波传播，从而可能产生共振现象，增强原始张量模（primordial tensor modes）的背景信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波是探测基础引力理论的有力探针。在广义相对论的扩展理论中，引力扇区（gravitational sector）的标量场等额外自由度可能通过改变有效摩擦项（effective friction term）和传播速度来修改引力波传播，这些修改可能引发共振现象，在引力波谱中产生独特特征。

Method: 论文分析原始宇宙信号如何在标量场修改引力波传播的场景中产生共振。研究重点在于共振是否足够强大，能将原始张量模的背景增强到LISA或爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein telescope）等未来引力波探测器可探测的水平。

Result: 谱背景引力波（SBGW spectrum）中的特征峰取决于共振模型的参数以及原始张量谱的参数，如张标比$r$和张量谱指数$n_t$。这些共振效应为探索极早期宇宙物理开辟了有力途径，能将原本微弱的信号放大到实验可探测水平。

Conclusion: 共振效应使得原始宇宙信号能够被放大到实验可探测范围，从而将早期宇宙物理学带入实验可及领域。这种放大机制为通过引力波观测探索极早期宇宙物理提供了新的可能性。

Abstract: Gravitational waves constitute a powerful probe of the underlying theory of gravity. In extensions of general relativity, additional degrees of freedom, such as scalar fields in the gravitational sector, can modify their propagation through changes in the effective friction term and propagation speed. These modifications may potentially induce resonant phenomena leading to distinctive signatures in the gravitational wave spectrum. One important aspect to be investigated is whether the resonances can be strong enough to enhance the underlying background of primordial tensor modes to levels detectable by upcoming gravitational wave detectors, such as LISA or the Einstein telescope. The characteristic peaks in the SBGW spectrum depend on the parameters of the resonant model as well as on the parameters of the primordial tensor spectrum, such as $r$ and $n_{t}$. Thus these resonance effects open a powerful pathway to explore physics of the very early Universe by amplifying otherwise feeble signals to experimentally detectable levels. Here we analyze how the signals of the primordial Universe can resonate in these scenarios, bringing the early universe physics into the realm of experimental access.

</details>


### [55] [A unified harmonic framework for dark siren cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13053)
*April Qiu Cheng,Jonathan Gair*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种利用引力波（GW）与星系交叉相关（cross-correlation）进行宇宙学推断的暗警报（dark siren）方法，无需电磁对应体，通过统计边际化潜在宿主星系，结合谱警报（spectral sirens）方法，可在下一代探测器上实现高精度宇宙学参数测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统暗警报方法通过统计边际化潜在宿主星系推断宇宙学参数，而交叉相关方法利用两点统计（2-point statistics）无需观测宿主星系，提供更高效的推断途径。该方法旨在解决传统群体推断（population inference）技术在下一代引力波实验中扩展性不足的问题。

Method: 该方法将引力波与星系交叉相关作为星系目录（galaxy catalog）方法的扩展，有效边际化未知星系场的所有可能实现，并联合星系-星系聚类（galaxy-galaxy clustering）信息。结合谱警报方法（编码引力波率演化、质量分布和选择效应信息），并开发了将引力波测量误差严格纳入似然函数的策略。

Result: 研究表明，在2台爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein Telescope）+1台宇宙探索者（Cosmic Explorer）配置下，仅引力波-星系交叉相关部分就可在2年数据内将哈勃常数（H₀）和物质密度参数（Ω_{m,0}）分别测量至1%和5%精度。该方法在下一代探测器上线前受限于大数统计（large-number statistics）要求。

Conclusion: 引力波-星系交叉相关方法是一种精确且可扩展的推断技术，特别适用于下一代引力波和星系巡天。与传统群体推断技术相比，该方法能更好地适应下一代实验的精度和目录规模要求，但需要等待下一代探测器上线才能充分发挥潜力。

Abstract: The galaxy catalog dark siren method aims to infer cosmological parameters from gravitational waves (GWs) without an electromagnetic counterpart by statistically marginalizing over possible host galaxies. The cross-correlation of GW sources and galaxies is a promising avenue for cosmological inference without requiring observed host galaxies, by leveraging 2-point statistics. We provide a detailed guide to the cross-correlation method, clarifying its relationship to standard dark siren techniques as well as the assumptions necessary to be able to use this formalism on GW data. We show that the cross-correlation method is an extension of the angular part of the galaxy catalog method in which we effectively marginalize over all possible realizations of the unknown galaxy field, jointly adding information from galaxy--galaxy clustering. Combined with the spectral sirens method, which encodes information from the GW rate evolution, mass distribution, and selection effects, one can perform an inference that leverages the joint constraining power of all dark siren methods. We also present a strategy to rigorously fold GW measurement errors into the likelihood. Using this method, we show that with a 2 Einstein Telescope + 1 Cosmic Explorer setup, the GW--galaxy cross-correlation part alone can jointly measure $H_0$ and $Ω_{m,0}$ to 1\% and 5\% precision with just 2 years of data, demonstrating its potential as a precise and scalable inference technique in the next generation of GW and galaxy surveys. This is in contrast with canonical population inference techniques, which are known to scale poorly with the precision and catalog size expected of next-generation GW experiments. Contrary to some previous projections, we remain pessimistic about the cross-correlation method until these next generation detectors are online, due to its implicit requirement of large-number statistics.

</details>


### [56] [Three-band dark-siren cosmology with intermediate-mass black hole binaries: synergy of Taiji, LGWA, and Einstein Telescope](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13080)
*Ji-Yu Song,Yue-Yan Dong,Shang-Jie Jin,Si-Ren Xiao,Jing-Fei Zhang,Xin Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究评估了三波段引力波探测器网络（Taiji、LGWA、ET）对中等质量黑洞双星（IMBHBs）的宇宙学约束能力。研究发现该网络在ΛCDM模型中对哈勃常数和物质密度的约束分别达到~0.12%和~0.6%，在wCDM模型中对暗能量状态方程参数w的约束达到~2.7%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波暗警报（GW dark sirens）为宇宙膨胀历史提供了独立探测手段，但其宇宙学约束能力严重依赖于精确的光度距离测量和天区定位，以便与星系目录进行交叉匹配。多波段引力波观测能够追踪不同频段的引力波事件，从而改善这两个关键参数。

Method: 研究采用包含Taiji（TJ）、月球引力波天线（LGWA）和爱因斯坦望远镜（ET）的三波段引力波探测器网络，模拟可探测的中等质量黑洞双星（IMBHBs）群体。使用分层贝叶斯暗警报框架进行分析，该框架考虑了星系目录完整性和红移不确定性。

Result: TJ-LGWA-ET网络在所有考虑的双探测器配置中表现最佳。在ΛCDM模型中，对哈勃常数（Hubble constant）和物质密度（matter density）的约束分别达到~0.12%和~0.6%。在wCDM模型中，仅4年暗警报样本就能将暗能量状态方程参数w约束到~2.7%。加入重子声学振荡（BAO）和Ia型超新星（SNe Ia）数据后，w的约束改进到~2.1%，略优于当前的CMB+BAO+SNe Ia组合。

Conclusion: 最终约束结果对IMBHB群体假设和星系目录限制保持敏感，这突显了需要具有精确红移测量的深度星系巡天。多波段引力波观测网络在宇宙学参数约束方面具有显著潜力，但需要更完善的星系目录支持。

Abstract: Gravitational-wave (GW) dark sirens provide an independent probe of the cosmic expansion history. Their cosmological constraining power, however, depends critically on precise luminosity-distance measurements and sky localizations for cross-matching with galaxy catalogs. Multiband GW observations can track GW events across different frequency bands and thus improve both. Motivated by this, we forecast the cosmological potential of intermediate-mass black hole binaries (IMBHBs) observed by a three-band GW detector network composed of Taiji (TJ), the Lunar Gravitational-wave Antenna (LGWA), and the Einstein Telescope (ET). We simulate detectable IMBHB populations and analyze them with a hierarchical Bayesian dark-siren framework that includes galaxy-catalog completeness and redshift uncertainties. We find that the TJ-LGWA-ET network outperforms all two-detector configurations considered here. In the $Λ$CDM model, it constrains the Hubble constant and matter density to $\sim 0.12\%$ and $\sim 0.6\%$, respectively. In the $w$CDM model, a 4-year dark-siren sample alone constrains the dark-energy equation-of-state parameter $w$ to $\sim 2.7\%$. Adding baryon acoustic oscillation (BAO) and Type Ia supernova (SNe Ia) data improves the $w$ constraint to $\sim 2.1\%$, slightly better than that from the current CMB+BAO+SNe Ia combination. We also show that the final constraints remain sensitive to IMBHB population assumptions and galaxy-catalog limitations, which highlights the need for deep galaxy surveys with precise redshift measurements.

</details>


### [57] [Negative Masses and Spatial Curvature: Alleviating Neutrino Mass Tensions in LambdaCDM and Extended Cosmologies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13208)
*Hayyim Pulido-Hernández,Jorge L. Cervantes-Cota*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了空间曲率（Ω_k）和动力学暗能量对中微子质量总和（∑m_ν）宇宙学约束的影响。通过联合分析最新宇宙微波背景辐射（CMB）、重子声波振荡（BAO）和Ia型超新星（SNe Ia）数据，发现包含空间曲率显著改变了后验分布，并减少了与地面实验下限的张力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前宇宙学对中微子质量总和（∑m_ν）的约束可能受到边界效应和几何简并性的显著影响。研究旨在量化空间曲率（Ω_k）和动力学暗能量参数如何改变这些约束，特别是考虑到物理边界附近的先验驱动偏差问题。

Method: 采用联合分析方法，整合了最新的宇宙微波背景辐射（CMB，包括Planck和ACT DR6）、重子声波振荡（BAO，DESI DR2）和Ia型超新星（SNe Ia，DESY5和DES-Dovekie）数据集。为减轻物理边界附近的先验驱动偏差，实施了允许有效负质量的对称扩展包装器。

Result: 在ΛCDM + Ω_k + ∑m_{ν,eff}框架下，得到∑m_{ν,eff} = -0.011^{+0.052}_{-0.050} eV，与地面实验下限0.06 eV的张力从ΛCDM + ∑m_{ν,eff}模型的2.59σ降至1.17σ。在最灵活的w_0 w_a CDM + Ω_k + ∑m_{ν,eff}场景中，∑m_{ν,eff} = -0.07 ± 0.11 eV，张力为1.13σ，但参数自由度增加显著降低了质量估计的精度。

Conclusion: 当前宇宙学对中微子质量总和（∑m_ν）的约束受到边界效应和几何简并性的严重影响。包含空间曲率显著改变了后验分布，并减少了与实验下限的张力，而增加参数自由度会降低质量约束的精度。

Abstract: We investigate the impact of spatial curvature, $Ω_k$, and dynamical dark energy on the cosmological constraints of the neutrino mass sum, $\sum m_ν$. Using a joint analysis of the latest CMB (Planck and ACT DR6), BAO (DESI DR2) and SNe Ia (DESY5 and DES-Dovekie) datasets, we perform an exploration of the neutrino mass parameter space. To mitigate prior-driven biases near the physical boundary, we implement a symmetric extension wrapper that allows for effective negative masses. We find that the inclusion of spatial curvature significantly modifies the posterior distributions, exhibiting a smooth transition across the $\sum m_ν= 0$ threshold. In the $Λ$CDM + $Ω_k$ + $\sum m_{ν,\mathrm{eff}}$ framework, we obtain $\sum m_{ν,\mathrm{eff}} = -0.011^{+0.052}_{-0.050}$, reducing the tension with the terrestrial lower limit of 0.06 eV from $2.59σ$ for the $Λ$CDM + $\sum m_{ν,\mathrm{eff}}$ model to $1.17σ$. For the most flexible scenario $w_0 w_a$CDM + $Ω_k$ + $\sum m_{ν,\mathrm{eff}}$, we find $\sum m_{ν,\mathrm{eff}} = -0.07 \pm 0.11$ with a tension of $1.13σ$, illustrating how the increased parameter freedom notably degrades the precision of the mass estimate compared to simpler extensions. Our results demonstrate that current cosmological bounds on $\sum m_ν$ are heavily influenced by boundary effects and geometric degeneracies.

</details>

### [58] [Determinantal formulas for Sklyanin-Whittaker integrals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12438)
*Taro Kimura*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了多变量积分（称为Sklyanin-Whittaker积分），证明了其行列式公式，并讨论了q-变形、行列式点过程及相关Mellin-Barnes积分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在研究一类特定的多变量积分，即Sklyanin-Whittaker积分，这类积分在数学物理中具有重要性，需要建立其精确的计算公式。

Method: 通过数学分析方法，作者证明了Sklyanin-Whittaker积分的行列式公式（determinantal formulas），并进一步探讨了其q-变形（q-deformation）和相关的行列式点过程（determinantal point process）。

Result: 主要成果是建立了Sklyanin-Whittaker积分的行列式公式，并成功将其推广到q-变形版本，同时关联到行列式点过程和Mellin-Barnes积分。

Conclusion: 该研究为Sklyanin-Whittaker积分提供了系统的行列式表示，建立了与q-变形、点过程和特殊函数理论之间的联系，为相关数学物理问题的进一步研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: We study multi-variable integrals, that we name Sklyanin-Whittaker integrals, and prove their determinantal formulas. We also discuss a $q$-deformation, a determinantal point process, and associated Mellin--Barnes integrals.

</details>


### [59] [The Lee-Huang-Yang energy for a dilute gas of hard spheres: an upper bound](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13084)
*Giulia Basti,Morris Brooks,Serena Cenatiempo,Alessandro Olgiati,Benjamin Schlein*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究推导了硬球玻色气体在稀薄极限下基态能量密度的上界，与著名的Lee-Huang-Yang公式在低阶项上匹配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究硬球玻色气体在热力学极限下的基态能量密度，特别关注稀薄极限（$ρ\frak{a}^3 \ll 1$）下的精确行为，旨在验证Lee-Huang-Yang公式的准确性。

Method: 考虑由$N$个半径为$\frak{a} > 0$的硬球组成的量子气体，服从玻色统计，在具有周期性边界条件的盒子$Λ= [0;L]^3$中运动。在热力学极限下（$N, L \to \infty$，固定密度$ρ= N / L^3$）分析基态能量密度。

Result: 推导出基态能量密度的上界，该上界在稀薄极限下与著名的Lee-Huang-Yang公式匹配，仅相差低阶项。

Conclusion: 该研究为硬球玻色气体在稀薄极限下的基态能量密度提供了严格的上界估计，支持了Lee-Huang-Yang公式的理论预测。

Abstract: We consider a quantum gas consisting of $N$ hard spheres with radius $\frak{a} > 0$, obeying bosonic statistics and moving in the box $Λ= [0;L]^3$ with periodic boundary conditions. We are interested in the ground state energy per unit volume in the thermodynamic limit, with $N, L \to \infty$ at fixed density $ρ= N / L^3$. We derive an upper bound for the ground state energy density, matching the famous Lee-Huang-Yang formula, up to lower order terms, in the dilute limit $ρ\frak{a}^3 \ll 1$.

</details>


### [60] [Robust symmetry breaking in gapless quantum magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13212)
*Chao Yin,Andrew Lucas*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究证明了在某些无能隙（gapless）和受挫（frustrated）多体量子系统中，低能本征态存在自发对称性破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking），特别是对经典模型进行对称量子微扰的情况。研究还提供了随机键伊辛模型（random-bond Ising models）中稳健铁磁性的新证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于建立无能隙量子系统中自发对称性破缺的严格理论框架。当前对稳定无能隙量子相（gapless quantum phases）的严格分类仍处于初步阶段，需要发展新的数学工具来理解这些系统中的对称性破缺现象。

Method: 研究方法基于建立量子瓶颈（quantum bottlenecks），类似于评估隧穿速率的"多体WKB"方法。该方法适用于满足量子类比皮尔斯条件（Peierls condition）的非局域经典模型的对称量子微扰系统。

Result: 研究证明了在二维随机键伊辛模型中，当随机耦合足够偏置且存在弱横向场时，系统表现出稳健的铁磁性（robust ferromagnetism）。同时提供了无能隙亚稳态（gapless metastable states）中虚假真空缓慢衰变的新证明。

Conclusion: 该工作代表了向严格分类稳定无能隙量子相迈出的第一步。发展的量子瓶颈方法为理解无能隙系统中自发对称性破缺和亚稳态行为提供了新的数学框架。

Abstract: We prove the existence of spontaneous symmetry breaking in suitably low-energy eigenstates of certain gapless and frustrated many-body quantum systems, namely symmetric quantum perturbations to classical models which exhibit spontaneous symmetry breaking of a finite group at some positive temperature. Additionally, the classical model need not be local in space, as long as it satisfies a quantum analogue of the Peierls condition. As an example of our technique, we establish robust ferromagnetism in random-bond Ising models in $d= 2$ dimensions with sufficiently biased random couplings, with weak transverse field. Our mathematical technique is based on establishing quantum bottlenecks, similar to a "many-body WKB" method for evaluating tunneling rates. Using these same methods, we provide new proofs of metastability and the slow decay of the false vacuum, applicable to gapless metastable states. Our work represents a first step towards a rigorous classification of stable gapless quantum phases.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在深入理解$B^+ \to K^+μ^+μ^-$衰变中的局域（local）和非局域（nonlocal）振幅贡献，特别是区分短程和长程相互作用对衰变过程的影响。

Method: 基于LHCb实验收集的8.4fb$^{-1}$积分亮度$pp$对撞数据，采用描述单粒子和双粒子非局域振幅的模型，对双μ子质量谱进行全面的振幅分析。

Result: 威尔逊系数组合$C_9+C_9'$和$C_{10}+C_{10}'$与标准模型预测的兼容性在$1.6\,σ$到$4\,σ$之间变化，具体取决于局域形状因子（local form factors）的选择。

Conclusion: 该研究实现了对$B^+ \to K^+μ^+μ^-$衰变中短程和长程贡献的联合测定，为检验标准模型和寻找新物理提供了重要约束。

Abstract: This paper presents a thorough study of the local and nonlocal amplitudes in $B^+ \to K^+μ^+μ^-$ transitions through an amplitude analysis of the dimuon mass spectrum of the decay. The analysis is based on $pp$ collision data corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 8.4fb$^{-1}$ collected by the LHCb experiment. This measurement employs a model that describes both one-particle and two-particle nonlocal amplitudes across the entirety of the dimuon mass spectrum, enabling the determination of both short- and long-distance contributions to the decay. The compatibility of the Wilson coefficient combinations $C_9+C_9'$ and $C_{10}+C_{10}'$ with the Standard Model prediction is found to vary between $1.6\,σ$ and $4\,σ$, depending on the choice of local form factors.

### [62] [Experimental aspects of the Quantum Tomography of tau lepton pairs at a Higgs factory collider](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12609)
*Daniel Jeans*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种在电子-正电子希格斯工厂（Higgs factory）对撞机上完全重建τ轻子对（tau lepton pairs）运动学的方法，通过测量粒子动量和碰撞参数来优化τ子自旋（spin）方向的提取，并评估了探测器性能对重建精度的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在希格斯工厂对撞机中产生的τ轻子对的自旋关联（spin correlations）源于量子纠缠（quantum entanglement），测量这些关联需要准确重建τ子的自旋分量及其相关性，这依赖于完全的运动学重建能力。

Method: 提出了一种利用测量粒子的动量（momenta）和碰撞参数（impact parameters）在电子-正电子希格斯工厂对撞机上完全重建τ轻子对事件运动学的方法。该方法为每个事件生成多个一致解，可根据不同事件属性分配权重，从而通过极化计（polarimeters）实现τ子自旋方向的最优提取。

Result: 在理想探测器条件下估算了极化计的重建精度，并量化了更实际探测器性能的影响。分析表明，实现约1毫弧度（mrad）的光子角分辨率（photon angular resolution）是探测器性能最关键的因素，而光子能量分辨率（photon energy resolution）和顶点探测器（vertex detector）性能的重要性显著较低。

Conclusion: 对于τ轻子对自旋关联的量子层析（quantum tomography）分析，探测器设计的首要目标应是实现约1毫弧度的光子角分辨率，这一要求比光子能量分辨率和顶点探测器性能更为关键。

Abstract: Quantum Tomography of tau lepton pairs produced at a Higgs Factory collider will enable measurements of their spin correlations arising from quantum entanglement. Such measurements rely on the ability to measure the components of and correlations between the taus' spins. We present a method to fully reconstruct the kinematics of tau pair events at an electron-positron Higgs factory collider, making use of measured particles' momenta and impact parameters. This procedure results in several consistent solutions per event, which can be assigned weights according to various event properties. Full kinematic reconstruction allows the optimal extraction of the taus' spin orientation via polarimeters. We estimate the precision with which polarimeters can be reconstructed in an ideal detector, and quantify the effects of more realistic detector performance. We conclude that for this analysis, achieving a photon angular resolution of around 1~mrad is the most crucial aspect of detector performance, while photon energy resolution and vertex detector performance are significantly less important.

</details>


### [63] [First results from LEGEND-200: searching for $0νββ$ decay in $^{76}$Ge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12884)
*Giovanna Saleh*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: LEGEND实验通过富集锗-76探测器搜索无中微子双β衰变（0νββ）。LEGEND-200已完成首年数据采集，未发现信号，设定了半衰期下限。联合分析进一步提高了灵敏度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在通过LEGEND实验搜索锗-76（⁷⁶Ge）的无中微子双β衰变（neutrinoless double beta decay, 0νββ），以探索中微子是否为马约拉纳粒子（Majorana particle）及轻子数守恒问题。

Method: 实验采用富集度超过86%的高纯度锗-76（⁷⁶Ge）活性探测器，分两阶段进行：LEGEND-200（已运行）和LEGEND-1000（下一代）。LEGEND-200在格兰萨索国家实验室（LNGS）运行，使用142.5公斤探测器，目标背景指数为2×10⁻⁴ counts/(keV kg yr)。

Result: 首年数据分析未发现0νββ信号，设定了90%置信水平下半衰期下限T₁/₂⁰ν > 0.5×10²⁶年。联合GERDA、MAJORANA Demonstrator和LEGEND-200数据的分析将下限提高至T₁/₂⁰ν > 1.9×10²⁶年（90% CL）。

Conclusion: LEGEND-200已成功运行并完成首年数据分析，为无中微子双β衰变研究提供了重要约束。实验将继续积累数据，目标是通过1000 kg·yr曝光量达到10²⁷年半衰期的3σ发现灵敏度。

Abstract: The LEGEND Experiment searches for the neutrinoless double beta (0$νββ$) decay of $^{76}$Ge employing active high purity germanium detectors enriched in $^{76}$Ge beyond 86%. LEGEND's experimental program is articulated in two phases: LEGEND-200, currently ongoing, and LEGEND-1000, the next generation development. LEGEND-200 started operating in 2023 at Laboratori Nazionali del Gran Sasso (LNGS) and ran in a stable physics data taking regime for about one year with 142.5 kg of detectors installed. With a target background index of $2 \cdot 10^{-4} $ counts/(keV kg yr) at Q$_{ββ} \sim$ 2039 keV and a final exposure of 1000 kg yr, LEGEND-200 aims to reach a 3$σ$ discovery sensitivity for a 0$νββ$ half-life of $10^{27}$ yr. In this contribution, the LEGEND-200 experiment will be presented, with a focus on its current status and on the results obtained with the first year of data. In particular, the employed analysis routines will be introduced, the signal identification and background suppression performance will be discussed, and the background appearing in the region of interest around $Q_{ββ}$ will be analyzed. The performed analysis of LEGEND-200 data finds no evidence for a 0$νββ$ signal: a lower limit to its half-life is set instead, $T_{1/2}^{0ν} > 0.5 \cdot 10^{26}$ yr, at 90% CL. A joint GERDA + MAJORANA Demonstrator + LEGEND-200 analysis provides a limit of $T_{1/2}^{0ν} > 1.9 \cdot 10^{26}$ yr, at 90% CL.
  This work is supported by the U.S. DOE and the NSF, the LANL, ORNL and LBNL LDRD programs; the European ERC and Horizon programs; the German DFG, BMBF, and MPG; the Italian INFN; the Polish NCN and MNiSW; the Czech MEYS; the Slovak RDA; the Swiss SNF; the UK STFC; the Canadian NSERC and CFI; the LNGS and SURF facilities.

### [64] [Dispersive analysis of the $π^+ π^-$ production at the CMD3 experiment and the compatibility with muon pair production measurement by KLOE2 and the pion form factor by JLAB](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12929)
*Dimitrios Petrellis,Vladimir Sauli*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究基于两组数据集提取了带电π介子形状因子（charged pion form factor）的谱函数，分析了CMD3数据与其他测量结果的兼容性问题，并利用提取的π介子谱函数计算了QED跑动电荷（QED running charge）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于分析CMD3实验测量的π⁺π⁻产生数据与其他近期测量结果的兼容性差异，并探讨这些差异对解析延拓到类空间区域（spacelike region）的影响，同时利用π介子谱函数研究量子电动力学（QED）跑动电荷。

Method: 方法包括：1）从两组数据集（包含与不包含CMD3数据）提取带电π介子形状因子的谱函数；2）通过色散关系（dispersion relation）从e⁺e⁻碰撞中的排他性强子产生过程提取强子真空极化（hadronic vacuum polarization）；3）将结果与JLaB-π实验的类空间π介子形状因子以及KLOE2实验的辐射返回μ⁻μ⁺产生数据进行对比。

Result: 研究发现：1）CMD3数据与其他近期测量结果存在显著不兼容性；2）然而，当用于解析延拓到类空间区域时，CMD3数据并未提供额外贡献；3）提取的π介子谱函数用于计算QED跑动电荷，并与KLOE2实验在ω/ρ介子能量处的辐射返回μ⁻μ⁺产生数据进行了比较。

Conclusion: 结论表明：1）CMD3数据与JLaB-π实验获得的类空间π介子形状因子存在不兼容性证据；2）尽管CMD3数据与其他测量存在差异，但在解析延拓到类空间区域时未产生额外效应；3）通过π介子谱函数获得的QED跑动电荷为相关实验比较提供了参考基准。

Abstract: The spectral function of the charged pion form factor was extracted from two data sets. The difference between the two sets is based on the presence or absence of the recent measurement of the $π^+ π^-$ production by CMD3. Although the CMD3 data are largely incompatible with other recent measurements, it was found to provide no excess when used for analytical continuation to spacelike region. Consequently, there is evidence for incompatibility when it is compared to the spacelike pion form factor obtained by the JLaB-$π$ experiment. Furthermore, the extracted pionic spectral function was used to obtain the QED running charge. It was then compared with the KLOE2 experiment for radiative return $μ^{-}μ^{+}$ production at $ ω/ρ$ meson energy.
  For this purpose the hadronic vacuum polarization has been extracted from exclusive hadronic productions in $e^+e^-$ collisions via the dispersion relation using combined data with and without the CMD3 data set included in.

### [65] [Recent electroweak measurements from the CMS experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12961)
*Cristina-Andreea Alexe*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: CMS实验在大型强子对撞机（LHC）上对电弱物理进行了精确测量，包括W/Z玻色子产生截面、Drell-Yan过程前后不对称性、有效轻子电弱混合角等，部分测量精度达到甚至超越了传统轻子对撞机的结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在通过CMS实验在高达13.6 TeV质心能量下的质子-质子对撞中，对粒子物理标准模型（Standard Model）的关键电弱参数和过程进行精确测试，验证标准模型的预测并探索可能的偏差。

Method: 研究采用CMS实验装置在大型强子对撞机（Large Hadron Collider, LHC）上收集的质子-质子对撞数据，通过精确测量电弱过程的关键观测量来测试标准模型。测量包括W/Z玻色子产生截面、Drell-Yan过程前后不对称性（forward-backward asymmetry）、有效轻子电弱混合角（effective leptonic electroweak mixing angle）、τ轻子性质以及多玻色子产生和矢量玻色子散射率。

Result: CMS实验在电弱物理研究中发挥了关键作用，多项测量首次在质子-质子对撞机上实现或达到最佳精度。部分测量精度达到甚至超越了传统轻子对撞机（lepton colliders）的遗留结果，为电弱相互作用的精确测试提供了重要数据。

Conclusion: CMS实验在高达13.6 TeV的质心能量下对电弱物理进行了精确测量，验证了标准模型的预测。这些高精度测量不仅确认了标准模型的有效性，也为未来发现可能的物理新现象奠定了基础。

Abstract: Recent measurements of electroweak phenomena from the Compact Muon Solenoid (CMS) experiment at the Large Hadron Collider are summarized. The standard model of particle physics was tested through highly precise determinations of its key electroweak parameters and through measurements of electroweak processes in proton-proton collisions at unprecedented center-of-mass energies of up to $13.6 \, \mathrm{TeV}$. The performance of the CMS experiment establishes its key role in the study of electroweak physics, with many measurements performed either for the first time or with the best precision at a proton-proton collider, in some cases reaching or even surpassing the precision of legacy results from lepton colliders. Recent electroweak results from the CMS experiment include: measurements of the W and Z bosons production cross sections; high-precision measurements of the forward-backward asymmetry in Drell-Yan production and of the effective leptonic electroweak mixing angle; measurements of tau lepton properties and of multiboson production and vector boson scattering rates.

### [66] [Search for Higgs boson pair production in association with top-quark pairs using 196 fb$^{-1}$ of proton-proton collision data at $\sqrt{s}=$ 13 and 13.6 TeV with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13113)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该论文首次在ATLAS探测器上搜索了与顶夸克对（$t\bar{t}HH$）相关的非共振希格斯玻色子对产生过程，基于196 fb$^{-1}$的质子-质子碰撞数据，测量了相对于标准模型预测的截面比$μ_{t\bar{t}HH}=-3^{+11}_{-12}$，并给出了希格斯有效场论威尔逊系数$c_{t\bar{t}HH}$的约束范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在首次搜索与顶夸克对相关的非共振希格斯玻色子对产生过程（$t\bar{t}HH$），这是对希格斯玻色子性质及其与顶夸克耦合的重要测试。通过测量这一稀有过程，可以检验标准模型（Standard Model）预测并约束超出标准模型（Beyond Standard Model）的新物理效应。

Method: 研究使用ATLAS探测器在大型强子对撞机（Large Hadron Collider）收集的质子-质子碰撞数据，对应196 fb$^{-1}$的积分亮度。分析针对$t\bar{t}HH$衰变预期的三个不同终态：单轻子（electron or muon）加至少五个b夸克、至少两个b夸克加同号电荷双轻子或多轻子、以及至少三个b夸克加双光子。

Result: 测量得到$t\bar{t}HH$产生截面相对于标准模型预测的比值为$μ_{t\bar{t}HH}=-3^{+11}_{-12}$，对应95%置信水平（confidence-level）的上限为标准模型预测的20倍。同时将希格斯有效场论（Higgs effective field theory）的威尔逊系数（Wilson coefficient）$c_{t\bar{t}HH}$约束在$-3.9<c_{t\bar{t}HH}<3.3$范围内。

Conclusion: 该研究首次对$t\bar{t}HH$过程进行了实验搜索，未发现显著超出标准模型预期的信号。结果为希格斯玻色子对产生过程设定了新的约束，并为希格斯有效场论中的相关耦合参数提供了重要的实验限制。

Abstract: This paper presents the first search for non-resonant Higgs boson pair production in association with a top-quark pair ($t\bar{t}HH$) using proton-proton collision data collected with the ATLAS detector at the Large Hadron Collider. The data sample corresponds to an integrated luminosity of 196 fb$^{-1}$, comprising 140 fb$^{-1}$ at a centre-of-mass energy of $\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV and 56 fb$^{-1}$ at 13.6 TeV. The search targets three distinct final states expected from $t\bar{t}HH$ decays: (i) one lepton (electron or muon) with at least five $b$-quarks, (ii) at least two $b$-quarks accompanied by two leptons with the same electric charges or multiple leptons, and (iii) at least three $b$-quarks with two photons. The $t\bar{t}HH$ production cross-section, relative to its Standard Model prediction, is measured to be $μ_{t\bar{t}HH}=-3^{+11}_{-12}$. This result corresponds to a 95$\% $ confidence-level upper limit of 20 times the Standard Model prediction for the $t\bar{t}HH$ production cross-section, with an expected limit of 21. The Higgs effective field theory Wilson coefficient $c_{t\bar{t}HH}$ is also constrained at the same confidence level to the range of $-3.9<c_{t\bar{t}HH}<3.3$, compared with the expected range of $-4.0<c_{t\bar{t}HH}<3.5$.

</details>

Winn,W. Wislicki,M. Witek,L. Witola,T. Wolf,E. Wood,G. Wormser,S. A. Wotton,H. Wu,J. Wu,X. Wu,Y. Wu,Z. Wu,K. Wyllie,S. Xian,Z. Xiang,Y. Xie,T. X. Xing,A. Xu,L. Xu,M. Xu,R. Xu,Z. Xu,Z. Xu,Z. Xu,S. Yadav,K. Yang,X. Yang,Y. Yang,Y. Yang,Z. Yang,Z. Yang,H. Yeung,H. Yin,X. Yin,C. Y. Yu,J. Yu,X. Yuan,Y Yuan,J. A. Zamora Saa,M. Zavertyaev,M. Zdybal,F. Zenesini,C. Zeng,M. Zeng,S. H Zeng,C. Zhang,D. Zhang,J. Zhang,L. Zhang,R. Zhang,S. Zhang,S. L. Zhang,Y. Zhang,Y. Z. Zhang,Z. Zhang,Y. Zhao,A. Zhelezov,S. Z. Zheng,X. Z. Zheng,Y. Zheng,T. Zhou,X. Zhou,V. Zhovkovska,L. Z. Zhu,X. Zhu,X. Zhu,Y. Zhu,V. Zhukov,J. Zhuo,D. Zuliani,G. Zunica*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文对B^0→K_S^0μ^+μ^-衰变进行了风味标记的时间依赖分析，首次在b→sl^+l^-过程中实验研究了时间依赖的CP破坏（CP violation），结果与标准模型（Standard Model）预测一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在首次实验探索b→sl^+l^-过程中的时间依赖CP破坏现象，通过分析B^0→K_S^0μ^+μ^-衰变来检验标准模型预测。

Method: 采用风味标记（flavor-tagged）的时间依赖分析方法，覆盖除J/ψ和ψ(2S)共振区外的全双μ子质量范围，使用LHCb实验在2011-2018年收集的质子-质子（proton-proton）对撞数据，对应积分亮度为9fb^{-1}。

Result: 测得CP破坏参数C = -0.13 ± 0.32 ± 0.04和S = +0.82 ± 0.29 ± 0.05，其中第一项为统计误差，第二项为系统误差，结果与标准模型预测相符。

Conclusion: 这是首次在b→sl^+l^-过程中进行时间依赖CP破坏的实验研究，测得的结果与标准模型预测一致，为相关物理过程提供了重要实验约束。

Abstract: A flavor-tagged time-dependent analysis of $B^{0}\rightarrow K_{S}^{0}μ^{+}μ^{-}$ decays is performed across the full dimuon mass range excluding the $J/ψ$ and $ψ(2S)$ resonance regions. The analysis uses proton-proton collision data collected by the LHCb experiment in 2011--2018 at center-of-mass energies of 7, 8 and 13TeV, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 9$fb^{-1}$. The CP violation parameters are determined to be $C=-0.13 \pm 0.32 \pm 0.04$ and $S= +0.82\pm 0.29 \pm 0.05$, where the first uncertainties are statistical and the second are systematic.The results are consistent with the Standard Model prediction. This is the first experimental study of time-dependent CP violation in $b\rightarrow sl^{+}l^{-}$ processes.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.dis-nn'></div>

# cond-mat.dis-nn [[Back]](#toc)

### [68] [Pruning-induced phases in fully-connected neural networks: the eumentia, the dementia, and the amentia](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12316)
*Haining Pan,Nakul Aggarwal,J. H. Pixley*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究通过改变训练和评估阶段的dropout率，在MNIST数据集上训练的全连接神经网络中发现了三个相：正常相（eumentia）、遗忘相（dementia）和无学习能力相（amentia）。这些相通过交叉熵损失随训练数据集大小的幂律标度行为（power-law scaling）来区分，其中正常相表现出准长程有序（quasi-long-range order）特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然剪枝（pruning）作为压缩过参数化神经网络的关键方法已得到充分发展，但剪枝是否会在神经网络中引发尖锐相变（sharp phase transitions）以及这些相变属于何种普适类（universality class）仍是未解决的问题。研究旨在通过统计力学（statistical mechanics）视角理解神经网络行为。

Method: 研究在MNIST数据集上训练全连接神经网络，通过独立改变训练和评估阶段的dropout率（即移除神经元）来绘制相图（phase diagram）。该方法将dropout诱导的剪枝作为具体实验设置，分析不同网络宽度和深度下的相结构鲁棒性。

Result: 识别出三个截然不同的相：正常相（网络学习）、遗忘相（网络遗忘）和无学习能力相（网络无法学习）。正常相和遗忘相之间的转变伴随尺度不变性（scale invariance）和发散的长度尺度，表现出类似Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless转变的特征。相结构在不同网络宽度和深度下保持稳健。

Conclusion: dropout诱导的剪枝为通过统计力学视角理解神经网络行为提供了具体实验框架。研究证实神经网络中存在尖锐相变，并揭示了其普适类特征，将机器学习文献中的神经标度律（neural scaling laws）与统计力学中的准长程有序联系起来。

Abstract: Modern neural networks are heavily overparameterized, and pruning, which removes redundant neurons or connections, has emerged as a key approach to compressing them without sacrificing performance. However, while practical pruning methods are well developed, whether pruning induces sharp phase transitions in the neural networks and, if so, to what universality class they belong, remain open questions. To address this, we study fully-connected neural networks trained on MNIST, independently varying the dropout (i.e., removing neurons) rate at both the training and evaluation stages to map the phase diagram. We identify three distinct phases: eumentia (the network learns), dementia (the network has forgotten), and amentia (the network cannot learn), sharply distinguished by the power-law scaling of the cross-entropy loss with the training dataset size. {In the eumentia phase, the algebraic decay of the loss, as documented in the machine learning literature as neural scaling laws, is from the perspective of statistical mechanics the hallmark of quasi-long-range order.} We demonstrate that the transition between the eumentia and dementia phases is accompanied by scale invariance, with a diverging length scale that exhibits hallmarks of a Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless-like transition; the phase structure is robust across different network widths and depths. Our results establish that dropout-induced pruning provides a concrete setting in which neural network behavior can be understood through the lens of statistical mechanics.

</details>


### [69] [Continuous unitary transformations using tensor network representations access the full many-body localized spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12851)
*Qiyu Liu,Jan-Niklas Herre,Dante M. Kennes,Christoph Karrasch*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出变分连续幺正变换（VCUTs），将Wegner-Wilson流方程与张量网络技术结合，用于近似对角化多体局域化哈密顿量，可精确再现遍历-MBL交叉区的全谱并追踪对角化幺正算符的空间纠缠结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在开发一种能够近似对角化多体局域化（many-body localized, MBL）哈密顿量的方法，以研究遍历相到MBL相的交叉区域，并追踪对角化幺正算符的空间纠缠结构。

Method: 该方法整合了Wegner-Wilson流方程与张量网络技术，称为变分连续幺正变换（variational continuous unitary transformations, VCUTs）。对角化幺正算符被表示为矩阵乘积算符（matrix product operator），其键维数控制计算精度。

Result: 对于无序海森堡链，VCUTs在小系统尺寸下精确再现了遍历-MBL交叉区的全谱，并可扩展到L=48个格点。该方法还能追踪对角化幺正算符U(l)在每个流步骤中的空间纠缠结构，从而识别MBL相深处的局域运动积分。

Conclusion: VCUTs方法成功地将流方程与张量网络技术结合，为研究多体局域化系统提供了有效的数值工具，不仅能计算本征能谱，还能分析对角化幺正算符的纠缠结构特性。

Abstract: We develop variational continuous unitary transformations (VCUTs), which integrate Wegner-Wilson flow equations with tensor network techniques to approximately diagonalize many-body localized (MBL) Hamiltonians. The diagonalizing unitary is represented as a matrix product operator whose bond dimension controls the accuracy. For the disordered Heisenberg chain, VCUTs accurately reproduces the full spectrum across the ergodic-to-MBL crossover at small system sizes and scales to $L = 48$ sites. Beyond eigenenergies, the method can track the spatial entanglement structure of the diagonalizing unitary $U(l)$ at each flow step, enabling identification of local integrals of motion deep in the MBL phase.

</details>


### [70] [A toy model of a protein prototype reveals nontrivial ultrametricity of the energy landscape](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13012)
*A. Kh. Bikulov,A. P. Zubarev*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种研究无序异聚物能量景观超度量性的模型，通过GPU计算实验发现蛋白质序列的能量景观具有层次化组织特征，验证了Frauenfelder的蛋白质超度量性假说。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究无序异聚物能量景观的超度量性（ultrametricity），将其作为蛋白质分子的简化模型。研究动机源于验证Frauenfelder关于蛋白质超度量性的假说，并探索自旋玻璃模型类比在蛋白质能量景观研究中的应用。

Method: 采用无序异聚物模型作为蛋白质简化模型，氨基酸残基被建模为点质量。相互作用包括通用排斥、Lennard-Jones势、带屏蔽的库仑势以及相邻残基间的弹性势。借鉴自旋玻璃模型类比，应用副本理论方法，但不对无序进行平均。副本间的重叠定义为平均成对能量向量间的皮尔逊相关系数。在GPU上对128个残基长的序列进行模拟，每个序列采用50个独立无序实现和50个副本，温度T=1.0。

Result: 计算实验发现，90.0%的序列中副本间距离矩阵包含超过一半的超度量三角形，其中97.8%以非平凡超度量性为主，表明能量景观具有层次化组织。对选定序列的重复实验确认了观测的可靠性：95.5%的序列再次表现出超度量性，其中97.7%以非平凡超度量性为主。

Conclusion: 获得的结果证实了Frauenfelder的蛋白质超度量性假说，为在更现实的蛋白质模型中系统研究超度量性质奠定了基础。该方法展示了自旋玻璃理论框架在蛋白质能量景观分析中的适用性。

Abstract: A model for studying the ultrametricity of the energy landscape in a disordered heteropolymer is presented. It is treated as a simplified model of a protein molecule in which amino acid residues are modeled as point masses. Pairwise interactions include universal repulsion, the Lennard-Jones potential, the Coulomb potential with screening, and the elastic potential for bonds between adjacent residues. An analogy with spin glass models is used, allowing the application of replica theory methods. Unlike the standard approach to disordered systems, averaging over disorder is not performed. The overlap between replicas is defined as the Pearson correlation coefficient between the vectors of average pairwise energies, which corresponds to a comparison of thermodynamic averages in the spirit of spin glass theory. The results of a computational experiment conducted using the developed algorithm on a graphics processing unit (GPU) are presented. The simulations were performed using a 128-residue-long sequence, with 50 independent disorder realizations and 50 replicas for each sequence at a temperature of T = 1.0. It was found that for 90.0% of the sequences, the distance matrix between replicas contains more than half of the ultrametric triangles, and nontrivial ultrametricity predominates in 97.8% of them, indicating a hierarchical organization of the energy landscape. A repeated computational experiment for selected sequences confirms the reliability of the observations: 95.5% of them again demonstrated ultrametricity, of which 97.7% showed a predominance of the nontrivial type of ultrametricity. The obtained results confirm Frauenfelder's hypothesis of protein ultrametricity and pave the way for a systematic study of ultrametric properties in more realistic protein models.

### [71] [Reduced-Order Variational Deterministic-Particle-Based Scheme for Fokker-Planck Equations in Microscopic Polymer Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12550)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文开发了一个模型降阶框架，整合了本征正交分解（POD）来加速微观Fokker-Planck方程的VDS计算。该方法通过识别低维结构来显著减少自由度，从而提高计算效率。

Result: 数值验证使用简单剪切流中的珠-弹簧链模型，表明降阶模型的计算效率随分子复杂性系统性提高。对于4珠链聚合物，降阶模型仅引入约6%的相对误差，而计算时间仅需原模型的约6%，自由度可显著减少至原模型的约0.1%。

Conclusion: 该研究为多尺度和复杂流体模拟建立了实用途径。通过POD发现的低维结构使得在保持可接受精度的同时，显著提高计算效率成为可能。

Abstract: This study proposes an acceleration technique for the computational challenges in extending the variational deterministic-particle-based scheme (VDS) [Bao et al., Journal of Computational Physics 522 (2025) 113589] to 3D complex fluid simulations with multi-bead polymers.
  While the original VDS effectively captures configuration space dynamics for 2D dumbbell polymers, its direct extensions reveal critical scalability limitations. The growing configuration space dimensionality necessitates prohibitively large particle ensembles to maintain distributional accuracy, so its quadratic computational cost scaling impedes practical applications.
  In this paper, we develop a model reduction framework integrating proper orthogonal decomposition (POD) to speed up the computation of the VDS for microscopic Fokker-Planck equations.
  Numerical validation using bead-spring chain models in simple shear flow demonstrates that the computational efficiency of the reduced model increases systematically with molecular complexity.
  The reduced-order model introduces about $6\%$ relative error in predicting the dynamics while requiring only about $6\%$ of the original computational time for $4$-bead chain polymers, where the relative numerical error of the reference dynamics is about $5\% \sim 10\%$, and the degrees of freedom can be reduced significantly to about $0.1\%$ of the original model, which means the low-dimensional structure is found by POD.
  This establishes a practical pathway for multiscale and complex fluid simulations.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: QMatSuite平台让代理记录具有完整溯源性的发现，在新计算前检索知识，并在专门的反思会话中纠正错误发现，将观察结果合成为跨化合物模式。

Result: 在六步量子力学模拟工作流的基准测试中，积累的知识使推理开销减少了67%，准确度从47%偏差提升到3%偏差（相对于文献值）。当转移到不熟悉的材料时，实现了1%偏差且零管道失败。

Conclusion: QMatSuite通过系统性地积累和重用知识，将AI代理从单纯的计算执行者转变为能够进行渐进式知识积累的研究者，显著提升了计算材料科学的效率和准确性。

Abstract: While large language models (LLMs) have transformed AI agents into proficient executors of computational materials science, performing a hundred simulations does not make a researcher. What distinguishes research from routine execution is the progressive accumulation of knowledge -- learning which approaches fail, recognizing patterns across systems, and applying understanding to new problems. However, the prevailing paradigm in AI-driven computational science treats each execution in isolation, largely discarding hard-won insights between runs. Here we present QMatSuite, an open-source platform closing this gap. Agents record findings with full provenance, retrieve knowledge before new calculations, and in dedicated reflection sessions correct erroneous findings and synthesize observations into cross-compound patterns. In benchmarks on a six-step quantum-mechanical simulation workflow, accumulated knowledge reduces reasoning overhead by 67% and improves accuracy from 47% to 3% deviation from literature -- and when transferred to an unfamiliar material, achieves 1% deviation with zero pipeline failures.

### [73] [Excitonic Quantum Anomalous Hall Effect in Collinear Magnets Without Spin-Orbit Coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12280)
*Xingxing Liu,ChaoYang Tan,Peng-Jie Guo,Zhong-Yi Lu,Zheng-Xin Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种无需强自旋轨道耦合（SOC）的激子凝聚机制来实现量子反常霍尔（QAH）绝缘体，并通过第一性原理计算预测V2SeTeO双层材料是潜在的激子QAH绝缘体候选材料。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling, SOC）是实现磁性材料中量子反常霍尔（quantum anomalous Hall, QAH）绝缘体的必要条件。本研究旨在探索在自旋轨道耦合可忽略的共线磁体中实现QAH效应的新机制。

Method: 提出两步实现机制：首先制备具有自旋劈裂的节线环（nodal-ring）能带结构，然后通过三重态激子凝聚（triplet exciton condensation）打开节线环能隙。研究还表明电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling）能将自旋织构从共线模式转变为非共线模式。

Result: 当三重态激子凝聚产生的面内自旋织构在动量空间呈非共线分布时，可获得非零陈数（Chern number）。该机制不仅适用于铁磁体（ferromagnets），也适用于交变磁体（altermagnets）。通过第一性原理计算预测双层材料V2SeTeO是激子QAH绝缘体的有前景候选材料。

Conclusion: 研究证明了一种不依赖强自旋轨道耦合的新型激子凝聚机制可实现量子反常霍尔效应，为在更广泛的磁性材料体系中探索QAH绝缘体提供了新途径。

Abstract: Spin-orbit coupling (SOC) is thought to be necessary in realizing quantum anomalous Hall (QAH) insulators in magnetic materials. In this Letter, we propose an exciton-condensation mechanism to realize QAH effect in collinear magnets with negligible spin-orbit coupling. This mechanism is realized by two steps: first prepare a spin-splitting nodal-ring band structure, and then gap out the nodal-ring via triplet exciton condensation. A nonzero Chern number can be obtained if the in-plane spin texture resulting from the triplet exciton condensation is noncollinear in momentum space. We show that the electron-phonon coupling can switch the spin texture from a colinear pattern to a noncolinear one and plays an essential role in realizing QAH effect. The above mechanism is not only suitable for ferrogmagnets but also applicable for altermagnets. Finally, through first-principles calculations we propose the bilayer material V2SeTeO to be a promising candidate of excitonic QAH insulator.

Conclusion: 多层螺旋结构中的电子态存在从三维扩展到二维局域化的转变，这一现象可通过Aubry-André模型描述，并在输运实验中具有可观测的特征。

Abstract: We study the electronic properties of multilayer "spirals" of two-dimensional materials with continuously increasing twist angle. The electronic states are shown to undergo a universal 3D-to-2D transition on increasing the in-plane momentum ${\bf k}_\parallel$ away from the $Γ$ point. The states with $k_\parallel>k_c$ are localized along the z axis due to mismatch between electronic dispersions of the twisted layers, whereas those with $k_\parallel<k_c$ are extended. We support our results by mapping of the system on the Aubry-André model and deduce the experimental signatures of 3D to 2D localization in transport experiments.

### [76] [Annihilation of Dirac points and its topological obstruction in a photonic Kagome lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12467)
*Zhaoyang Zhang,Matthieu Finck,Changchang Li,Shun Liang,Jerome Dubois,Yumin Tian,Jiahao Wen,Yanpeng Zhang,Guillaume Malpuech,Dmitry Solnyshkov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究在原子蒸气中构建的光子Kagome晶格中，通过光学调控势能差移动狄拉克点（Dirac points），观测到狄拉克点碰撞时存在湮灭阻碍现象，并揭示了由本征态非阿贝尔框架旋转诱导的拓扑相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 狄拉克点（Dirac points）作为决定二维材料特殊性质的拓扑奇点，通常由离散拓扑不变量分类。本研究旨在探索狄拉克点在碰撞过程中的行为，特别是其湮灭（annihilation）的可能性与拓扑不变量变化之间的关系。

Method: 在原子蒸气中构建光子Kagome晶格（photonic Kagome lattice），通过光学工程调控构成Kagome晶胞的三个格点间的势能差，同时保持时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）和孤立狄拉克点的稳定性。采用锥形衍射（conical diffraction）测量狄拉克点位置和拓扑不变量（欧拉数，Euler number）。

Result: 实验展示了狄拉克点碰撞过程中的湮灭阻碍（obstruction to annihilation），以及欧拉数变化导致湮灭发生的拓扑相变（topological transition）。这种相变由布里渊区环面（Brillouin zone torus）上本征态的非阿贝尔框架旋转（non-Abelian frame rotation）诱导，狄拉克点四元数电荷（quaternionic charges）的转换解释了欧拉数的变化。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了狄拉克点碰撞行为的拓扑机制，通过非阿贝尔框架旋转诱导的拓扑相变，实现了从湮灭阻碍到欧拉数变化后湮灭发生的转变，深化了对狄拉克点拓扑动力学（topological dynamics）的理解。

Abstract: Dirac points (DPs) are topological singularities that determine the extraordinary properties of two-dimensional materials. They are generally classified by discrete topological invariants, which determine the possibility of DPs' annihilation upon their collision. Here, we study the behaviors of DPs within a photonic Kagome lattice created in atomic vapor. With optically engineering the potential difference among three sites constituting the Kagome unit cell while preserving time-reversal symmetry and the stability of an isolated DP, the DPs move in reciprocal space. By employing conical diffraction to measure their position and the topological invariant (Euler number), we demonstrate an obstruction to DPs' annihilation during collision and a transition to a case where the Euler number changes and annihilation occurs. Such topological transition is induced by a non-Abelian frame rotation of the eigenstates around the Brillouin zone torus. The associated conversion of the DP quaternionic charges during their motion explains the change of Euler number.

</details>

Abstract: Wigner crystals are typically confined to ultralow temperatures where thermal motion is frozen out. Moiré superlattices in twisted two-dimensional materials have extended their stability to higher temperatures and densities, but rely on delicate stacking that fixes the lattice geometry and limits tunability. Here we demonstrate a lithographic approach that bypasses these constraints. Using high-resolution nanofabrication, we pattern a nanoscale triangular lattice directly into a graphene gate integrated with a monolayer MoSe2 semiconductor. This engineered potential landscape localizes electrons into generalized Wigner crystal states that persist up to 15 K and densities of 2X10^12 cm-2, representing an order of magnitude improvement over pristine monolayer MoSe2.   <summary>Details</summary>

Using semiclassical theory and symmetry analysis, we demonstrate that this effect is generic across altermagnets and validate it through first-principles calculations in CrSb. Our results establish linear magnetoresistance as an alternative detection of the Berry curvature and Neel order in unconventional antiferromagnets.

This behavior has been predicted in a variety of setups, including Fabry-Pérot and Mach-Zehnder interferometers, and more recently in quantum dots. ### [83] [Imaging the high-frequency charging dynamics of a single impurity in a semiconductor on the atomic scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13040)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: As electronic devices approach the atomic limit, the charge dynamics of individual dopant atoms increasingly constrain performance, stability, and coherence. In scanning tunnelling microscopy (STM), donor ionization is typically interpreted as a static threshold process arising from tip-induced band bending. Here we show that the ionization of individual sulfur donors in InAs is intrinsically dynamic and governed by the local electric field. Using MHz-frequency STM noise spectroscopy with atomic-scale spatial mapping, we resolve pronounced random telegraph noise that is invisible in time-averaged tunnelling spectra. A bias-dependent model quantitatively links the noise spectra to microscopic ionization and neutralization processes of the donor states, enabling direct extraction of nanosecond charge-state lifetimes. The switching rate is strongly bias dependent, demonstrating that the electric field continuously drives charge-state transitions. Unexpectedly, we show that the degenerately doped bulk leads to a sharp bias-dependent onset of donor ionization as the donor level crosses the Fermi level, giving rise to a characteristic shoulder in the noise power spectrum that is captured by our model. These results establish donor ionization as a non-equilibrium dynamical process with nontrivial contribution by the bulk electrons, and identify impurity switching as a universal nanoscale charge-noise mechanism relevant to quantum devices.

### [84] [Extending Topological Bound on Quantum Weight Beyond Symmetry-Protected Topological Phases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13041)

Method: 通过投影谱（projected spectrum）定义的拓扑不变量来下界量子权重，并引入对称性破缺修正项到量子度量中。该方法在对称性破缺时仍然成立，并可通过外场下的光学电导率求和规则进行实验验证。

Conclusion: 成功将量子几何的拓扑下界从对称性保护拓扑相推广到更广泛的系统，提出的下界在对称性破缺条件下仍然有效，为实验验证提供了可行途径。

Abstract: The quantum metric encodes the geometric structure of Bloch wave functions and governs a wide range of physical responses. Its Brillouin-zone integral, the quantum weight, appears in the structure factor and provides lower bounds on observables such as the optical gap and dielectric constant. In symmetry-protected topological (SPT) phases, the nontrivial band topology imposes a lower bound on the quantum weight and constraints on the observables. Here, we generalize the topological bound on quantum geometry to encompass systems beyond the SPT phases. We show that topological invariants defined via the projected spectrum lower-bound the quantum weight with a symmetry-breaking correction to the quantum metric. Our proposed bound holds even when the underlying symmetries are broken, and it would be amenable to experimental verification via the optical conductivity sum rule under external fields. We illustrate our theory by adding a nonzero spin-orbit coupling term to a spin Chern insulator model, where we show that our proposed bound applies even though the conventional topological bound does not hold.

### [85] [A Straight Forward Method to Read the Nuclear Qudit of $4f$ Single-Molecule Magnets : $^{163}$DyPc$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13047)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用毫开尔文（millikelvin）温度下的自旋极化扫描隧道显微镜（spin-polarized scanning tunneling microscopy），通过分析Dy$^{3+}$磁矩反转产生的电报噪声（telegraph noise）统计特性来读取核自旋状态。超精细相互作用（hyperfine interactions）调制噪声统计，无需磁场扫描即可揭示核自旋信息。

Result: 在35毫开尔文温度下观测到超过分钟的核自旋弛豫时间$T_1$。通过射频场驱动核自旋跃迁，并在隧道电流中直接检测核磁共振信号，发现分裂的Kondo峰附近的电导依赖于核自旋状态。

Conclusion: 该方法为$^{163}$DyPc$_2$单分子磁体的核自旋读取提供了无需磁场扫描的新途径，实现了长弛豫时间的核自旋状态检测和核磁共振直接观测，为量子信息处理应用奠定了基础。

Abstract: Nuclear spins in $4f$ single-molecule magnets (SMMs) are promising qubits or qudits candidates for quantum information processing due to their relative isolation and reduced susceptibility to environmental disturbances, while hyperfine coupling with the $4f$ moments enables readout and control. So far, the nuclear spin states of individual TbPc$_2$ SMMs have been detected in transport measurements via the spin-cascade effect, in which transitions of the Tb$^{3+}$ magnetic moment coupled to the unpaired ligand electron manifest as conductance jumps in spin-polarized transport. The ligand electron also gives rise to a Kondo effect through its interaction with the metallic contacts. By sweeping a magnetic field along the easy axis of the Tb$^{3+}$ moment, the system is tuned to avoided crossings of the hyperfine levels, such that the magnetic field at which the conductance jumps occur indicates the nuclear spin state. Here, we present a method to read the nuclear spin of $^{163}$DyPc$_2$ ($I=5/2$) using millikelvin spin-polarized scanning tunneling microscopy without the need for magnetic-field sweeps. Instead, hyperfine interactions modify the statistics of the telegraph noise generated by reversals of the Dy$^{3+}$ moment, thereby revealing the nuclear spin state. We observe nuclear spin relaxation times $T_1$ in excess of minutes at \SI{35}{mK}. Furthermore, we drive nuclear spin transitions using a radio-frequency field and detect the resulting nuclear magnetic resonance directly in the tunneling current, as the conductance near the split Kondo peaks depends on the nuclear spin state.

</details>

*Wlodzimierz Jaskolski*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了双层石墨烯中由电场定义的量子点内的拓扑束缚态，重点关注电场反转形成的畴壁及其导致的边界局域态。

Method: 采用超越简单连续单谷模型的原子紧束缚方法，考虑矩形量子点沿扶手椅和锯齿方向的取向，分析原子结构、电场强度、谷混合和谷不对称性等效应。

Result: 电场在双层石墨烯中打开能隙，反转电场形成畴壁并产生局域的一维手性无带隙能带；量子点有限尺寸导致这些能带量子化，在点边界出现离散的局域束缚态。

Conclusion: 原子紧束缚方法揭示了与石墨烯原子结构相关的新效应，包括电场强度、谷混合和谷不对称性对量子点内拓扑束缚态的影响，超越了连续模型描述的范畴。

Abstract: We study topological bound states in quantum dots defined by an electric field in bilayer graphene. An external field is perpendicular to the bilayer and changes sign in a finite region that defines the quantum dot. The electric field opens a gap in the bilayer graphene, and the reversed field creates a domain wall with one-dimensional chiral gapless bands localized therein. The finite size of dots leads to the quantization of these bands and the appearance of discrete bound states localized at the dot boundary. We consider rectangular dots oriented along the armchair and zigzag directions. We go beyond a simple continuum one-valley model and use an atomistic tight-binding approach. This allows us to identify new effects related to the atomic structure of graphene, strengths of the electric field, valley mixing, and valley asymmetry.

### [87] [Band offsets in InP/ZnSe nanocrystals evaluated using two-photon transitions analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13074)
*K. I. Russkikh,A. A. Golovatenko,A. V. Rodina*
