<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解球形核壳InP/ZnSe纳米晶体的能带结构和光学特性，特别是通过分析单光子和双光子吸收光谱来确定价带偏移（valence band offsets）范围，并探究异质界面处的物理特性。

Method: 采用八带Kane模型（eight-band Kane model）和六带Luttinger哈密顿量（six-band Luttinger Hamiltonian）在球形近似下分别计算电子和空穴能谱；库仑相互作用（Coulomb interaction）以微扰方式考虑；计算了作为InP核与ZnSe壳之间带偏移函数的单光子和双光子吸收光谱。

Result: 计算表明，在存在非均匀展宽（inhomogeneous broadening）时，基态双光子活性激子态（ground two-photon-active exciton state）的跃迁可能被更高能态的强跃迁掩盖；通过对比计算光谱与实验数据，确定价带偏移范围为0.85-1 eV，超过自然偏移值0.57 eV，表明InP/ZnSe异质界面处存在由优先Zn-P键形成的电偶极子（electric dipoles）。

Conclusion: 研究成功识别了InP/ZnSe纳米晶体双光子吸收光谱主要特征对应的激子态，预测了线性-圆二色性（linear-circular dichroism）信号的光谱依赖性，并揭示了界面电偶极子对价带偏移的显著影响，为理解该类纳米晶体的光学性质提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We present a semi-analytical theoretical kp-study of the energy structure and optical transitions in spherical core-shell InP/ZnSe nanocrystals. We use the eight-band Kane model and the six-band Luttinger Hamiltonian in the spherical approximation to calculate the electron and hole energy spectra, respectively. The influence of the Coulomb interaction is considered perturbatively. The one- and two-photon absorption spectra are calculated as functions of the band offsets between the InP core and ZnSe shell. Exciton states responsible for the main features in the two-photon absorption spectra of InP/ZnSe nanocrystals are identified and the spectral dependence of the linear-circular dichroism signal is predicted. We show that in the presence of inhomogeneous broadening, the transition to the ground two-photon-active exciton state can be hidden behind intense transitions to higher-lying states. A comparison of the calculated one- and two-photon absorption spectra with the available experimental data shows that, depending on the lattice strain in the InP core, the range of possible valence band offsets is 0.85-1 eV. The determined range exceeds the natural valence band offset of 0.57 eV and indicates the presence of electric dipoles formed by the preferential Zn-P bonds at the InP/ZnSe heterointerface.

### [88] [Nested Feature Spectrum Topology: Tripartite Topological Equivalence of Feature, Entanglement, and Wilson Loop Spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13128)
*Yi-Chun Hung,T. Tzen Ong,Hsin Lin*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出嵌套特征谱拓扑（nested feature spectrum topology）概念，通过递归投影算子揭示特征谱、纠缠谱和Wilson环谱之间的三重等价关系，完善了传统的体边对应关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统拓扑相通过对称性分类，在对称性破缺情况下，投影谱（projected spectrum）为拓扑相分类提供了清晰方法。本文旨在深化对特征谱拓扑起源的理解，建立更完善的拓扑分类框架。

Method: 引入嵌套特征谱拓扑（nested feature spectrum topology），将投影算子递归应用于特征谱的子扇区，生成特征谱的层次结构。在非相互作用费米子系统中建立特征谱拓扑、纠缠谱和Wilson环谱之间的三重等价关系。

Result: 发现特征谱编码了量子可观测量扇区之间的纠缠，如自旋分辨拓扑中的自旋向上和向下态。证明了纠缠谱中的谱流（spectral flow）和特征谱中的Wilson环绕数（Wilson loop winding）是特征-能量互补性的等价表现。

Conclusion: 特征-能量互补性完善了传统的体边对应关系（bulk-boundary correspondence），表明即使能谱有隙，拓扑边界模仍可能在特征谱中持续存在。结果为特征谱中的能带拓扑起源提供了更深理解和坚实基础。

Abstract: Topological phases of matter are traditionally characterized through symmetry-based classifications. In cases of symmetry breaking, the projected spectrum - obtained by projecting the ground state onto the eigenstates of a pertinent quantum observable, such as spin or orbital angular momentum - provides a clear method for classifying topological phases. This approach underpins well-known frameworks such as spin-resolved topology and feature spectrum topology. Here we introduce nested feature spectrum topology, in which projection operators are applied recursively to subsectors of the feature spectrum, generating a hierarchy of feature spectra. We uncover a fundamental tripartite equivalence among the topology of feature, the entanglement, and the Wilson loop spectra in non-interacting fermionic systems. This equivalence reveals that the feature spectrum encodes the entanglement between sectors of the quantum observable, such as the spin-up and spin-down states in spin-resolved topology. We further prove that spectral flow in the entanglement spectrum and the Wilson loop winding in the feature spectrum are equivalent manifestations of the feature-energy complementarity: the appearance of gapless spectral flow in either energy or projected spectra on the boundary. This complementarity refines the conventional bulk-boundary correspondence by demonstrating that topological boundary modes may persist in the feature spectrum even when energy spectra are gapped. Our results provide a deeper understanding and solid foundation for the origin of band topology in the feature spectrum.

### [89] [Inverse Faraday Effect in Rashba two-dimensional electron systems: interplay of spin and orbital effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13187)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的导电系统中，逆法拉第效应（inverse Faraday effect）的轨道贡献机制尚未得到充分探索。本研究旨在阐明光致磁化的微观起源，并揭示低维电子系统中自旋与轨道机制在光驱动磁化动力学中的相互作用。

Method: 采用量子动力学方程（quantum kinetic equation）和格林函数图解法（Green's-function diagrammatics），对具有Rashba自旋轨道耦合（Rashba spin-orbit coupling）的无序二维电子系统进行理论分析。

Result: 在非相互作用Rashba金属中，自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）强烈改变轨道磁化，使其在现实参数范围内可与自旋磁化相当甚至超越。当辐射频率接近Rashba自旋分裂时，自旋和轨道磁化均表现出共振增强。

Conclusion: 研究结果阐明了光致磁化的微观起源，强调了低维电子系统中自旋与轨道机制在光驱动磁化动力学中的相互作用，为理解自旋轨道耦合系统中逆法拉第效应（inverse Faraday effect）的轨道贡献提供了重要理论依据。

Abstract: The inverse Faraday effect (IFE) refers to the generation of a DC magnetization by circularly polarized light through the transfer of optical angular momentum to electronic degrees of freedom. In conducting systems, this response can arise from two microscopic channels - spin polarization of itinerant electrons and orbital magnetization generated by circulating charge currents. However, the orbital contribution to the inverse Faraday effect in spin-orbit-coupled conducting systems remains largely unexplored. We present a theoretical analysis of the IFE in disordered two-dimensional electron systems with Rashba spin-orbit coupling using both the quantum kinetic equation and Green's-function diagrammatics. We find that in a noninteracting Rashba metal the orbital magnetization is strongly modified by spin-orbit coupling and can become comparable to, or exceed, the spin magnetization for realistic parameter regimes. When the radiation frequency approaches the Rashba spin splitting, both spin and orbital magnetizations exhibit resonant enhancement. These results clarify the microscopic origin of light-induced magnetization and highlight the interplay of spin and orbital mechanisms in optically driven magnetization dynamics in low-dimensional electronic systems.

Conclusion: 该研究为现代量子技术器件的实际设计提供了精确的成分依赖性带偏移参数，通过分析拟合表达式促进了模拟中的直接应用，解决了实验数据稀疏导致的成分依赖性设计难题。

Abstract: Accurate band offsets are essential for predictive continuum modeling of nanostructures such as quantum wells and quantum dots formed in strained Si/Si1-xGex and Ge/Si1-xGex heterostructures. Experimental offset data for these systems remain sparse away from endpoint compositions, making composition-dependent design difficult. We use atomistic first-principles density functional theory to compute valence- and conduction-band offsets across the full range 0 <= x <= 1. Random alloying is treated with special quasirandom structures, interface lineup terms are extracted from macroscopically averaged local Kohn-Sham potentials in thick periodic superlattices, valence-band spin-orbit coupling is included through species-resolved Mulliken weights, and conduction-band edges are refined using the screened hybrid Heyd-Scuseria-Ernzerhof functional. The resulting offsets show pronounced composition nonlinearity beyond the linear models explored in previous works, agree with experimental benchmarks, and reproduce the high-Ge slope change in the relaxed-alloy band gap. Analytic fitting expressions are provided for direct use in simulations, facilitating practical design of modern quantum technology devices.

### [91] [Magnetotransport in the presence of real and momentum space topology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13229)
*Azaz Ahmad,Takami Tohyama*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了时间反演对称性破缺、无倾斜外尔半金属（Weyl semimetal）在动量空间贝里曲率（Berry curvature）和实空间拓扑（斯格明子诱导的涌现磁场）共存条件下的磁输运特性，揭示了两种拓扑效应如何独立调控输运响应的几何特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究动量空间贝里曲率（Berry curvature）与实空间拓扑（由斯格明子诱导的涌现磁场产生）同时存在时的混合拓扑体系中磁输运特性，特别关注两种拓扑效应如何相互作用并产生可观测的输运特征。

Method: 采用包含贝里曲率修正和谷间散射（intervalley scattering）的半经典玻尔兹曼方法（semiclassical Boltzmann approach），分析混合拓扑体系中的纵向磁导率（longitudinal magnetoconductivity）和平面霍尔电导率（planar Hall conductivity）。

Result: 研究发现：无涌现磁场时，增强谷间散射导致纵向磁导率发生强烈符号反转；有限涌现磁场引入抛物线型磁场依赖关系的额外偏移，产生弱符号反转区域而不改变曲率；两种效应共存产生强-弱符号反转区域。涌现磁场还导致纵向和平面霍尔电导率角度依赖性的不对称性，且仅通过改变涌现磁场方向即可产生有限平面霍尔响应。

Conclusion: 结论表明斯格明子诱导的涌现磁场作为独立的拓扑调控参数，揭示了外尔系统中实空间与动量空间贝里曲率相互作用的可测量后果，提供了实空间拓扑的输运特征。

Abstract: We investigate magnetotransport in a time-reversal symmetry-broken, untilted Weyl semimetal in the simultaneous presence of momentum-space Berry curvature and real-space topology arising from a skyrmion-induced emergent magnetic field $\mathbf{B}_{\mathrm{emer}}$. Using a semiclassical Boltzmann approach incorporating Berry-curvature corrections and intervalley scattering, we analyze the longitudinal magnetoconductivity and planar Hall conductivity in this mixed-topology regime. In the absence of $B_{\mathrm{emer}}$, increasing intervalley scattering drives a strong sign reversal of the longitudinal magnetoconductivity. A finite $\mathbf{B}_{\mathrm{emer}}$ introduces an additional shift of the parabolic magnetic-field dependence, leading to a weak sign-reversal regime without altering the curvature. The coexistence of these effects naturally produces a strong-and-weak sign-reversal regime, demonstrating that intervalley scattering and real-space topology control distinct geometric features of the response. The emergent field further induces asymmetry in the angular dependence of both longitudinal and planar Hall conductivities. We show that a finite planar Hall response can arise solely from $\mathbf{B}_{\mathrm{emer}}$ when its direction is varied, providing a transport signature of real-space topology. Our results establish that the skyrmion-induced emergent field acts as an independent topological tuning parameter, revealing measurable consequences of the interplay between real- and momentum-space Berry curvature in Weyl systems.

### [92] [Quantum obstructions for N=1 infinite distance limits -- Part I: $g_s$ obstructions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12315)
*Lukas Kaufmann,Jeroen Monnee,Timo Weigand,Max Wiesner*

Main category: hep-th

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于分析四维N=1超对称弦紧化中经典无限远距离极限的量子阻碍效应。这些量子效应标志着与微扰有效作用量的显著偏离，对弦模型构建具有重要影响。

Method: 研究方法聚焦于Type IIB定向化（orientifold）与O7/O3-平面的复结构模空间及其F-理论描述。通过研究F-理论对Type IIB定向化的描述，其中所有纯g_s修正都编码在椭圆Calabi-Yau四重形的（经典）几何中。

Result: 主要发现是：根据O7-平面的位置，g_s的非微扰修正可能变得不受抑制，从而阻碍场空间相应渐近区域中的微扰Type IIB描述。g_s修正的模空间与经典模空间存在显著差异，极端情况下经典无限远距离退化可能在g_s修正的量子水平上完全消失。

Conclusion: 结论表明g_s修正会显著改变经典模空间结构，对弦模型构建具有重要影响。α'修正及对弦模型构建的启示将在后续论文中讨论。

Abstract: We analyse quantum obstructions to classical infinite distance limits in four-dimensional string compactifications with N=1 supersymmetry. Such quantum effects signal a severe departure from the perturbative effective action and can be of considerable importance for string model building. Our focus is on the complex structure moduli space of Type IIB orientifolds with O7/O3-planes and its F-theory description. In this first part of our analysis, we investigate the behaviour of $g_s$ corrections in infinite distance complex structure limits. Our main finding is that, depending on the location of the O7-plane, non-perturbative corrections in $g_s$ can become unsuppressed, thus obstructing a perturbative Type IIB description in the corresponding asymptotic region of the field space. In particular, this applies to large complex structure limits. To show this, we study the F-theory description of the Type IIB orientifold, in which all pure $g_s$ corrections are encoded in the (classical) geometry of an elliptic Calabi-Yau fourfold. This $g_s$-corrected moduli space is found to differ significantly from the classical moduli space. In extreme cases the classical infinite distance degeneration can be completely removed at the $g_s$-corrected quantum level. The behaviour of $α'$ corrections, as well as implications for string model building, are discussed in a companion paper.

### [93] [Outer automorphisms are sufficient conditions for RG fixed points](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12318)
*Thede de Boer,Andreas Trautner*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 论文指出外自同构（outer automorphism）的存在是量子场论重整化群流中存在固定超平面（fixed hyperplane）的充分条件，这为't Hooft的技术自然性论证提供了数学基础，并能推导重整化群β函数的非微扰约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究量子场论（Quantum Field Theory）中重整化群（renormalization group）流的固定点（fixed point）存在条件，特别是为't Hooft的技术自然性（technical naturalness）论证提供数学基础。

Method: 通过对称性论证（symmetry argument）分析外自同构（Outer Automorphism, Out）与重整化群流的关系，无需依赖微扰理论（perturbation theory）即可确定固定超平面。

Result: 发现外自同构的存在是重整化群流中存在固定超平面（fixed hyperplane, separatrix）的充分条件；当外自同构存在时，完全耦合的β函数系统的对称性大于作用量的对称性。

Conclusion: 外自同构为推导重整化群β函数的非微扰全阶约束提供了系统方法，并强调了在这些考虑中包含"goofy transformations"的重要性。

Abstract: We point out that the existence of an outer automorphism (Out) is a sufficient condition for the existence of a fixed hyperplane (fixed point, separatrix) in the renormalization group (RG) flow of a Quantum Field Theory (QFT). The corresponding RG fixed hyperplane is determined by a symmetry argument and can be computed without resorting to perturbation theory. This provides the mathematical underpinning of 't Hooft's technical naturalness argument, and results in a systematic way to derive non-perturbative all-order constraints on the RG beta functions. If an Out exists, the symmetry of the fully coupled system of beta functions is larger than the symmetry of the action. We also stress the importance of including goofy transformations in these considerations.

</details>

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究计算了在非平凡空间拓扑宇宙中量子场的有限、方案独立的卡西米尔应力-能量张量贡献，并发现对于共形耦合标量场，该贡献在膨胀的德西特相期间会驱动各向异性膨胀，即使宇宙初始处于局部均匀和各向同性状态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索非平凡空间拓扑宇宙中量子场的有限、方案独立的卡西米尔应力-能量张量贡献，及其对宇宙动力学的影响，特别是对均匀性和各向同性的潜在破坏作用。

Method: 方法包括计算共形耦合标量场和最小耦合标量场的卡西米尔应力-能量张量贡献，并分析该贡献在膨胀的德西特相期间对爱因斯坦方程的反作用。

Result: 结果显示，对于共形耦合标量场，卡西米尔应力-能量张量贡献在膨胀的德西特相期间会驱动各向异性膨胀，即使宇宙初始处于局部均匀和各向同性状态。

Conclusion: 结论指出，底层非平凡拓扑的量子印记不可避免地导致局部偏离均匀性和各向同性，表明拓扑量子效应能够显著影响宇宙的演化动力学。

Abstract: A finite, scheme-independent Casimir contribution to the stress-energy tensor arises naturally for quantum fields in universes with non-trivial spatial topology. We compute this Casimir stress-energy tensor contribution for a conformally coupled scalar field and for a minimally coupled scalar field. We show that, for the conformally coupled case, the backreaction of this contribution to the Einstein equations during an expanding de Sitter phase drives anisotropic expansion even when the Universe begins in a locally homogeneous and isotropic state. We conclude that quantum imprints of the underlying non-trivial topology inevitably give rise to local departures from homogeneity and isotropy.

### [95] [On the SymTFTs of Finite Non-Abelian Symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12323)
*Oren Bergman,Jonathan J. Heckman,Max Hübner,Daniele Migliorati,Xingyang Yu,Hao Y. Zhang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种针对有限非阿贝尔对称群的3D对称拓扑场论（SymTFT）构造方法，通过离散BF型理论拉格朗日量来更清晰地展示对称性数据，特别是处理表面附着非真线算符和非阿贝尔结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对于有限非阿贝尔对称群G，传统的Dijkgraaf-Witten拓扑场论虽然能明确展示对称性的"电"表示，但会掩盖部分磁数据以及绝对量子场论中的非阿贝尔结构，特别是那些无法完全脱离拓扑边界的对称算符。

Method: 针对3D对称拓扑场论，构建了有限群的离散BF型理论拉格朗日量，这些群可以表示为有限阿贝尔群和有限（可能非阿贝尔）群的扩展。这种方法能够直接处理非阿贝尔群元素而非仅其共轭类。

Result: 该方法不仅提供了重建伴随Drinfeld中心融合规则的简化途径，还能构造与直接非阿贝尔群元素相关的表面附着非真线算符。论文还概述了如何将这一处理推广到更高维对称拓扑场论。

Conclusion: 通过离散BF型理论框架，能够更清晰地展示有限非阿贝尔对称群的对称性数据，特别是处理传统方法中难以捕捉的非阿贝尔结构和边界附着算符，为对称拓扑场论研究提供了新工具。

Abstract: The $(D+1)$-dimensional symmetry topological field theory (SymTFT$_{D+1}$) of a $D$-dimensional absolute quantum field theory (QFT$_D$) provides a topological characterization of symmetry data. In this framework, the SymTFT comes equipped with a physical boundary specifying a relative QFT, and a topological boundary which specifies the global form of symmetries. In general, there need not be a unique bulk theory which encodes this information but it is often helpful to have a more manifest presentation of symmetries in terms of bulk degrees of freedom. For the case of a finite non-Abelian symmetry group $G$, the bulk SymTFT may be described by a Dijkgraaf-Witten TFT with gauge group $G$. This makes manifest the ``electric'' presentation of the symmetry data but can obscure some of the magnetic data as well as non-Abelian structure present in the absolute QFT$_D$ such as symmetry operators which cannot fully detach from the topological boundary. We address these issues for 3D SymTFTs by constructing discrete BF-like theory Lagrangians for finite groups which admit a presentation as an extension by a finite Abelian group and a finite (possibly non-Abelian) group. This enables us to give a streamlined approach to reconstructing the fusion rules of the accompanying Drinfeld center, but also allows us to construct surface-attaching non-genuine line operators associated directly with non-Abelian group elements rather than just their conjugacy classes. We also sketch how our treatment generalizes to higher-dimensional SymTFTs.

### [96] [Stable Black Strings from Warped Backgrounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12332)
*Sylvain Fichet,Eugenio Megias,Mariano Quiros,Geovanna Yamanaki*

Main category: hep-th

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究黑洞弦（black strings）的经典稳定性问题，特别关注时空曲率（spacetime curvature）本身是否能够提供稳定机制，而不依赖其他因素。

Method: 在具有平坦膜（flat brane）的一致五维膨胀子-引力（dilaton-gravity）系统中进行分析，考虑黑洞弦从膜延伸到类时边界（timelike boundary）的配置，包括正则边界和共形边界两种情况。

Result: 发现足够大的黑洞弦在经典意义上是稳定的，即使在临界情况的线性膨胀子时空（linear dilaton spacetime）中也是如此。在某些弯曲背景中，黑洞弦即使具有无限视界面积（infinite horizon area）也能保持稳定。

Conclusion: 时空曲率（spacetime curvature）本身足以经典地稳定黑洞弦，这一发现在具有无限视界面积的弯曲背景中尤其显著，扩展了对黑洞弦稳定机制的理解。

Abstract: We show that spacetime curvature alone can classically stabilize black strings. Working within a consistent five-dimensional dilaton-gravity system with a flat brane, we find that sufficiently large black strings are classically stable when they extend from the brane to a timelike boundary, which may be either regular or conformal. Black strings are also classically stable in the critical case of the linear dilaton spacetime. In some of the curved backgrounds considered, black strings are stable despite having infinite horizon area.

### [97] [Calabi-Yau Metrics with Kähler Moduli Dependence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12384)
*Andrei Constantin,Andre Lukas,Luca A. Nutricati*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合机器学习数值数据与解析拟设的方法，为Calabi-Yau三维流形上的Ricci平坦Kähler度量构造具有显式Kähler模依赖性的近似解析表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机在于建立Calabi-Yau度量数值结果与解析构造之间的桥梁，实现对Kähler模依赖性的系统研究。当前缺乏具有显式模依赖性的Ricci平坦Kähler度量的解析表达式。

Method: 方法结合了机器学习获取的数值数据与显式解析拟设（Ansatz）。具体流程包括：使用神经网络在Kähler模空间选定点学习Kähler势；将数据拟合到具有Kähler模依赖参数的解析表达式；通过符号回归（symbolic regression）确定这些系数作为Kähler模函数的解析形式。

Result: 该方法应用于两个具有h^{1,1}=2的Calabi-Yau三维流形：$\mathbb{P}^2 \times \mathbb{P}^2$中的双三次超曲面和$\mathbb{P}^1 \times \mathbb{P}^3$中的双次数(2,4)超曲面。所得解析表达式以百分比级精度再现数值学习的Kähler势，并保持底层流形的离散对称性。

Conclusion: 研究结果为Calabi-Yau度量的纯数值结果与解析构造之间建立了具体桥梁，为系统研究其Kähler模依赖性打开了大门。该方法能够重构保留显式Kähler模依赖性的闭式近似Ricci平坦度量。

Abstract: We present a method to construct approximate analytic expressions for Ricci-flat Kähler metrics on Calabi-Yau threefolds with explicit dependence on the Kähler moduli. Our strategy combines numerical data obtained from machine learning with an explicit analytic Ansatz for the Kähler potential and symbolic regression methods. Specifically, we use neural networks to learn the Kähler potential at selected points in Kähler moduli space, fit this data to analytic expressions with Kähler moduli-dependent parameters, and determine an analytic form of these coefficients as functions of the Kähler moduli using symbolic regression. In this way, we reconstruct closed-form approximations to the Ricci-flat metric that retain explicit Kähler-moduli dependence. We apply this method to two Calabi-Yau threefolds with $h^{1,1}=2$, namely a bicubic hypersurface in $\mathbb{P}^2 \times \mathbb{P}^2$ and a bi-degree $(2,4)$ hypersurface in $\mathbb{P}^1 \times \mathbb{P}^3$, both of which admit nontrivial discrete symmetry groups that simplify the structure of the metric. In both cases, the resulting analytic expressions reproduce the numerically learned Kähler potentials with percent-level accuracy and respect the discrete symmetry of the underlying manifold. Our results represent a concrete bridge between purely numerical results for Calabi-Yau metrics and analytic constructions, opening the door to a systematic study of their dependence on Kähler moduli.

Abstract: We study the relation between the Jones index and the Rényi entropies of two disjoint intervals on the line and of the ground state for a generic value of the Rényi index in the two conformal field theory models given by the Ising model and a free Majorana fermion, where Haag duality is satisfied. The analytic expressions of the crossing asymmetry for all the submodels displaying a violation of the Haag duality that are closed under the fusion rules are obtained. In the limiting regime where the two intervals become adjacent, the leading term of the expansion of the crossing asymmetry provides the Jones global index, for any finite value of the Rényi index.

### [100] [Is Time Reversal in de Sitter Space a Spontaneously Broken Gauge Symmetry?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12434)
*Leonard Susskind*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文探讨全息理论（holographic theory）中时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）的本质，认为时间反演确实是规范对称性（gauge symmetry），但通过自发对称破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking）被隐藏，并提出"确凿证据"——一条闭合曲线和使前进时钟变为后退时钟的holonomy。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在重新审视全息理论中涉及时间反演（time-reversal）的对称性是否应在体理论（bulk）中被规范化的标准观点。作者针对Harlow和Numasawa认为时间反演是规范对称性，以及Witten认为时间反演不同且不表现为体规范对称性的两种对立观点，提出自己的见解。

Method: 作者采用概念性而非数学严格性的方法，回顾时间反演自发对称破缺的案例。通过分析闭合曲线（closed curve）和holonomy——这种holonomy能将前进时钟（forward-going clocks）翻转为后退时钟（backward going clocks），来解释时间反演对称性的隐藏机制。

Result: 论文提出时间反演确实是规范对称性，但通过自发对称破缺被隐藏。关键的"确凿证据"（smoking gun）是存在一条闭合曲线和相应的holonomy，这种holonomy能够翻转时钟的时间方向，从而揭示时间反演对称性的本质。

Conclusion: 作者认为时间反演是全息理论中的规范对称性，但其表现因自发对称破缺而被隐藏。这一观点通过闭合曲线和时钟方向翻转的holonomy得到支持，为理解时间反演在全息对偶（holographic duality）中的角色提供了新视角。

Abstract: I'll begin with some well-deserved acknowledgements: I am grateful to Daniel Harlow for discussions of time-reversal holonomies. I have also benefited from a long ongoing correspondence with Edward Witten, but frankly in both cases I can't tell whether they agree with me or not. I have often been accused of imprecision, especially toward the later parts of a paper, where I expect that my readers have ``caught on." That does eventually happen -- the readers catching on and I thank them -- but I'm now almost 86 and I can't wait. So I've tried to maintain a level of conceptual if not mathematical rigor throughout. Mathematical rigor(mortis) can sometimes be the enemy of conceptual clarity. I thank my friend Richard Feynman for reminding me of that lesson. Finally I thank the chatbot who gave me the definition of scaffold in section \ref{Scaff}. It was better than anything I was able to do.
  Symmetries of a Holographic theory; whether continuous or discrete, local or global, are gauge symmetries of the bulk. This includes discrete space-time symmetries such as C and P. But time-reversal is sufficiently different from other symmetries that we may question the standard wisdom and ask whether symmetries involving T should be gauged in the bulk. Harlow and Numasawa \cite{Harlow:2023hjb} say yes; time-reversal is a gauge symmetry. Witten \cite{Witten:2025ayw} says no: time reversal is different and does not manifest as a gauge symmetry of the bulk. My view is -- yes -- but with a twist: Time-reversal is indeed a gauge symmetry; but it is hidden by spontaneous symmetry breaking. In this paper I will review the case for spontaneous symmetry breaking of time-reversal and explain the ``smoking gun" -- a closed curve and a holonomy which flips forward-going clocks to backward going clocks, and vice versa.

Method: 方法是通过沿视界零生成元的仿射膨胀（affine dilations）和绕对称轴的旋转（rotations about the axis of symmetry）的交换作用生成形变，类似于Moyal-Rieffel形变，从而在物理上实现视界的非交换几何结构。

Result: 主要结果是计算了形变视界理论中相干态的相对熵（relative entropy），发现其保持严格正性，并展现出形变参数的新颖二阶修正。这种修正对于视界面积足够小的黑洞尤为重要，因为此时普朗克尺度效应变得不可忽略。

Abstract: We construct a deformed algebraic quantum field theory on bifurcate Killing horizons in stationary axisymmetric spacetimes. The deformation is generated by the commuting actions of affine dilations along the null generators of the horizon and rotations about the axis of symmetry, analogously to the Moyal-Rieffel deformation. Physically, this effectively implements a noncommutative geometric structure of the horizon. Moreover, we compute the relative entropy between coherent states in the deformed horizon theory, which remains strictly positive and exhibits a novel second-order correction in the deformation parameter, which becomes particularly significant for black holes whose horizon area is sufficiently small for Planck-scale effects to become non-negligible.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究在FLRW背景与紧致维度乘积时空上标量场的量子效应，其中紧致维度尺寸允许随时间变化，这扩展了传统静态Casimir效应的研究框架。

Method: 修改标准绝热正则化（adiabatic regularization）方案，使其适用于乘积时空$\mathcal{M}^{1, \,d-1} \times \mathcal{S}^1$，其中紧致维度$\mathcal{S}^1$的尺度因子随时间变化。该方法能够处理d=3和d=4维度的解析计算。

Result: 在无质量（massless）且共形耦合（conformally coupled）极限下，主导阶时间相关结果与已知的时间无关Casimir贡献一致。当FLRW与紧致维度尺度因子重合时，高阶时间相关修正与(1+d)维FLRW时空的已知结果匹配。

Conclusion: 所发展的修改绝热正则化方案能够有效处理紧致维度尺寸随时间变化的乘积时空中的量子场论问题，为研究动态Casimir效应和额外维度演化提供了理论工具。

Abstract: We compute the vacuum expectation value of the stress-energy tensor of a scalar field on a product spacetime composed of an FLRW background times a compact dimension ($\mathcal{M}^{1, \,d-1} \times \mathcal{S}^1$), where the size of the latter is allowed to vary with time. We modify the standard adiabatic regularization prescription to obtain analytic expressions for both $d=3$ and $d=4$. In the massless and conformally coupled limit, the leading order time-dependent results are consistent with known time-independent Casimir contributions. Furthermore, in this limit the higher-order time-dependent corrections, when the FLRW and compact-dimension scale factors coincide, match known results for ($1+d$)-dimensional FLRW spacetime.

</details>


### [103] [Two Times for Freudenthal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13067)
*Alexander Kamenshchik,Alessio Marrani,Federica Muscolino*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了Bars等人提出的双时间物理（two-time physics）的代数结构，阐明了其与二次和三次约当代数（Jordan algebras）以及基于它们的约化Freudenthal三重系统（reduced Freudenthal triple systems, FTS）之间的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于澄清双时间物理的代数结构，特别是Bars引入的"扩展"相空间（'extended' phase space）与约当代数和约化Freudenthal三重系统之间的数学联系。

Method: 方法包括将扩展相空间赋予基于半单三次约当代数（称为洛伦兹自旋因子，Lorentzian spin factor）构建的约化FTS结构，该结构由原始不变对称四阶张量表征。应用典型的$Sp(2,\mathbb{R})$-规范固定程序（gauge fixing procedure）分析相关四次多项式的代数-微分约束。

Result: 结果表明，规范固定程序对与张量相关的四次多项式施加了代数-微分约束，这意味着扩展相空间坐标化的共轭变量仅跨越洛伦兹自旋因子自同构群（automorphism group）非传递作用的两个（同构的）幂零轨道（nilpotent orbits）。

Conclusion: 结论阐明了双时间物理的代数结构，并将其结果应用于相对论性和非相对论性物理系统，包括相对论性洛伦兹协变系统、非相对论性大质量粒子、氢原子以及具有非零能量的Carroll粒子。

Abstract: We investigate the algebraic structure of the two-time physics introduced some time ago by I. Bars and his co-authors, clarifying its relations with quadratic and cubic Jordan algebras, as well as with reduced Freudenthal triple systems (FTS) based on them. In particular, the `extended' phase space introduced by Bars can be endowed with the structure of a reduced FTS constructed over a semi-simple cubic Jordan algebra (named Lorentzian spin factor), characterized by a primitive, invariant symmetric tensor of rank $4$. The $Sp(2,\mathbb{R})$-gauge fixing procedure typical of two-time physics yields algebraic-differential constraints on the quartic polynomial associated to such a tensor, implying that only two (isomorphic) nilpotent orbits of the non-transitive action of the automorphism group of the Lorentzian spin factor are spanned by the conjugated variables which coordinatize the `extended' phase space. We illustrate our results in relativistic, manifestly Lorentz-covariant physical systems, as well as in non-relativistic systems (such as the non-relativistic massive particle, the hydrogen atom, and the Carroll particle with non-vanishing energy).

</details>


### [104] [(De-)Exciting the Third Poschl-Teller Kink](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12590)
*Hengyuan Guo,Jarah Evslin,Stefano Bolognesi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了σ=3标量模型中具有反射无损耗孤子（reflectionless kinks）的特性，该模型展现出φ^{8/3}势能，其真空态三阶导数发散，但通过计算辐射激发或退激发孤子形状模（shape modes）的振幅和概率，发现领头阶振幅仍为有限值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: σ=3孤子模型因具有φ^{8/3}势能而受到较少关注，该势能在真空态的三阶导数发散，导致传统微扰理论中远离孤子的三次相互作用发散。研究旨在探讨这一看似病理性模型的实际物理性质。

Method: 使用该发散的三次相互作用计算入射辐射激发或退激发孤子两个形状模的振幅和概率。尽管相互作用在远离孤子区域发散，但形状模局域于孤子附近，使得领头阶振幅计算可行。

Result: 计算结果显示领头阶振幅为有限值，表明σ=3模型并非病理性模型。其介子可视为Znojil束缚态的量子场论扩展。

Conclusion: σ=3标量模型虽然具有φ^{8/3}势能及其真空态三阶导数发散的特性，但通过计算辐射与孤子形状模相互作用的振幅，证明该模型物理上合理，其介子构成量子场论框架下的束缚态扩展。

Abstract: There is a series of scalar models possessing reflectionless kinks whose linear perturbations are described by a Pöschl-Teller potential at integer level $σ$. The cases $σ=1$ and $2$ are the well-known Sine-Gordon and $φ^4$ double-well models. The $σ=3$ kink has received relatively little attention because it exhibits a $φ^{8/3}$ potential, whose third derivative diverges in the vacuum. In old-fashioned perturbation theory this yields a cubic interaction that diverges far from a kink. We nonetheless use this interaction to calculate the amplitudes and probabilities for incoming radiation to excite or de-excite one of the kink's two shape modes. As each shape mode is localized about the kink, the leading order amplitudes are nonetheless finite. This suggests that the $σ=3$ model is not pathological, but rather its mesons are quantum field theoretic extensions of Znojil's bound states.

</details>


### [105] [Testing the AdS/CFT Correspondence Through Thermodynamic Geometry of Nonlinear Electrodynamics AdS Black Holes with Generalized Entropies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12678)
*Abhishek Baruah,Amijit Bhattacharjee,Prabwal Jyoti Phukon*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了三种非线性电磁理论（ModMax、NED和Euler-Heisenberg）中的AdS黑洞热力学及其全息对偶CFT描述，分析了三种熵框架下的相结构，发现热力学临界点与温度-熵关系的极值点一致，且Legendre不变GTD曲率的奇异性再现了这些临界点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究非线性电磁理论中的AdS黑洞热力学及其全息对偶CFT描述，分析不同熵框架（Bekenstein-Hawking熵、广义Rényi熵和Kaniadakis熵）对相结构的影响，理解热力学临界点的几何解释。

Method: 研究方法包括：分析三种非线性电磁理论（ModMax、NED和Euler-Heisenberg）的AdS黑洞解；在三种熵框架下研究热力学性质；通过温度、比热和几何热力学（GTD）标量曲率的行为分析相结构；比较体黑洞系统与其对偶CFT描述。

Result: 研究发现：热力学临界点对应温度-熵关系的极值点，并与比热的发散点一致；Legendre不变GTD曲率的奇异性再现了这些临界点，提供了相变的几何解释；全息对应下临界点的数量和结构保持不变；Euler-Heisenberg AdS黑洞展现出比ModMax和NED更复杂的相结构；Kaniadakis熵在所有系统中都产生额外的临界点。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明：非线性电磁动力学与广义熵形式共同影响AdS黑洞及其对偶CFT的临界行为；几何热力学为相变提供了自洽的几何解释；全息对应保持了临界点结构的对应关系；不同熵框架对相结构有显著影响，特别是Kaniadakis熵引入额外的临界行为。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamics and thermodynamic geometry of several Anti--de Sitter black hole solutions arising from nonlinear electromagnetic theories, namely the ModMax, nonlinear electrodynamics (NED), and Euler--Heisenberg AdS black holes, together with their holographically dual conformal field theory (CFT) descriptions. The analysis is carried out within three entropy frameworks: the standard Bekenstein--Hawking entropy and the generalized Rényi and Kaniadakis entropies. For each system, we analyze the phase structure through the behavior of temperature, specific heat, and the scalar curvature obtained from geometrothermodynamics (GTD). We find that thermodynamic critical points correspond to extrema in the temperature--entropy relation and coincide with divergences of the specific heat. These locations are reproduced by singularities in the Legendre--invariant GTD curvature, demonstrating a consistent geometric interpretation of the phase transitions. A comparison between the bulk black hole systems and their dual CFT counterparts shows that the number and structure of critical points are preserved under the holographic correspondence. Our results further reveal that the Euler--Heisenberg AdS black hole exhibits a more intricate phase structure compared with the ModMax and NED cases, while the Kaniadakis entropy consistently generates an additional critical point across all systems considered. These findings highlight the combined influence of nonlinear electromagnetic dynamics and generalized entropy formalisms on the critical behavior of AdS black holes and their dual CFTs.

### [106] [Carroll symmetries in field theory and gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12902)
*Florian Ecker*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文从Cartan几何视角研究Carroll对称性在场论和引力中的应用，推导了Carroll量子场论的普适对易关系，在二维时空中建立了与全息原理的联系，并发展了Carroll引力理论，特别研究了具有热力学性质的Carroll黑洞及其量子效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在通过Carroll对称性在场论和引力中的应用，探索量子引力在特定标度极限（称为tantum gravity limit）下的性质。Carroll几何为理解这一极限提供了有价值的理论框架。

Method: 采用Cartan几何方法描述弯曲Carrell流形，研究包括标量和矢量Carroll swiftons在内的多种场论。在二维时空中引入Carroll dilaton引力，定义具有热力学性质的Carroll黑洞，并研究其量子物质效应。

Result: 推导出适用于所有Carroll量子场论的应力-能量张量分量的普适对易关系。在二维时空中，Carroll boost反常导致对易关系中产生额外的Schwinger-like项，这些项成为三维渐近平坦爱因斯坦引力渐近对称性中心扩展的来源。对于Carroll-Schwarzschild黑洞，发现了非零的渐近能量密度，称为Carroll-Hawking效应。

Conclusion: Carroll对称性为研究量子引力在特定标度极限下的性质提供了有效框架。Carroll引力理论不仅建立了与全息原理的联系，还揭示了Carroll黑洞的热力学性质及其量子效应，特别是Carroll-Hawking效应的发现具有重要意义。

Abstract: This thesis explores several facets of Carroll symmetries through their applications to field theories and gravity. The geometric description of curved Carroll manifolds is developed from a Cartan-geometric viewpoint, reviewed at the outset. On these backgrounds, we study various field theories, including scalar and vector Carroll swiftons. Imposing causality and locality, we derive a universal sector of the commutators between Carroll stress-energy tensor components valid for any Carroll quantum field theory. In two dimensions, we confirm the connection to holography by showing that a Carroll boost anomaly gives rise to additional Schwinger-like terms in these brackets, sourcing the familiar central extensions of the asymptotic symmetries of three-dimensional asymptotically flat Einstein gravity. Afterwards, we come to theories of Carroll gravity which, as we argue, provide a valuable playground for understanding quantum gravity in a specific scaling limit which we refer to as the tantum gravity limit. At first, we review Carroll gravity in general dimensions and subsequently restrict to two spacetime dimensions where we introduce Carroll dilaton gravity. We define Carroll black holes as massive vacuum solutions to these theories that admit well-defined thermodynamic properties but have a Carroll extremal surface instead of an event horizon. After investigating several models and their solutions we finally add quantum matter to these backgrounds and study how the thermodynamic properties of a Carroll black hole reflect in its vacuum states. For the Carroll-Schwarzschild black hole we find a non-vanishing asymptotic energy density. We refer to this phenomenon as the Carroll-Hawking effect.

### [107] [Conformal Vacuum of dS$_4\times \mathbb R$ with Oppositely Oriented Boundaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13145)
*Lucas K. Kovalsky,Shivesh Pathak,Kyle Ritchie*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究de Sitter时空（dS$_4$）的真空结构及其在量子引力中的稳定性问题。通过构造具有特殊商结构的时空，探索dS$_4$真空态的简化表示及其与AdS$_3$时空的共形关系。

Method: 推导了一个dS$_4 \times \mathbb R$商时空，该时空渐近于dS$_4$，其商结构使得过去边界与未来边界具有相反取向。通过引入类光奇点（lightlike singularity）来分离时空的对映点（antipodes）。

Result: 该真空态共形等价于一个无限可定向覆盖（infinite orientable cover）的真空态，该覆盖对应一个具有S$^2$丛的非可定向AdS$_3$时空。真空的可分离性（separability）扩展到其全息对偶（holographic dual），后者是Cardy态的乘积。发现该候选dS$_4$真空态在量子引力中由于Hagedorn温度为零而存在微扰不稳定性（perturbatively unstable）。

Conclusion: 所构造的dS$_4 \times \mathbb R$商时空提供了一个简化的真空结构，但其在量子引力框架下存在微扰不稳定性，这源于Hagedorn温度的消失。该结果对de Sitter时空的真空稳定性研究具有重要意义。

Abstract: We derive a dS$_4 \times \mathbb R$ quotient spacetime that is asymptotically dS$_4$, where the quotient makes its past boundary oppositely oriented relative to its future boundary. This introduces a lightlike singularity that severs the antipodes of the spacetime and simplifies its global vacuum to a trivial product on antipodal static patches. We show that this state is conformal to the vacuum of an infinite orientable cover of a non-orientable AdS$_3$ spacetime with an S$^2$ bundle. The vacuum's separability extends to its holographic dual, which is a product of Cardy states. We find that this candidate dS$_4$ vacuum state is perturbatively unstable within quantum gravity due to a vanishing Hagedorn temperature.

### [108] [Interaction-Driven Ferrimagnetic Stripes in the Extended Hubbard Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12309)
*Chunhan Feng,Miguel A. Morales,Shiwei Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 在扩展哈伯德模型中引入最近邻排斥相互作用V会引发从反铁磁条纹序到调制亚铁磁序与棋盘电荷密度波交织的相变，该现象对铜氧化物材料和量子模拟器具有重要意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长程相互作用能显著重组关联电子基态。在方晶格哈伯德模型中，在位排斥作用会在掺杂时产生反铁磁自旋和电荷条纹序。研究旨在探索引入最近邻排斥相互作用V如何改变这一行为。

Method: 采用辅助场量子蒙特卡洛（auxiliary-field quantum Monte Carlo）和密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group）方法研究扩展哈伯德模型。通过引入最近邻排斥V和次近邻跳跃t'等参数，系统分析相互作用对基态序的影响。

Result: 当V/U超过临界比值（约0.25）时，系统发展出调制亚铁磁序（modulated ferrimagnetic order）与棋盘电荷密度波（checkerboard charge-density-wave）交织的基态。在亚铁磁畴内，自旋密度在正值（或负值）与接近零值之间交替变化。

Conclusion: 即使短程非局域相互作用也能稳定全新的磁织构，这对理解铜氧化物材料和设计可编程量子模拟器具有重要启示。次近邻跳跃t'会改变调制波长但不破坏序的稳定性。

Abstract: Long-range interactions can qualitatively reorganize correlated-electron ground states. In the square-lattice Hubbard model, on-site repulsion produces antiferromagnetic spin and charge stripes upon doping. We show that including a nearest-neighbor repulsion $V$ can dramatically alter this behavior. Using auxiliary-field quantum Monte Carlo and density matrix renormalization group methods, we find that, above a critical ratio $V/U$ ($\sim 0.25$), the system develops a modulated ferrimagnetic order intertwined with checkerboard charge-density-wave. Inside the ferrimagnetic domains, spin density alternates between positive (or negative) and nearly zero values. When the total spin is fixed to zero, positive and negative domains alternate in space; when spins are unconstrained, a ferrimagnetic state emerges with finite magnetization. Including a next-nearest-neighbor hopping $t'$ changes the modulation wavelength but leaves the order robust. Our results demonstrate that even short-range nonlocal interactions can stabilize qualitatively new magnetic textures, with implications for cuprate materials and programmable quantum simulators.

</details>


### [109] [Fracton Spin Liquid and Exotic Frustrated Phases in Ising-like Octochlore Magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12313)
*Matthew Stern,Michael D. Burke,Michel J. P. Gingras,Judit Romhányi,Kristian Tyn Kai Chung*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文提出八氯晶格（octochlore lattice）作为三维阻挫磁性的新一代研究平台，发现了包括分形子经典自旋液体（fracton CSL）在内的多种新奇阻挫相，为在真实材料中实现分形子拓扑序开辟了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近三十年来，三维阻挫磁性研究主要集中于角共享四面体（corner-sharing tetrahedra）的烧绿石几何和经典自旋液体（classical spin liquid, CSL）的自旋冰（spin ice）。本研究旨在探索角共享八面体晶格作为研究三维阻挫磁性的新一代平台。

Method: 研究八氯晶格（octochlore lattice）上伊辛自旋（Ising spins）的相图，考虑每个八面体内的第一和第二近邻相互作用。该晶格在反钙钛矿（anti-perovskite）和某些钾氟化合物中可实现。

Result: 发现了丰富的阻挫相，包括具有广泛基态简并度的经典自旋液体（CSLs），以及介于自旋液体和长程有序之间的亚广泛简并度相。特别识别出一种新颖的分形子经典自旋液体（fracton CSL），其激发被限制在一维线上移动，是著名X-cube模型（X-cube model）的经典U(1)类似物。此外还发现了自旋向列相（spin nematic phase），表现出从立方到四方再到正交对称性的两阶段维度约化。

Conclusion: 这项工作为在真实材料中实现分形子经典自旋液体（fracton CSLs）和探索其他奇异阻挫态铺平了道路，将八氯晶格确立为研究三维阻挫磁性的有前景平台。

Abstract: For nearly three decades frustrated magnetism research in three dimensions (3D) has centered on the pyrochlore geometry of corner-sharing tetrahedra and the classical spin liquid (CSL) known as spin ice. In this work, we propose that a lattice of corner-sharing octahedra -- appropriately dubbed the octochlore lattice -- may provide a next-generation platform for the study of 3D frustrated magnetism, with realizations in anti-perovskite and certain potassium-fluoride compounds. We study the phase diagram of Ising spins on the octochlore lattice with first- and second-neighbor interactions within each octahedron, which displays a rich variety of frustrated phases, including CSLs with extensive ground state degeneracies, as well as phases with subextensive ground state degeneracies intermediate between spin liquids and long-range order. In addition to a spin ice CSL, we identify a novel fracton CSL with excitations restricted to move along one-dimensional (1D) lines, which is a classical U(1) analog of the celebrated X-cube model, a paradigmatic realization of fracton topological order. The existence of these two CSLs is rationalized as condensation of 1D ferro-spinons bound states from a parent phase with subextensive degeneracy due to frustration of ferromagnetically polarized chains. We also find a spin nematic phase exhibiting two-stage dimensional reduction from cubic to tetragonal (uniaxial) and finally orthorhombic (biaxial) symmetry, driven by strong fluctuations arising from deconfined 1D antiferro-spinons. This work paves the way for the potential realization of fracton CSLs and the exploration of other exotic frustrated states in real materials.

</details>


### [110] [Parity and time-reversal invariant Ising spin ordering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12330)
*Yue Yu,Jin Matsuda,Hikaru Watanabe,Ryotaro Arita,Daniel F. Agterberg*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一类新型共面反铁磁体，其在实空间产生宇称和时间反演对称的伊辛自旋序，能够实现纯非相对论性纵向/横向自旋电导、通过圆偏振光产生非相对论性交变磁性自旋劈裂，以及通过宇称对称破缺产生非相对论性奇宇称自旋劈裂。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反铁磁序、动量依赖的布洛赫自旋劈裂、时间反演对称和时间反演对称在非相对论系统中的相互作用已成为自旋电子学的核心主题。现有研究主要关注宇称保持/时间反演破缺的交变磁体（altermagnets）和宇称破缺/时间反演保持的奇宇称磁体，两者均表现出伊辛型布洛赫自旋劈裂。

Method: 作者引入了一类新型共面反铁磁体（coplanar AFMs），其在实空间产生宇称和时间反演对称的伊辛自旋序。通过理论分析，研究了这类系统产生的自旋旋转对称破缺所允许的物理现象。从Magndata数据库中识别了16种候选材料，并提供了有效微观模型和基于密度泛函理论的计算结果。

Result: 研究发现这类共面反铁磁体能够实现：纯非相对论性纵向（或横向）自旋电导（spin-conductivities）、通过圆偏振光产生非相对论性交变磁性自旋劈裂（altermagnetic spin-splittings），以及通过宇称对称破缺（如外加电场）产生非相对论性奇宇称自旋劈裂（odd-parity spin-splittings）。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了一类新型共面反铁磁体在实空间产生宇称和时间反演对称的伊辛自旋序，其自旋旋转对称破缺能够产生多种非相对论性响应。研究不仅扩展了对磁性材料中对称性-性质关系的理解，还为自旋电子学应用提供了新的材料平台。

Abstract: The interplay of antiferromagnetic order, momentum-dependent Bloch spin-splitting, time-reversal (T), and parity (P) symmetries in non-relativistic systems has emerged as a central theme for spintronics. Two well-known examples are P-preserving and T-violating altermagnets and P-violating and T-preserving odd-parity magnets. These both exhibit an Ising, or uniaxial, Bloch spin-splitting. Here we introduce a new class of coplanar AFMs that generate a P and T symmetric, translation-invariant Ising spin order in real space. Naively, such AFMs are not expected to exhibit unusual phenomena. Here we show that the spin-rotational symmetry breaking generated by these AFMs allows: pure non-relativistic longitudinal (or transverse) spin-conductivities, the generation of non-relativistic altermagnetic spin-splittings through circularly polarized light, and the generation of non-relativistic odd-parity spin-splittings through parity symmetry breaking, by, for example, applied electric fields. We identify 16 candidate materials in the Magndata database for which our theory applies and provide effective microscopic models and DFT-based results that highlight the large emergent responses.

### [111] [Electronic correlations and dynamical screening with ab initio quantum embedding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12336)
*Chia-Nan Yeh,Francesco Petocchi,Alexander Hampel,Philipp Werner,Olivier Parcollet,Antoine Georges,Miguel Morales*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种高效的全自洽GW+EDMFT实现，结合了GW级别的非局域效应和扩展动力学平均场理论（EDMFT）中的局域关联非微扰处理，为强关联量子材料提供了预测性从头算框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强关联量子材料的精确描述需要同时处理强局域多体效应和非局域动力学屏蔽。现有方法如约束随机相位近似（constrained-RPA）存在过度屏蔽问题，需要发展能够一致描述跨能量尺度屏蔽过程的理论框架。

Method: 采用全自洽GW+EDMFT方法，在格林函数和动力学屏蔽相互作用中实现完全自洽。通过插值可分离密度拟合（interpolative separable density fitting, ISDF）技术压缩双粒子关联函数，实现高效计算。

Result: 将方法应用于莫特绝缘体SrMnO₃和关联金属LaNiO₃，全自洽性解决了约束RPA方法固有的过度屏蔽问题。通过抑制虚假低能屏蔽通道，为SrMnO₃获得了与实验定量一致的莫特绝缘态。

Conclusion: 全自洽GW+EDMFT被确立为强关联量子材料的预测性从头算框架，能够一致描述跨能量尺度的屏蔽过程，为相关材料研究提供了可靠的理论工具。

Abstract: First-principles descriptions of correlated quantum materials require a simultaneous treatment of strong local many-body effects and nonlocal dynamical screening. We present an efficient fully self-consistent implementation of $GW$+EDMFT that combines nonlocal effects at the $GW$ level with a non-perturbative treatment of local correlations within extended dynamical mean-field theory (EDMFT), while providing a controlled double-counting prescription. Crucially, self-consistency in both the Green's function and the dynamically screened interaction is essential to achieve a consistent description of screening processes across energy scales. The efficient computation of this self-consistent solution is enabled here by compressing two-particle correlation functions using interpolative separable density fitting (ISDF). Applying the scheme to the Mott insulator SrMnO$_3$ and the correlated metal LaNiO$_3$, we show that full self-consistency resolves the overscreening inherent to constrained-RPA approaches. By suppressing spurious low-energy screening channels, a Mott-insulating state in quantitative agreement with experiment is obtained for SrMnO$_3$. These results establish fully self-consistent $GW$+EDMFT as a predictive ab initio framework for strongly correlated quantum materials.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 迁移率边（mobility edges）是理解安德森局域化（Anderson localization）的核心概念，本研究旨在探讨多个相互可公度的准周期频率对迁移率边形成的影响，特别关注在准周期势中添加常数偏移的效应。

Method: 研究聚焦于一维全带平钻石链（all-bands-flat diamond chain）的准周期势，通过添加常数偏移来改变系统特性，分析其对迁移率边形成的影响。

Result: 研究发现常数偏移能将异常迁移率边（anomalous mobility edges，分离局域态与多重分形态）转化为常规迁移率边（conventional mobility edges，分离局域态与退局域态），并首次展示了Avila全局理论在解析预测迁移率边位置方面的失效，表现为位置不匹配和多重迁移率边的形成。

Conclusion: 准周期势中常数偏移的添加能显著改变迁移率边的性质，将异常迁移率边转化为常规迁移率边，同时揭示了Avila全局理论在预测此类系统迁移率边位置方面的局限性。

Abstract: The mobility edges (MEs) that separate localized, multifractal and ergodic states in energy are a central concept in understanding Anderson localization. In this work we study the effect of several mutually commensurate quasiperiodic frequencies on the mobility-edge formation. We focus on the example of the addition of a constant offset to the quasiperiodic potential of the one-dimensional all-bands-flat diamond chain. We show that this additional offset can transform the anomalous mobility edges (AMEs), i.e. the energies, separating localized and multifractal states, into conventional mobility edges, separating localized from delocalized states. Also this appears to be the first example which shows the failure of Avila's global theory to analytically predict the ME location. We observe this violation both quantitatively, through the ME location mismatch, and qualitatively, via the formation of multiple MEs, not predicted by the theory.

By measuring the transitions' magnetic-field dependence we determined an antiferromagnetic ordering with spins oriented along or slightly canted from the crystal's $a^*$ axis. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 向列相（nematic phases）在量子材料中广泛存在，但其起源及其与其他对称性破缺相（symmetry-breaking phases）的关系仍是重要而具有挑战性的研究课题。本研究旨在阐明CoTa₃S₆中提出的向列相与共线及非共面反铁磁序（collinear and non-coplanar antiferromagnetic orders）之间的交织关系。

Method: 采用弹阻实验（elastoresistivity experiments）研究向列涨落（nematic fluctuations），并结合补充的磁阻测量（magnetoresistance measurements）分析六方晶系（hexagonal system）中的三态向列性（three-state nematicity）特征。

Result: 在条纹反铁磁转变（stripe antiferromagnetic transition）以下观察到发散状的非对称弹阻响应（divergence-like antisymmetric elastoresistivity），表明存在与磁序耦合的独立向列自由度（nematic degree of freedom）。向列涨落受外加面外磁场（external out-of-plane magnetic field）强烈调制，电阻各向异性（resistivity anisotropy）起始温度表现出显著的应变依赖性（strain dependence），但反铁磁转变温度在磁场或应变下几乎保持不变。

Conclusion: CoTa₃S₆代表了向列相与反铁磁序（nematic and AFM orders）相互交织但具有不同起源的独特案例，为理解量子材料中对称性破缺相之间的复杂关系提供了重要见解。

Abstract: Nematic phases that break rotational symmetry are widely observed in quantum materials, and clarifying their origin and relationship with other symmetry-breaking phases remains an important but challenging task. In this work, we investigate nematic fluctuations in CoTa$_3$S$_6$ using elastoresistivity experiments to resolve the nature of the proposed nematic phase intertwined with collinear and non-coplanar antiferromagnetic orders. We observe a divergence-like antisymmetric elastoresistivity that rapidly develops below the stripe antiferromagnetic transition, consistent with a distinct nematic degree of freedom coupled to the magnetic order. While nematic fluctuations are strongly modulated by an external out-of-plane magnetic field and the onset temperature of resistivity anisotropy shows pronounced strain dependence, the antiferromagnetic transition temperatures remain nearly unchanged under either magnetic field or strain. Additionally, complementary magnetoresistance measurements reveal characteristic signatures of three-state nematicity in a hexagonal system. Our findings demonstrate CoTa$_3$S$_6$ as a unique case of intertwined nematic and AFM orders with distinct origins.

### [115] [Discovery of a hybridization-wave electronic order in a van der Waals Kondo lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12720)
*Lu Cao,Jiefei Shi,Lanxin Liu,Xuan Luo,Yu-Ping Sun,Yi-feng Yang,Yugui Yao,Jinhai Mao,Yuhang Jiang*

TL;DR: 该研究首次在层状过渡金属二硫化物6R-TaS2中直接观测到杂交波（hybridization wave），验证了长期的理论预测，并展示了范德华材料作为探索杂交驱动量子相的平台潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近藤晶格（Kondo lattice）系统中，局域磁矩与巡游电子相干杂交会产生丰富的量子现象。理论上提出杂交强度可作为空间调制的序参量，形成所谓的杂交波（hybridization wave），但直接实验证据一直是未解决的挑战。

Method: 研究使用扫描隧道显微镜和光谱学（STM/STS）技术，在天然异质结构6R-TaS2（由交替的1T-和1H-TaS2层组成）中进行观测。通过识别1T层中的杂交隙（hybridization gap）来证明相干近藤晶格的建立。

Result: 研究发现杂交隙呈现单轴晶胞加倍调制，破坏了底层大卫之星超晶格（Star-of-David superlattice）的平移和旋转对称性。这种晶胞加倍并非由结构形貌引起，因此构成了杂交波序的实空间可视化。此外，杂交波与具有相同周期性和取向的能量依赖向列序（nematic order）相关，揭示了交织的电子不稳定性。

Conclusion: 该发现不仅验证了长期的理论预测，而且确立了层工程范德华材料（layer-engineered van der Waals materials）作为探索和控制杂交驱动量子相（hybridization-driven quantum phases）的多功能平台。

Abstract: Kondo lattice systems, in which localized magnetic moments coherently hybridize with itinerant electrons, exhibit a rich landscape of emergent quantum phenomena. Within this framework, the hybridization strength itself has been theoretically proposed as a spatially modulated order parameter, giving rise to a so-called hybridization wave. However, direct experimental evidence of this quantum state has remained an outstanding challenge. Here, we report the direct observation of a hybridization wave in the layered transition metal dichalcogenide 6R-TaS2, a naturally occurring heterostructure composed of alternating 1T- and 1H-TaS2 layers. Using scanning tunneling microscopy and spectroscopy (STM/STS), we identify the hybridization gap in 1T layer, demonstrating the establishment of a coherent Kondo lattice. Notably, we discover that the hybridization gap present a uniaxial unit-cell doubling modulation, which breaks the both translational and rotational symmetries of the underlying Star-of-David superlattice. Such unit-cell doubling is not caused by structural topography, and therefore, constitutes the real-space visualization of the hybridization-wave order. Furthermore, the hybridization wave correlates with an energy-dependent nematic order that shares the same periodicity and orientation, revealing intertwined electronic instabilities. Our findings not only validate a long-standing prediction but also establish layer-engineered van der Waals materials as a versatile platform for exploring and controlling hybridization-driven quantum phases.

Here we present a new strategy combining high-throughput first-principles calculations, magnetic force theory, and spin Hamiltonian analysis. Starting from the 150,000 material database, we catalogue candidate materials that may host competing exchange interactions and new types of magnetic states with the focus on kagome or triangular lattices. ### [117] [Many-body correlations in Floquet steady-states: Frequency-resolved renormalization group of the driven Anderson impurity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12844)
*Jan-Niklas Herre,Christoph Karrasch,Dante M. Kennes*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个在Floquet稳态中直接表述的函数重整化群框架，能够系统性地纳入频率依赖的相互作用效应。以周期性驱动的单杂质安德森模型为例，该方法在中等相互作用强度下与最先进的Floquet格林函数方法定量一致，并揭示了Kondo云在局域周期性驱动下的强韧性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在开发一个能够系统处理频率依赖相互作用效应的理论框架，以分析驱动相互作用系统中的动力学响应函数和非平衡输运。这为解决周期性驱动量子材料中的非平衡物理问题提供了新途径。

Method: 引入了一个在Floquet稳态中直接表述的函数重整化群（functional renormalization group）框架，该方法保留了两粒子顶点（two-particle vertex）的频率结构直至相互作用强度的二阶。以周期性驱动的单杂质安德森模型（single-impurity Anderson model）作为范例系统进行验证。

Result: 该方法在中等相互作用强度下与最先进的Floquet格林函数方法（Floquet Green's function methods）在有限频率可观测量上定量一致。研究发现，尽管周期性驱动通过非弹性散射（inelastic scattering）显著展宽了Kondo共振（Kondo resonance），但多体Kondo云（many-body Kondo cloud）基本保持完整，这抑制了Kondo峰的Floquet复制（Floquet replicas）并导致Kondo钉扎（Kondo pinning）的部分持续。

Conclusion: 该函数重整化群框架为研究驱动相互作用系统中的动力学响应提供了可控途径。研究揭示了局域周期性驱动下涌现多体关联（emergent many-body correlations）的强韧性，同时表明静态性质通常可由更简单的近似可靠捕获，这为建模驱动量子材料提供了实用路径。

Abstract: We introduce a functional renormalization group framework formulated directly in the Floquet steady-state that systematically incorporates frequency-dependent interaction effects. By retaining the frequency structure of the two-particle vertex up to second order in interaction strength, our approach provides controlled access to dynamical response functions and nonequilibrium transport in driven, interacting systems. Using the periodically driven single-impurity Anderson model as a paradigmatic example, we benchmark our results against state-of-the-art Floquet Green's function methods and find quantitative agreement for finite-frequency observables up to intermediate interaction strengths. Remarkably, we also show that static properties are often captured reliably by much simpler approximations, suggesting practical pathways for modeling driven quantum materials. Finally, we demonstrate that although periodic driving of the dot strongly broadens the Kondo resonance through inelastic scattering, it leaves the many-body Kondo cloud largely intact. This robustness suppresses Floquet replicas of the Kondo peak and leads to a partial persistence of Kondo pinning, highlighting the resilience of emergent many-body correlations under local periodic driving.

*K. Ramesh Kumar,Xudong Huai,Allen O. Scheie,Thao T. Tran*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本教程为研究人员提供了关于热容（heat capacity）测量的实用指南，涵盖数据收集、分析和解释，特别关注当代量子材料中的相变和激发研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热容测量是研究凝聚态物质中微观自由度与宏观行为关系的有力工具，但数据分析对新研究人员构成显著挑战。尽管已有教科书阐述理论方面，但实际应用仍具难度。

Method: 本教程通过概述热力学、热容和熵（entropy）之间的联系，以及测量方法和数据分析，指导研究人员处理热容数据。涵盖代表性示例，包括声子动力学（phonon dynamics）、自旋波（spin waves）、超导体（superconductors）等量子材料。

Result: 教程提供了热容测量的实用框架，使研究人员能够将热容作为定量工具，用于理解奇异物质态（exotic states of matter）。

Conclusion: 本指南旨在为研究人员提供简洁、易用的热容数据分析方法，使其能够有效利用热容作为研究量子材料中相变和激发的定量透镜（quantitative lens）。

Abstract: Heat capacity measurements are a powerful tool that researchers rely on when studying the relationship between microscopic degrees of freedom and macroscopic behavior in condensed matter. This uniqueness stems from heat capacity capturing contributions from lattice, electronic, and magnetic components, as well as energy-level populations, enabling an effective approach to studying phase transitions and excitations across different classes of materials. However, analyzing heat capacity data presents a common, appreciable challenge for new researchers. Although comprehensive theoretical aspects of heat capacity are presented in several elegant textbooks, practical application remains a daunting task. To overcome this challenge, this tutorial guides researchers in collecting, analyzing, and interpreting heat capacity data in contemporary quantum materials. We outline the connections between thermodynamics, heat capacity, and entropy, as well as measurement methodology and data analysis for representative examples, including phonon dynamics, spin waves, superconductors, magnetic skyrmions, proximate quantum spin liquids, and heavy-fermion materials. Our goal is to provide a concise, accessible guide that enables new researchers to utilize heat capacity as a quantitative lens for understanding exotic states of matter.

</details>


### [119] [Orbital dimerization-induced first-order structural phase transition: a case study in La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12924)
*Xingchen Shen,Wei Ku*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了一阶结构相变（first-order structural phase transition）通常源于超越传统计算考虑的原子间关联（inter-atomic correlation），并以镍酸盐超导体La₃Ni₂O₇为例，提出了"轨道二聚化（orbital dimerization）"机制作为通用解释框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 一阶结构相变是材料中常见现象，能显著改变物理性质，但其突变性质通常无法通过现实计算解释，表明在描述邻近稳定相的电子结构时忽略了重要物理机制。

Method: 以新近发现的镍酸盐超导体La₃Ni₂O₇为原型示例，采用低能活性轨道的全多体处理（full many-body treatment），超越传统材料计算中考虑的原子内关联（intra-atomic correlation）。

Result: 研究发现一阶结构相变存在通用的原子间"轨道二聚化"机制，对应于自旋单重态键（spin-singlet bond）形成时的能量突降。这种原子间关联不仅从根本上改变了晶格键合，也改变了相变过程中低能电子性质的特征。

Conclusion: 该强机制和开发的计算框架广泛适用于多种离子材料，为理解其物理性质和功能所必需的原子与电子结构提供了有价值的见解。

Abstract: First-order structural phase transition is a common phenomenon in materials that qualitatively alters their physical properties. Yet, the abrupt first-order nature is usually unexplained by realistic computations, implying an omission of important physics in describing the electronic structure of the nearby stable phases. Using the recently discovered nickelate superconductors La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ as a prototypical example, we demonstrate that such first-order nature is typically beyond intra-atomic correlation considered in state-of-the-art material computations. Instead, a full many-body treatment of low-energy active orbitals reveals a generic inter-atomic "orbital dimerization" mechanism of first-order structural phase transition, corresponding to abrupt energy reduction upon a spin-singlet bond formation. Such an inter-atomic correlation qualitatively changes not only the essential lattice bonding but also the characteristics of low-energy electronic properties across the transition. This strong mechanism and the developed computational framework are generally applicable to a wide variety of ionic materials, to produce valuable insights into atomic and electronic structures essential for their physical properties and functionalities.

</details>


### [120] [Data-efficient surrogate modeling of spectral functions using Gaussian processes: An application to the $t$-$t'$-$t''$-$J$ model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13064)
*Sanket Jantre,Nathan M. Urban,Weiguo Yin,Niraj Aryal*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种数据高效的谱函数（spectral function）代理模型，使用深度核高斯过程（deep-kernel Gaussian process）与稀疏变分推断（sparse variational inference），仅需10%的训练数据即可达到与全数据前馈神经网络（feed-forward neural network）相当的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 谱函数编码了关键的多体信息，但高保真度计算成本高昂。机器学习代理模型已成为有力替代方案，但许多方法需要大量训练数据集。本研究旨在开发数据高效的谱函数代理模型。

Method: 使用$t$-$t'$-$t''$-$J$模型描述量子反铁磁体（quantum antiferromagnet）中的空穴运动。基于约10^5个自洽玻恩近似（self-consistent Born approximation）谱，训练深度核高斯过程稀疏变分推断（DKL-SVGP）代理模型，仅使用10%可用训练数据。以前馈神经网络（FFNN）作为基准进行对比。

Result: DKL-SVGP模型在减少数据情况下持续优于FFNN，尽管仅使用10%训练数据，其谱级误差与全数据FFNN基线处于同一数量级。最差尾部诊断显示在困难谱上保真度提高，峰值水平分析表明DKL-SVGP以可比精度恢复主导峰值高度，并在匹配峰值评估下改善峰值位置一致性。

Conclusion: 这些结果突显了基于高斯过程（GP-based）的代理模型在稀缺数据条件下作为谱函数预测的竞争性且数据高效的方法。

Abstract: Spectral functions encode key many-body information but are costly to compute with high fidelity. Machine-learning surrogates have emerged as a powerful alternative, yet many approaches require large training datasets. We develop a data-efficient surrogate for spectral functions using the $t$-$t'$-$t''$-$J$ model, which describes the motion of a hole in a quantum antiferromagnet. Using $\sim$ 10$^5$ self-consistent Born approximation-based spectra from Lee, Carbone and Yin (Phys. Rev. B 107, 205132 (2023)), we train a deep-kernel Gaussian process surrogate model with sparse variational inference (DKL-SVGP) using only 10% of the available training spectra. We benchmark against feed-forward neural networks (FFNN) trained on the same reduced subset and on the full dataset. The proposed DKL-SVGP model consistently outperforms the reduced-data FFNN and, despite using only 10% of the training spectra, achieves spectrum-wise errors within the same order-of-magnitude as the full-data FFNN baseline. Worst-tail diagnostics show improved fidelity on difficult spectra, while peak-level analysis indicates that DKL-SVGP recovers dominant peak heights with comparable accuracy and improves peak-location agreement under a matched-peak evaluation that mitigates rare peak-swapping cases. Overall, these results highlight GP-based surrogates as a competitive and data-efficient approach for spectral-function prediction in scarce-data regimes.

</details>


### [121] [SU(2) gauge theory of fluctuating stripe order in the two-dimensional Hubbard model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13071)
*Henrik Müller-Groeling,Pietro M. Bonetti,Paulo Forni,Walter Metzner*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究提出了二维哈伯德模型（Hubbard model）中条纹序（stripe order）涨落的SU(2)规范理论，通过电子算符分数量子化（fractionalization）为赝自旋（pseudospin）费米子荷子（chargons）和中性自旋子（spinons），描述了电荷有序赝隙相（pseudogap phase）的特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在建立二维哈伯德模型中条纹序涨落的规范理论框架，以理解电荷有序赝隙相中费米面重构（reconstructed Fermi surface）和自旋隙（spin gap）等物理现象的形成机制。

Method: 采用SU(2)规范理论，将电子算符分数量子化为具有赝自旋自由度的费米子荷子和电荷中性自旋子。荷子采用重整化平均场理论（renormalized mean-field theory）处理，而自旋子则用非线性σ模型（non-linear sigma model）描述，其赝自旋刚度由荷子决定。

Result: 理论预测了电荷有序赝隙相的存在，该相具有重构的费米面和自旋隙。单粒子激发谱函数（spectral function）展现出费米弧（Fermi arcs）及其他结构，这些弧出现在布里渊区（Brillouin zone）的不同区域，但从不局限于布里渊区对角线附近。

Conclusion: 该SU(2)规范理论成功描述了条纹序涨落导致的电荷有序赝隙相，解释了费米弧等实验观测特征，并确保物理SU(2)自旋对称性在有限温度下不被破坏。

Abstract: We present an SU(2) gauge theory of fluctuating stripe order in the two-dimensional Hubbard model. The theory is based on a fractionalization of the electron operators in fermionic chargons with a pseudospin degree of freedom, and charge neutral spinons capturing fluctuations of the spin orientation. The chargons are treated in a renormalized mean-field theory. We focus on regions of the phase diagram where they undergo stripe order. The spinons are described by a non-linear sigma model with pseudospin stiffnesses determined by the chargons. They prevent breaking of the physical SU(2) spin symmetry at any finite temperature, resulting in a charge ordered pseudogap phase with a reconstructed Fermi surface and a spin gap. The spectral function for single-particle excitations exhibits a collection of Fermi arcs and other structures. The arcs appear in various regions of the Brillouin zone, but never exclusively around the Brillouin zone diagonals.

### [122] [Putative quantum critical point in locally noncentrosymmetric CeCoGe$_2$ crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13111)
*F. Garmroudi,C. S. T. Kengle,M. H. Schenck,J. D. Thompson,E. D. Bauer,S. M. Thomas,P. F. S. Rosa*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究合成了CeCoGe₂单晶，发现其具有重费米子基态和非费米液体行为，但未观察到超导或磁有序。分析表明本征钴空位导致的随机势散射抑制了相干电荷输运和超导性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 局部非中心对称重费米子化合物可能产生长程关联量子相，如具有非阿贝尔准粒子的自旋三重态超导性，但识别合适的候选体系具有挑战性。本研究旨在探索CeCoGe₂单晶的量子物性。

Method: 采用In助熔剂法合成CeCoGe₂单晶，该化合物属于高度可调谐的赝四方CeTX₂家族。通过调控生长化学计量比和温度曲线，控制缺陷浓度并研究其对电阻率的影响。

Result: 发现重费米子基态，索末菲系数γ≈120 mJ mol⁻¹ K⁻²，电阻率呈现非费米液体指数行为，可能接近量子临界点。在20 mK以下未检测到超导或磁有序信号。本征钴空位（约4%）导致的强随机势散射抑制了相干电荷输运和超导性。

Conclusion: CeCoGe₂中的强随机势散射抑制了超导性，但通过控制缺陷浓度可以调节剩余电阻率。推测采用不同技术生长的高质量CeCoGe₂晶体中可能发现超导性。

Abstract: Locally noncentrosymmetric heavy-fermion compounds may produce long-sought correlated quantum phases, such as spin-triplet superconductivity with non-Abelian quasiparticles, but identifying the right candidate systems is challenging. Here, using the In flux method, we synthesize CeCoGe$_2$ single crystals, belonging to the highly tunable pseudotetragonal ($Cmcm$) Ce$TX_2$ family, which allows for substitutions at both the transition metal $T$ and at the $X$ sites. We identify a heavy-fermion ground state with a Sommerfeld coefficient $γ\approx 120$ mJ mol$^{-1}$ K$^{-2}$ and a non-Fermi-liquid exponent of the electrical resistivity, which may indicate its proximity to the putative quantum critical point. However, no signs of superconductivity or magnetic order are detected down to 20 mK. Our analysis of electrical transport and structural properties indicates that coherent charge transport and the emergence of superconductivity observed under hydrostatic pressure in related compounds (CePtSi$_2$ and CeRhGe$_2$) are suppressed in CeCoGe$_2$ by strong random potential scattering due to intrinsic Co vacancies (approximately 4% even in the highest-quality crystals). By tuning the growth stoichiometry and temperature profile, we demonstrate that the defect concentration can be controlled and has a pronounced effect on the residual resistivity. We hypothesize that superconductivity may be found in higher-quality CeCoGe$_2$ crystals grown by different techniques.

### [123] [Two-channel physics in a lightly doped antiferromagnetic Mott insulator revealed by two-hole spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13222)
*Pit Bermes,Sebastian Paeckel,Annabelle Bohrdt,Lukas Homeier,Fabian Grusdt*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过超高分辨率数值模拟，在强耦合掺杂莫特绝缘体的t-J模型中发现了两个耦合的空穴对分支，揭示了d波配对在SU(2)对称极限下的近共振相互作用特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解掺杂莫特绝缘体强耦合区域中的配对机制是铜氧化物超导体研究中的开放性问题。研究旨在探索t-J模型中低能区域的两粒子谱特征，以揭示非常规超导性的微观起源。

Method: 采用超高分辨率数值模拟方法，研究高度欠掺杂t-J模型中的谱函数。通过调节自旋各向异性，从Ising极限到SU(2)对称的海森堡区域，分析两粒子谱中的空穴对分支演化。

Result: 在低能区域发现两个耦合的空穴对分支，最低d波配对从单一双极化子分支演化为两个通过避免交叉分离的杂化分支。研究提出有效的双通道模型，涉及紧密束缚的双极化子态和与两个磁极化子相关的第二通道。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了超越单粒子格林函数的两粒子谱学作为揭示非常规超导性微观起源的有力工具。模型表明SU(2)对称t-J模型中存在近共振d波相互作用，与接近涌现的Feshbach型共振一致。

Abstract: Understanding pairing in the strong-coupling regime of doped Mott insulators remains an open problem in the context of cuprate superconductors. We perform ultra-high resolution numerical simulations of spectral functions in the highly underdoped $t-J$ model and discover two coupled branches of hole pairs emerging at low energies in the largely unexplored two-particle spectrum. As spin anisotropy is tuned from the Ising limit to the $SU(2)$-symmetric Heisenberg regime, the lowest $d$-wave pair evolves from a single bipolaronic branch into two hybridized branches separated by an avoided crossing. We explain this behaviour using an effective two-channel model involving a tightly bound bipolaronic state and a second channel associated with two magnetic polarons. The model reproduces the qualitative low-energy spectra and implies near-resonant $d$-wave interactions in the $SU(2)$-symmetric $t-J$ model, consistent with proximity to an emergent Feshbach-type resonance. To probe these predictions experimentally, we propose a Raman spectroscopy scheme for the attractive Hubbard model that can be directly implemented using ultracold atoms in optical lattices. Our work establishes two-particle spectroscopy, beyond single-particle Green's functions, as a powerful tool for revealing the microscopic origins of unconventional superconductivity.

### [124] [Lattice Discrete Particle Model (LDPM): Comparison of Various Time Integration Solvers and Implementations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13190)
*Erol Lale,Jan Eliáš,Ke Yu,Matthew Troemner,Monika Středulová,Julien Khoury,Tianju Xue,Ioannis Koutromanos,Alessandro Fascetti,Bahar Ayhan,Baixi Chen,Giovanni Di Luzio,Yuhui Lyu,Madura Pathirage,Gilles Pijaudier-Cabot,Lei Shen,Alessandro Tasora,Lifu Yang,Jiawei Zhong,Gianluca Cusatis*

TL;DR: 本文系统比较了晶格离散粒子模型（LDPM）在混凝土等准脆性材料数值模拟中的多种实现方案，包括瞬态隐式/显式求解器、稳态求解器以及CPU/GPU平台，通过一系列基准测试评估计算性能与精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在系统比较晶格离散粒子模型（Lattice Discrete Particle Model, LDPM）在不同求解器类型（瞬态隐式/显式、稳态）和计算平台（CPU/GPU）上的实现方案，为研究人员选择合适模拟方法提供参考依据。

Method: 通过一组描述计算复杂度递增行为的基准测试进行比较，包括弹性振动、约束应变硬化压缩响应、拉伸断裂和非约束应变软化压缩响应。采用宏观应力-应变响应、计算时间、迭代次数和能量平衡误差等指标进行评估。

Result: 研究提取了模拟中的关键性能指标，并通过相关系数和归一化均方根误差对最终裂纹模式进行成对比较。针对最具数值挑战性的非约束压缩滑动边界条件情况，通过扰动解、改变收敛准则和时间步长测试了应变软化响应的稳定性。

Conclusion: 论文提供了完整的基准测试输入数据，便于研究人员运行示例并与自身实现进行比较。大多数报告的实现方案已在开源软件包中公开可用，促进了LDPM模拟方法的标准化与验证。

Abstract: This article presents a comparison of various implementations of the Lattice Discrete Particle Model (LDPM) for the numerical simulation of concrete and other heterogeneous quasibrittle materials. The comparison involves the use of transient implicit and explicit solvers and steady-state (static) solvers and implementations for Central Processing Unit (CPU) as well as Graphics Processing Unit (GPU). The various implementations are compared on the basis of a set of benchmarks tests describing behaviors of increasing computational complexity. They include elastic vibrations, confined strain-hardening compressive response, tensile fracture, and unconfined strain-softening compressive response. Metrics of interest extracted from the simulations include macroscopic stress versus strain responses, computational times, number of iterations, and energy balance error. Pairwise comparison of final crack patterns is provided through the correlation coefficient and normalized root mean square error of the crack opening vectors. Moreover, for the most numerically challenging case of unconfined compression with sliding boundary conditions, the stability of the strain-softening response is tested by perturbing the solutions as well as changing the convergence criteria and time step size. Attached to this paper is the complete input data of the benchmark tests; this will allow researchers to run the examples and compare them with their own implementations. In addition, most of the reported implementations are publicly available in open source packages.

### [125] [IceCube Search for MeV Neutrinos from Mergers using Gravitational Wave Catalogs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13076)
*Nora Valtonen-Mattila*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: IceCube中微子观测站利用LVK引力波探测器O1-O3运行期数据，搜索来自致密双星并合（特别是含中子星的BNS和NSBH并合）的MeV中微子信号，未发现显著超出，但对GW170817等事件设定了迄今最强的MeV中微子发射上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 致密双星并合（特别是含至少一颗中子星的BNS和NSBH并合）在并合过程中会产生高温高密环境，可能产生热中微子暴（thermal neutrino burst）。通过引力波事件触发，可以针对性地搜索这些MeV能段的中微子信号，以探测并合过程的核物理和天体物理特性。

Method: 利用IceCube中微子观测站，在LVK引力波探测器O1、O2、O3运行期检测到的引力波事件周围，以并合时间为中心设置四个时间窗口，搜索探测器活动的短时增加。对含中子星和不含中子星的两类事件群体进行二项式检验（binomial test）。

Result: 未发现显著的中微子超出（no significant excess of neutrinos）。对每个事件设定了MeV中微子通量上限（upper limits on the MeV neutrino flux），并对含至少一颗中子星的并合事件给出了MeV中微子发射约束（constraints on MeV neutrino emission）。特别展示了首个确认的BNS并合事件GW170817的上限，这是迄今对此类源MeV中微子发射最强的限制之一。

Conclusion: 尽管未探测到来自致密双星并合的MeV中微子信号，但研究为含中子星并合事件的MeV中微子发射设定了严格的观测限制，特别是对GW170817事件的上限是目前最强的约束之一，为理解并合过程的物理机制提供了重要参考。

Abstract: We report on a search using the IceCube Neutrino Observatory for MeV neutrinos from compact binary mergers detected through gravitational waves during the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA (LVK) O1, O2, and O3 observing runs. The search focuses on events involving at least one candidate neutron star, such as binary neutron star (BNS) and neutron star--black hole (NSBH) mergers, which may produce a burst of thermal neutrinos due to the hot and dense conditions created during the merger. We looked for short-time increases in IceCube's detector activity around each gravitational-wave event, using four time windows centered on the merger time. We also performed a binomial test for two populations, those with and without at least one neutron star. No significant excess of neutrinos was found. We set upper limits on the MeV neutrino flux for each event, and we place constraints on MeV neutrino emission from mergers that have at least one neutron star. We showcase upper limits for GW170817, the first confirmed BNS merger, providing one of the strongest limits to date on MeV neutrino emission from such sources.

### [126] [Slowly Rotating Two-Fluid Neutron Stars: Coupled Frame-Dragging, Inertia Splitting, and Universal Relations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12613)
*Ankit Kumar,Hajime Sotani*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个完全相对论性框架，用于研究引力耦合双流体中子星在慢旋转近似下的旋转响应。该框架将两个组分视为独立守恒的完美流体，仅通过时空曲率相互作用，推导出耦合的平衡方程和框架拖曳方程，并利用其线性结构构建旋转响应的基分解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究引力耦合双流体中子星的旋转响应，特别是包含暗物质（dark matter）的中子星。旨在理解额外引力束缚组分如何修改全局旋转响应及其与潮汐形变（tidal deformability）的关系。

Method: 采用完全相对论性框架，在慢旋转近似（slow-rotation approximation）下处理两个独立守恒的完美流体（perfect fluids）。推导耦合的平衡方程和框架拖曳（frame-dragging）方程，利用线性结构构建旋转响应的基分解（basis decomposition）。

Result: 该框架导出了有效总转动惯量（effective total moment of inertia）的自然定义，推广了单流体概念且仅依赖于平衡背景。揭示了耦合系统存在两个本征转动惯量（eigen-moments of inertia）不同的本征旋转模（collective rotational eigenmodes）。应用于含暗物质中子星时，发现旋转-潮汐普适性（rotational-tidal universality）的保持或破坏由暗区微观物理而非额外组分的存在决定。

Conclusion: 建立了一个统一框架，用于解释多组分相对论性恒星中的旋转可观测量、本征模结构和普适关系。证明了旋转-潮汐普适性的命运取决于暗区微观物理细节，而非仅仅存在额外组分。

Abstract: We develop a fully relativistic framework to study the rotational response of gravitationally coupled two-fluid neutron stars within the slow-rotation approximation. Treating the two components as independently conserved perfect fluids interacting only through spacetime curvature, we derive the coupled equilibrium and frame-dragging equations and exploit their linear structure to construct a basis decomposition of the rotational response. This formulation leads to a natural definition of the effective total moment of inertia, which generalizes the single-fluid concept and depends solely on the equilibrium background. It further reveals that the coupled system admits two intrinsic collective rotational eigenmodes, characterized by distinct eigen-moments of inertia, even in the absence of relative rotation between the fluids. Applying this framework to neutron stars containing dark matter, we explore how the presence of an additional gravitationally bound component modifies the global rotational response and its relation to tidal deformability. Our results demonstrate that the persistence or breakdown of rotational-tidal universality in two-fluid neutron stars is governed by dark-sector microphysics rather than by the mere presence of an additional component, and establish a unified framework for interpreting rotational observables, intrinsic mode structure, and universal relations in multi-component relativistic stars.

</details>
