### [127] [Theory of the Matchgate Commutant](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12392)
*Piotr Sierant,Xhek Turkeshi,Poetri Sonya Tarabunga*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文解决了匹配门（matchgate）电路在量子信息理论中的复制对称性问题，通过Majorana费米子表示揭示了正交李代数结构，并构建了正交基，为费米子高斯态相关计算提供了系统工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子信息理论和统计物理中，系统多个副本（replicas）的对称性至关重要。对于酉系综（unitary ensembles），这些对称性编码在复制对易子（replicated commutant）中。虽然完整酉群的对易子容易确定，但对于结构化、计算相关的电路族（如匹配门电路），这仍是一个主要障碍。

Method: 使用Majorana费米子表示，证明耦合不同系统副本的算子生成正交李代数$\mathfrak{so}(k)$。通过Gelfand-Tsetlin构造完全解析了匹配门对易子的不可约扇区，并为所有$k$和$n$提供了显式的正交归一基。

Result: 完全解析了匹配门对易子的结构，提供了维度随$n$多项式增长的计算公式。刻画了Clifford-匹配门子群的对易子，发现当$k \geq 4$时其性质与匹配门情况存在质的不同。构建的正交基将代数分类转化为实用工具箱。

Conclusion: 该研究为费米子高斯态相关计算提供了系统框架，包括匹配门旋转通道（twirling channels）、费米子Weingarten微积分、高斯态轨道矩、非稳定性和非高斯性度量层次，以及费米子de Finetti定理等应用。

Abstract: In quantum information theory and statistical physics, symmetries of multiple copies, or replicas, of a system play a pivotal role. For unitary ensembles, these symmetries are encoded in the replicated commutant: the algebra of operators commuting with the ensemble across $k$ replicas. Determining the commutant is straightforward for the full unitary group, but remains a major obstacle for structured, computationally relevant circuit families. We solve this problem for matchgate circuits, which prepare fermionic Gaussian states on $n$ qubits. Using a Majorana fermion representation, we show that operators coupling different system copies generate the orthogonal Lie algebra $\mathfrak{so}(k)$, endowing the space of invariants with rich and tractable structure. This underlying symmetry decomposes the matchgate commutant into irreducible sectors, which we completely resolve via a Gelfand--Tsetlin construction. We provide an explicit orthonormal basis of the matchgate commutant for all $k$ and $n$, together with a formula for its dimension that grows polynomially in $n$. Furthermore, we characterize the commutant of the Clifford--matchgate subgroup, showing that restricting to signed permutations of Majorana modes yields a commutant that qualitatively diverges from the matchgate case for $k \geq 4$ replicas. Ultimately, our orthonormal basis turns algebraic classification into a working toolbox. Using it, we derive closed-form expressions for matchgate twirling channels and a fermionic analogue of Weingarten calculus, the projector encoding all moments of the Gaussian state orbit, state and unitary frame potentials, the average nonstabilizerness of fermionic Gaussian states, a systematic hierarchy of non-Gaussianity measures, and a fermionic de Finetti theorem.

</details>


### [128] [Asymptotic non-Hermitian degeneracy phenomenon and its exactly solvable simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13141)
*Miloslav Znojil*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文解释了PT对称虚立方振子缺乏一致量子力学解释的原因，揭示了其内在例外点（IEP）奇异性无法通过小扰动正则化，而传统例外点（EP）奇异性则可正则化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PT对称虚立方振子长期缺乏一致的量子力学概率解释，因为其哈密顿量被数学家证明具有内在例外点（intrinsic-exceptional-point, IEP）奇异性。本文旨在解释为何这类不可接受的量子模型无法通过小扰动方法进行正则化。

Method: 通过建立IEP奇异性与传统例外点（exceptional point, EP）的部分形式类比，构建了一个简化的N×N矩阵玩具模型哈密顿量。该模型允许渐近（即高激发）EP相关的波函数简并，在大N极限下模拟IEP类似物的若干方面。

Result: 研究发现EP奇异性可以通过大小为O(1/N)的特设扰动进行正则化，而IEP奇异性则无法类似正则化（需考虑N→∞极限）。这解释了为何基于小扰动的正则化方法对IEP奇异模型无效。

Conclusion: PT对称虚立方振子的IEP奇异性与常规EP奇异性存在本质差异：前者无法通过小扰动方法正则化，这解释了该模型长期缺乏一致量子力学解释的根本原因。

Abstract: Up to these days, the popular PT-symmetric imaginary cubic oscillator did not find any consistent probabilistic quantum-mechanical interpretation because its Hamiltonian has been shown, by mathematicians, intrinsic-exceptional-point (IEP) singular. In the paper we explain why there is even no reasonable small-perturbation-based regularization of the similar unacceptable (i.e., IEP-singular) quantum models. The explanation is based on a partial formal analogy of the IEP singularity with the conventional exceptional point (EP). What is important is that we are able to construct a simplified $N$ by $N$-matrix (and exactly solvable) toy-model Hamiltonian admitting the asymptotic (i.e., high-excitation) EP-related wave-function degeneracy which, in some sense (i.e., in the limit of large $N$) mimics several aspects of its IEP analogue. In this comparison, the difference is that the regularization of the EP singularities is possible (using an ad hoc perturbation of size ${\cal O}(1/N)$) while an analogous regularization of the IEP singularity is not (we have to consider $N \to \infty$).

</details>


### [129] [Emergent causal order and time direction: bridging causal models and tensor networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12283)
*Carla Ferradini,Giulia Mazzola,V. Vilasini*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究构建了因果模型与张量网络之间的双向映射框架，将无方向性的关联函数与操作性的信号传递概念联系起来，并应用于全息张量网络以分析涌现的因果结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探讨时间方向和时空因果结构是否可以从操作原则中推断出来。因果模型和张量网络提供了互补视角：前者通过有向图编码因果关系，具有内在顺序性；后者在无向图上描述多体系统，不预设方向性。

Method: 构建了因果模型与张量网络框架之间的双向映射（two-way mappings），将方向不可知的关联函数（direction agnostic correlation functions）与信号传递的操作概念联系起来。引入了因果模型的离散"时空旋转"（discrete space-time rotations），并应用因果推断工具如图分离（graph-separation）来分析涌现的因果结构。

Result: 该框架阐明了张量网络中因果影响的操作意义，并引入了保持信号传递关系的因果模型离散"时空旋转"。通过允许循环和不确定的因果结构（cyclic and indefinite causal structures），研究结果实现了张量网络与多种因果框架之间的技术转移。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一个统一框架，将因果模型与张量网络联系起来，为分析全息张量网络中的涌现因果结构提供了新工具，并促进了不同因果框架之间的技术交流。

Abstract: Can the direction of time and the causal structure of space-time be inferred from operational principles? Causal models and tensor networks offer complementary perspectives: the former encodes cause-effect relations via directed graphs, with intrinsic ordering; the latter describes multipartite systems on undirected graphs, without presupposing directionality. We construct two-way mappings between these two frameworks, linking direction agnostic correlation functions and operational notions of signalling. This clarifies the operational meaning of causal influence in tensor networks and introduces discrete "space-time rotations'' of causal models which preserve signalling relations. Applying our framework to holographic tensor networks, we use tools from causal inference, like graph-separation, to analyse emergent causal structures. By permitting cyclic and indefinite causal structures, our results enable transfer of techniques across tensor networks and a range of causality frameworks.

</details>


### [130] [Many-Body Entanglement Properties of Finite Interacting Fermionic Hamiltonians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11300)
*Irakli Giorgadze,Grayson Welch,Haixuan Huang,Elio J. König,Jukka I. Väyrynen*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文分析了相互作用费米子系统中的多体纠缠，证明了若粒子数守恒的费米子哈密顿量仅包含至多M体相互作用项，则其N粒子基态不能是最大M体纠缠的。研究还展示了基态的多体纠缠结构可对其母哈密顿量的相互作用强度施加定量约束，并在Hubbard和扩展SYK模型中验证了相关定理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于分析相互作用费米子系统中的多体纠缠结构，特别关注哈密顿量相互作用阶数与基态纠缠性质之间的关系。通过M体约化密度矩阵来量化多体纠缠，旨在建立哈密顿量结构与基态纠缠特性之间的理论联系。

Method: 研究方法基于M体约化密度矩阵分析多体纠缠。关键证明步骤显示，最大M体混合态的能量期望值等于哈密顿量在相应N粒子子空间上的谱均值。研究进一步在Hubbard模型和扩展SYK模型中验证定理及其推论。

Result: 主要结果证明：若粒子数守恒的费米子哈密顿量仅包含至多M体相互作用项，则其N粒子基态不能是最大M体纠缠的。研究还展示了基态纠缠结构可对母哈密顿量的相互作用强度施加定量约束，并分析了Slater行列式初态下幺正动力学中的纠缠生成。

Conclusion: 结论表明哈密顿量的相互作用阶数限制了其基态可能达到的最大纠缠程度。研究进一步推导了在阿贝尔对称性存在下M体纠缠的对称性细化饱和上界，为理解多体量子系统中的纠缠结构与哈密顿量特性之间的关系提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We analyze many-body entanglement in interacting fermionic systems by using the $M$-body reduced density matrix. We demonstrate that if a particle number conserving fermionic Hamiltonian contains only up to $M$-body interaction terms, then its $N$-particle ground state cannot be maximally $M$-body entangled. As a key step in the proof, we show that the energy expectation value of a maximally $M$-body mixed state is equal to the spectral mean of the Hamiltonian on the corresponding $N$-particle subspace. We further demonstrate that the many-body entanglement structure of a ground state can place quantitative constraint on the interaction strength of its parent Hamiltonian. We illustrate the theorem and its implications in Hubbard and extended SYK models. Going beyond ground states, we analyze entanglement generation under unitary dynamics from Slater-determinant initial states in these models. We determine early-time growth and estimate entanglement saturation times. Finally, we derive explicit symmetry-refined saturation upper bounds for $M$-body entanglement in the presence of an Abelian symmetry.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统超导量子比特读取中使用的非互易组件存在损耗、尺寸和磁场问题，而参数耦合模式网络虽可直接集成但缺乏对单量子系统的深入理解，因此需要开发新的理论工具来设计和分析此类集成系统。

Method: 研究开发了基于第一性原理的理论工具来理解和设计集成嵌入式量子比特的线性模式网络，并将该理论应用于指导和分析集成三模非互易系统的量子比特读取实验实现。

Result: 实验实现了集成非互易系统的量子比特读取，测量和退相干速率在理论与实验间达到良好一致性；理论分析预测同一系统作为集成非互易放大器运行时，在合理实验参数下可实现高效率。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了理解和设计集成量子比特的线性模式网络的理论框架，成功验证了集成非互易系统在量子比特读取中的应用，并展示了其在非互易放大器中的潜在高效率性能。

Abstract: High fidelity qubit readout is a cornerstone for quantum information protocols. In traditional superconducting qubit readout, a chain of microwave amplifiers and nonreciprocal components aid in detecting the qubit's state with tolerable added noise and backaction. However, the loss, size, and magnetic field of standard nonreciprocal components have sparked a decades-long search for more efficient and scalable alternatives. One prominent approach employs networks of parametrically coupled modes to achieve nonreciprocity. While this class of devices can be directly integrated with the qubit's readout cavity, current understanding of the resulting single quantum system is substantially lacking. Here we provide a first-principles theoretical tool to understand and design networks of linear modes integrated with embedded qubits. We utilize this theory to inform and analyze the experimental implementation of a qubit readout with an integrated three-mode nonreciprocal system. In doing so, we achieve excellent agreement between the experimental and theoretical qubit measurement and dephasing rates. We then theoretically analyze the same system operated as an integrated nonreciprocal amplifier, predicting high efficiency for reasonable experimental parameters.

### [132] [Quantum algorithms for compact polymer thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12334)
*Davide Rattacaso,Daniel Jaschke,Antonio Trovato,Ilaria Siloi,Simone Montangero*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于量子计算的紧凑聚合物热力学性质估算方法，通过构建局部母哈密顿量（local parent Hamiltonian）的独特基态实现对哈密顿环（Hamiltonian cycles）的量子采样，相比经典蒙特卡洛方法获得二次加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从哈密顿环系综中高效采样对于预测紧凑聚合物的热力学性质至关重要，在蛋白质和RNA折叠建模以及软材料设计中具有应用价值。经典蒙特卡洛方法在应用于紧凑聚合物时效率受到严重限制。

Method: 通过量子方程推理（quantum equational reasoning）构建局部母哈密顿量，其独特基态实现了所有哈密顿环的量子采样。该量子态可通过量子退火等基态制备方法在量子硬件上制备，并进一步操作以生成目标温度下的聚合物和杂聚物量子样本。

Result: 实现了紧凑聚合物和杂聚物热力学性质估算的二次加速。通过将量子样本近似为张量网络，揭示了纠缠面积定律（entanglement area law）。对于固定宽度的矩形晶格，获得了哈密顿环全系综的时间高效紧凑编码。

Conclusion: 该方法通过张量收缩实现了期望值、配分函数和构型概率的高效计算，无需依赖采样。量子计算为紧凑聚合物的热力学性质估算提供了显著的加速优势。

Abstract: Efficient sampling from ensembles of Hamiltonian cycles is critical for predicting the thermodynamic properties of compact polymers, with applications including modeling protein and RNA folding and designing soft materials. Although classical Monte Carlo methods are widely regarded as the standard approach, their efficiency is strongly limited when applied to compact polymers. In this work, we enable a quadratic speedup in the estimation of thermodynamic properties of maximally compact polymers and heteropolymers by quantum computation. To this end, we encode the target thermodynamic ensemble into the amplitudes of a quantum state, i.e., a quantum sample, which can be processed via amplitude amplification. Using quantum equational reasoning, we construct a local parent Hamiltonian whose unique ground state realizes a quantum sample of all Hamiltonian cycles. This state can be prepared on quantum hardware using ground-state preparation methods, such as quantum annealing, and subsequently manipulated to generate quantum samples of polymers and heteropolymers at a target temperature. Finally, we approximate the quantum sample as a tensor network, revealing an entanglement area law. For fixed-width rectangular lattices, we obtain a time-efficient and compact encoding of the full ensemble of Hamiltonian cycles, enabling the efficient evaluation of expectation values, partition functions, and configuration probabilities via tensor contractions, without resorting to sampling.

### [133] [Absence of Charge Offset Drift in a Transmon Qubit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12367)
*Adria Rospars,Hector Hutin,Yannick Seis,Cristóbal Lledó,Réouven Assouly,Romain Cazali,Rémy Dassonneville,Ambroise Peugeot,Alexandre Blais,Audrey Bienfait,Benjamin Huard*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文报道了一种基于钽（tantalum）的超导transmon量子比特，其电荷偏移（charge offset）在近三个月的测量中保持为零，包括两次热循环，且未观察到量子比特寿命的妥协。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导量子电路对其静电环境敏感：约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction）电极上积累的不可控电荷会改变量子比特的能级，干扰其操作并限制设计。这种效应由单一参数——电荷偏移（charge offset）——所捕获，其缓慢、不可预测的漂移在实践中难以消除。

Method: 研究采用基于钽的超导transmon量子比特，通过X射线表面光谱学（X-ray surface spectroscopy）分析表明，在制造过程中无意中在约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction）旁形成了薄的超导层。

Result: 电荷偏移在近三个月的测量中保持为零，包括两次热循环，且未观察到量子比特寿命的妥协。这种异常稳定性在后续的冷却过程中消失，表明存在脆弱的机制在起作用。

Conclusion: 该稳定性归因于制造过程中在约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction）旁无意形成的薄超导层的电感。X射线表面光谱学（X-ray surface spectroscopy）表明该层源于蓝宝石上钽的不完全湿法刻蚀（incomplete wet-etch）。有意设计这样的层为更广泛地消除超导电路中的电荷偏移漂移提供了途径。

Abstract: Superconducting quantum circuits are sensitive to their electrostatic environment: uncontrolled charges accumulating on the electrodes of a Josephson junction shift the energy levels of a qubit, perturbing its operation and restricting their design. This effect is captured by a single parameter - the charge offset - whose slow, unpredictable drift has proven difficult to eliminate in practice. Here, we report a tantalum-based transmon qubit in which the charge offset remains pinned at zero over nearly three months of measurements, including two thermal cycles, with no observable compromise to the qubit lifetime. This exceptional stability disappears in later cooldowns, indicating a fragile mechanism at play. We attribute it to the inductance of a thin superconducting layer inadvertently formed in parallel with the Josephson junction during fabrication. X-ray surface spectroscopy suggests this layer arises from an incomplete wet-etch of tantalum on sapphire. Deliberately engineering such a layer offers a route to eliminating charge-offset drift in superconducting circuits more broadly.

</details>


### [134] [Distributed Quantum Computing via Adaptive Circuit Knitting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12411)
*K. Grace Johnson,Aniello Esposito,Gaurav Gyawali,Xin Zhan,Rohit Ganti,Namit Anand,Raymond G. Beausoleil,Masoud Mohseni*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出自适应电路编织（Adaptive Circuit Knitting, ACK）方法，通过发现子系统间最小纠缠区域来高效划分量子电路，可将采样开销降低高达四个数量级，支持在多个量子处理单元（QPUs）上分布式执行大规模量子模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于单个量子处理单元（Quantum Processing Unit, QPU）的尺寸限制，将量子工作负载分布到多个QPU上是实现实用量子优势的关键步骤。在缺乏高保真量子互连的情况下，电路编织（circuit knitting）提供了一种仅使用经典通信在多个有限尺寸QPU上分布式计算大型量子系统特定属性的途径。

Method: 本文引入自适应电路编织（Adaptive Circuit Knitting, ACK）方法，通过发现子系统间最小纠缠区域来寻找量子电路的高效划分。该方法采用并行GPU加速实现，并模拟了1D和2D无序混合场伊辛模型（disordered mixed-field Ising models）至60量子比特规模。

Result: ACK方法可将电路编织采样开销降低高达四个数量级，适用于感兴趣的观测量（observables）。研究强调了高效经典模拟器对分布式量子算法开发的重要性，并展示了该技术在近期和容错架构中实现高效量子模拟分布的潜力。

Conclusion: 自适应电路编织技术能够实现量子模拟的高效分布，适用于近期和容错量子计算架构。该方法通过最小化子系统间纠缠来优化电路划分，显著降低了采样和经典后处理的开销。

Abstract: Distributing quantum workloads over many Quantum Processing Units (QPUs) is a crucial step in scaling up quantum computers toward practical quantum advantage due to the limitations in size of a single QPU. In the absence of high-fidelity quantum interconnects, circuit knitting could provide a path to computing certain properties of large quantum systems on many QPUs of limited size in a distributed fashion using only classical communication. Circuit knitting partitions large quantum circuits into manageable sub-circuits, however, reconstructing observables in a straightforward manner comes at an exponential cost in sampling and classical post-processing. To mitigate the overhead this technique incurs, we introduce an Adaptive Circuit Knitting (ACK) method that finds efficient partitions of quantum circuits by discovering regions of minimal entanglement between subsystems. We simulate 1D and 2D disordered mixed-field Ising models up to 60 qubits and show that the ACK approach can reduce circuit knitting sampling overheads by up to four orders of magnitude for observables of interest. We highlight our parallel GPU-accelerated implementation and discuss the need for efficient classical simulators to enable distributed quantum algorithm development. Our techniques could enable efficient distribution of quantum simulation for both near-term and fault-tolerant architectures.

</details>


### [135] [Doppler-induced tunable and shape-preserving frequency conversion of microwave wave packets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12436)
*Felix Ahrens,Enrico Bogoni,Renato Mezzena,Andrea Vinante,Nicolò Crescini,Alessandro Irace,Andrea Giachero,Gianluca Rastelli,Iacopo Carusotto,Federica Mantegazzini*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于动态多普勒效应（dynamic Doppler effect）的新型微波频率转换方法，利用传播前沿（propagating front）分离不同相速度（phase velocity）区域，实现了高达3.7%的频率偏移，同时完全保持微波波包（microwave wave packet）的时间形状。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在超导电子学（superconducting electronics）中，控制微波波包频率对于超导量子处理器（superconducting quantum processors）操作和超导传感器（superconducting sensors）读取等应用至关重要。传统基于频率混频（frequency-mixing）的方法存在局限性，需要新的频率转换技术。

Method: 采用高动感抗（high-kinetic-inductance）超导传输线（superconducting transmission line）的行波结构（travelling-wave geometry），通过传播前沿诱导的动态多普勒效应实现频率转换。该方法利用准直流电流（quasi-dc current）振幅连续调谐，并能对长时间波包的瞬时频率剖面（instantaneous frequency profile）施加任意模式。

Result: 实验实现了500 MHz和4 GHz微波波包高达3.7%的频率偏移，完全保持了波包的时间形状。与传统混频方法不同，该方法避免了杂散混频产物（spurious mixing products），且频率转换连续可调。

Conclusion: 通过设计允许更大相速度变化的传输线或级联多个多普勒诱导频率转换，理论上可实现无限量的频率偏移。该技术展示了作为先进微波波包控制工具在不同量子应用中的潜力。

Abstract: In superconducting electronics, the ability to control the frequency of microwave wave packets is crucial for several applications, such as the operation of superconducting quantum processors and the readout of superconducting sensors. We introduce a new approach to microwave frequency conversion harnessing a dynamic Doppler effect induced by a propagating front separating regions of different phase velocities. Employing a high-kinetic-inductance superconducting transmission line in a travelling-wave geometry, we were able to implement frequency shifts of microwave wave packets at 500 MHz and 4 GHz of up to 3.7 % while fully preserving their temporal shape. In contrast to conventional methods based on frequency-mixing, our Doppler-induced frequency-conversion method avoids spurious mixing products, is continuously tunable by a quasi-dc current amplitude, and allows to imprint arbitrary patterns on the instantaneous frequency profile of temporally long wave packets. By engineering transmission lines that allow for larger phase-velocity changes and/or by cascading multiple Doppler-induced frequency conversions, an unlimited amount of frequency shifting is in principle attainable. These features demonstrate the potential of our frequency-conversion technique as a promising tool for advanced control of microwave wave packets for different quantum applications.

Result: 研究发现参与熵和稳定子熵均表现出临界慢化（critical slowing down）：它们的饱和时间与系统尺寸呈线性关系，这与纯粹幺正动力学中饱和发生在对数时间尺度形成鲜明对比。二分参与和稳定子互信息显示出与纠缠熵相似的标度行为。通过对几个典型克利福德电路（Clifford circuits）的分析，发现在各自临界点附近存在类似的慢动力学行为。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，在非幺正量子电路动力学的临界线上，参与熵和稳定子熵表现出显著的临界慢化现象，其动力学时间尺度与系统尺寸呈线性关系。这一发现揭示了非幺正动力学在临界区域特有的慢弛豫特性，与幺正动力学形成本质区别。

Abstract: We study the participation and stabilizer entropy of non-unitary quantum circuit dynamics, focusing on the critical line that separates the low-entanglement spin-glass phase and the paramagnetic phase. Along this critical line, the entanglement has a logarithmic scaling, which enables us to access the critical regime using large-scale matrix product state simulations with modest bond dimension. We find that both the participation entropy and stabilizer entropy exhibit critical slowing down: their saturation time scales linearly with the system size, in stark contrast to purely unitary dynamics, where saturation occurs on logarithmic time scales. In addition, we study bipartite participation and stabilizer mutual information, and find that it shows similar scaling behavior to the entanglement entropy. Finally, by analyzing the participation entropy of several paradigmatic Clifford circuits, we identify similar slow dynamical behavior near their respective critical points.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，量子多体系统耦合到非平衡库时可能表现出活性物质行为，但由此产生的稳态高度混合且仅携带弱量子特征。本研究旨在探索在纯态系综中是否也能观察到活性物质的量子特征。

Method: 研究考虑了一个spinful Luttinger liquid，该系统受到将自旋向上粒子向左移动、自旋向下粒子向右移动的测量过程影响。通过分析弱监测强度和铁磁自旋相互作用条件下的系统行为。

Result: 在弱监测强度和铁磁自旋相互作用下，发现了自旋电流与电荷密度之间的幂律量子关联（power-law quantum correlations），这被识别为活性量子物质的标志性特征。监测过程具有双重作用：弱强度时产生量子活性关联，而较大强度时驱动Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless（BKT）相变到短程关联态。

Conclusion: 活性物质的特征不仅出现在耦合到非平衡库的量子多体系统中，也出现在经历监测量子动力学的纯态系综中。测量过程在产生量子活性关联和驱动相变方面扮演关键角色，为活性量子物质的研究提供了新视角。

Abstract: Quantum many-body systems coupled to out-of-equilibrium reservoirs can behave as active matter and exhibit signs of flocking. However, the resulting steady states are highly mixed and carry only weak quantum signatures. We show that signatures of active matter also arise in ensembles of pure states undergoing monitored quantum dynamics. We consider a spinful Luttinger liquid subject to measurement processes that shuffle spin-up particles to the left and spin-down particles to the right. For weak monitoring strengths and ferromagnetic spin interactions, we find power-law quantum correlations between spin current and charge density, which we identify as a hallmark of active quantum matter. The monitoring plays a dual role, generating the quantum active correlations for weak strengths while driving a Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless (BKT) phase transition to a shortrange correlated state at larger strengths.

Abstract: Many-body localization (MBL) provides a mechanism by which interacting quantum systems evade thermalization, leading to persistent memory of initial conditions and slow entanglement growth. Probing these dynamical signatures in large systems and at long evolution times remains challenging for both classical simulations and current quantum devices. Here we experimentally investigate the ergodic-MBL crossover in quasiperiodic Floquet Ising systems using up to 144 qubits on an IBM Quantum processor. By implementing deep Floquet circuits reaching up to 5000 cycles, we access long-time many-body dynamics beyond the regime explored in previous quantum computing experiments. Measurements of autocorrelation functions reveal a smooth crossover from rapid thermalization at weak quasiperiodic potential strength to persistent correlations in the strong-disorder regime. Notably, in addition to the one-dimensional system, we also observe clear signatures consistent with localization behavior in the two-dimensional system. Furthermore, the quantum Fisher information exhibits logarithmic growth over thousands of Floquet cycles, providing evidence for slow entanglement spreading characteristic of the MBL regime. These results demonstrate that programmable quantum processors can serve as experimental platforms for probing nonergodic quantum many-body dynamics and exploring localization phenomena in regimes beyond the reach of classical simulations.

### [140] [Quantum timekeeping and the dynamics of scrambling in critical systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13016)

Method: 通过将时间作为估计参数，推导了广义量子克拉美-罗界（generalized quantum Cramer-Rao bound），将时间估计精度与时间无序关联函数（out-of-time ordered correlators, OTOCs）衰减及子系统量子费舍尔信息（subsystem quantum Fisher information, QFI）联系起来。采用基于虚时间关联函数（imaginary-time correlators）的标度分析，并通过对混沌伊辛链（chaotic Ising chain）的数值分析进行验证。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了量子混沌与量子计量学之间的理论联系，揭示了信息扰频系统的局部子系统可作为有效的时间测量工具，其量子费舍尔信息特性与量子混沌动力学及相变临界行为密切相关。

Abstract: In this work, we develop a quantum metrological framework for quantum chaos by showing that local subsystems of information scrambling systems naturally function as quantum stopwatches. The reduced quantum state of a subsystem encodes the passage of time through its growing distinguishability from the initial preparation. Treating time as the estimation parameter, we then derive a generalized quantum Cramer-Rao bound that directly relates the precision of time estimation to the decay of out-of-time ordered correlators (OTOCs) and subsystem quantum Fisher information (QFI). As a main result, we obtain continuity bounds for quantum Lyapunov exponent in terms of the subsystem QFI in quantumly chaotic dynamics. Furthermore, using a scaling analysis based on imaginary-time correlators, we show that the subsystem QFI exhibits universal critical amplification near quantum phase transitions. Our results are demonstrated and verified by a numerical analysis of the dynamics of a chaotic Ising chain.

### [141] [Experimental realization of a $\cos(2\varphi)$ transmon qubit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13114)
*Erwan Roverc'h,Alvise Borgognoni,Marius Villiers,Kyrylo Gerashchenko,W. Clarke Smith,Christopher Wilson,Benoit Douçot,Alexandru Petrescu,Philippe Campagne-Ibarcq,Zaki Leghtas*

TL;DR: 该研究实现了基于cos(2φ)量子比特的超导电路，利用电荷宇称对称性（charge-parity symmetry）抑制电荷诱导误差，在软transmon（soft-transmon）工作模式下获得了100倍电荷矩阵元抑制，将电荷诱导损耗限制提升至10ms以上。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 实验采用cos(2φ)量子比特结构，由一个通过选择性传输Cooper对（Cooper pairs）对的隧穿元件接地的岛组成。在软transmon工作模式下运行，测量了量子比特的相干特性、单次读取（single-shot readout）能力，并观测了量子跳跃（quantum jumps）。

Result: 观测到13.6MHz的相反Cooper对宇称态双重态分裂，电荷诱导损耗被抑制至超出测量相干时间。相比未受保护的plasmon跃迁，岛电荷矩阵元被抑制100倍，将介电损耗限制提升至10ms以上。测得T₁=70μs和T₂^echo=2.5μs，主要受隧穿元件环路中1/f磁通噪声（1/f flux noise）限制。

Conclusion: 将Cooper对配对推入transmon工作模式能够为电荷诱导损耗设置高限制，同时保持对低频量子比特的相干控制和单次读取能力。磁通噪声被确定为剩余主要限制因素，需要梯度计设计（gradiometric designs）或新型4e隧穿元件（4e-tunneling elements）来解决。

Abstract: Superconducting circuits with embedded symmetries are good candidates to robustly protect quantum information from dominant error channels. The $\cos(2\varphi)$ qubit, consisting of an island shunted to ground through a tunneling element that selectively transmits pairs of Cooper pairs, leverages charge-parity symmetry to protect from charge-induced errors. In this experiment, we observe a doublet of states of opposite Cooper-pair parity split by $13.6~\mathrm{MHz}$. Operating in a soft-transmon regime, this splitting is two orders of magnitude smaller than in previous implementations, pushing charge-induced losses well beyond the measured coherence times. Despite the low transition frequency, we demonstrate coherent qubit control, single-shot readout, and resolve quantum jumps. Charge protection of the qubit is evidenced by a $100-$fold suppression of the island charge matrix element compared to the unprotected plasmon transition, placing dielectric loss limits above $10~\mathrm{ms}$. The measured $T_1 = 70~μ\mathrm{s}$ and $T_2^\mathrm{echo}= 2.5~μ\mathrm{s}$ are instead limited by $1/f$ flux noise in the tunnelling element's loop. This experiment shows that pushing Cooper-pair pairing in the transmon regime sets high limits on charge-induced losses while preserving coherent control and single-shot readout of the low-frequency qubit. We identify flux noise as the dominant remaining limitation, calling for gradiometric designs or novel $4e$-tunneling elements.

Motivation: 传统观点认为β相钽（β-Ta）因其较低的超导临界温度而不利于量子比特性能，但该研究旨在挑战这一普遍认知。β-Ta在室温下易于成核的特性使其在可扩展量子比特制造中具有吸引力。

Method: 研究通过在蓝宝石衬底上制备β-Ta薄膜来制造低损耗transmon量子比特。通过谐振器研究分析了主要的微波损耗通道，并测量了薄膜的动力学电感特性。

Result: 11个量子比特的平均时间平均品质因子为(5.6±2.3)×10^6，最佳量子比特达到(10.1±1.3)×10^6。研究表明主要微波损耗通道为表面双能级系统（surface two-level systems），β-Ta的表面损耗贡献约为α-Ta的两倍。β-Ta薄膜表现出显著的动力学电感，对应的磁穿透深度估计为(1.78±0.02)μm。

Conclusion: 该工作确立了蓝宝石上的β-Ta作为实现低损耗transmon量子比特的材料平台，同时也可用于紧凑谐振器、动力学电感探测器（kinetic inductance detectors）和准粒子陷阱（quasiparticle traps）等其他超导器件。

Abstract: Tantalum-based transmon qubits are a promising platform for building large-scale quantum processors. So far, these qubits have been made from tantalum films grown exclusively in the alpha phase (α-Ta). The beta phase of tantalum (\{beta}-Ta) readily nucleates at room temperature, making it attractive for scalable qubit fabrication. However, \{beta}-Ta is widely believed to be detrimental to qubit performance because it has a lower superconducting critical temperature than α-Ta. We challenge this prevailing belief by fabricating low-loss transmon qubits from \{beta}-Ta films on sapphire. Across 11 qubits, the mean time-averaged quality factor is (5.6 +/- 2.3) x 10^6, with the best qubit recording a time-averaged quality factor of (10.1 +/- 1.3) x 10^6. Resonator studies demonstrate that the dominant microwave loss channel is surface two-level systems, with the surface loss contribution for \{beta}-Ta being about twice that of α-Ta. \{beta}-Ta films exhibit significant kinetic inductance, consistent with an estimated magnetic penetration depth of (1.78 +/- 0.02) μm. This work establishes \{beta}-Ta on sapphire as a material platform for realizing low-loss transmon qubits and other superconducting devices such as compact resonators, kinetic inductance detectors, and quasiparticle traps.

</details>


### [143] [Quantifying surface losses in superconducting aluminum microwave resonators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13183)
*Elizabeth Hedrick,Faranak Bahrami,Alexander C. Pakpour-Tabrizi,Atharv Joshi,Q. Rumman Rahman,Ambrose Yang,Ray D. Chang,Matthew P. Bland,Apoorv Jindal,Guangming Cheng,Nan Yao,Robert J. Cava,Andrew A. Houck,Nathalie P. de Leon*

TL;DR: 该研究测量了超导铝谐振器中表面两能级系统（TLS）的微波吸收，发现铝谐振器寿命主要受限于2.7 nm厚天然AlOx中的TLS表面损耗，并估算铝界面TLS对先进钽-硅量子比特弛豫率的贡献约为27%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期钽-硅transmon量子比特实现毫秒级相干时间的研究表明，在高纯度超高真空环境中沉积Al/AlOx/Al约瑟夫森结对获得寿命受限的相干性至关重要，这促使研究者仔细研究铝表面两能级系统（TLS）浴。

Method: 采用为钽谐振器开发的方法学，测量超导铝谐振器中表面TLSs的微波吸收；通过改变薄膜和表面性质，并将微波测量与材料表征相关联；使用49% HF处理完全去除表面AlOx。

Result: 铝谐振器寿命主要受限于2.7 nm厚天然AlOx中的TLS表面损耗；HF处理虽能完全去除AlOx，但氧化物的快速再生长限制了表面损耗的改善和器件长期稳定性；铝界面TLSs对先进钽-硅量子比特弛豫率的贡献约为27%。

Conclusion: 铝表面TLSs是超导谐振器和量子比特性能的重要限制因素，天然AlOx中的TLS损耗主导铝谐振器性能，且对含铝约瑟夫森结的先进量子比特弛豫率有显著贡献。

Abstract: The recent realization of millisecond-scale coherence with tantalum-on-silicon transmon qubits showed that depositing the Al/AlOx/Al Josephson junction in a high purity, ultrahigh vacuum environment was critical for achieving lifetime-limited coherence, motivating careful examination of the aluminum surface two-level system (TLS) bath. Here, we measure the microwave absorption arising from surface TLSs in superconducting aluminum resonators, following methodology developed for tantalum resonators. We vary film and surface properties and correlate microwave measurements with materials characterization. We find that the lifetimes of superconducting aluminum resonators are primarily limited by surface losses associated with TLSs in the 2.7 nm-thick native AlOx. Treatment with 49% HF removes surface AlOx completely; however, rapid oxide regrowth limits improvements in surface loss and long term device stability. Using these measurements we estimate that TLSs in aluminum interfaces contribute around 27% of the relaxation rate of state-of-the-art tantalum-on-silicon qubits that incorporate aluminum-based Josephson junctions.

### [144] [Transition Waves for Energy Trapping and Harvesting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13046)
*Sneha Srikanth,Andres F. Arrieta*

Main category: nlin.PS

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了利用多稳态力学超材料中的过渡波锁定机制实现能量捕获和冲击吸收，同时展示了该系统在能量收集方面的多功能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多稳态力学超材料（multistable mechanical metamaterials）中的多稳态特性和非线性现象（如迟滞）为实现频率无关的能量收集和冲击吸收提供了可能。本研究旨在探索通过锁定过渡波（transition waves）来捕获能量并实现冲击吸收的机制。

Method: 采用一维双稳态单元链（one-dimensional chain of bistable units）作为多稳态超材料模型，其过渡波动力学与由φ⁴方程（φ⁴ equation）描述的拓扑孤立波（topological solitary waves）相关。通过数值模拟和实验验证能量捕获效果，并与线性超材料进行对比。

Result: 研究表明，通过过渡波捕获能量能够显著提升阻尼性能，优于相应的线性超材料。实验证实多稳态超材料能同时实现改进的能量收集和更好的阻尼性能。此外，还提出了增加过渡波能量捕获的设计变体，并识别了能量分裂（energy splitting）作为一种阻尼机制。

Conclusion: 利用过渡波创建多功能多稳态超材料具有显著优势，能够同时实现冲击吸收和能量收集的双重功能。该研究为设计具有能量捕获和阻尼性能的多功能材料提供了理论依据和实验验证。

Abstract: The presence of multiple stable states and associated nonlinear phenomena, such as hysteresis, in multistable mechanical metamaterials enables frequency-independent energy harvesting and shock absorption. This study focuses on shock absorption achieved by locking transition waves to trap energy at designed locations within a multistable metamaterial. We further demonstrate that the same system can simultaneously harvest energy from impact loading, thereby exhibiting multifunctionality. The model of the multistable metamaterial is a one-dimensional chain of bistable units whose transition wave dynamics are related to topological solitary waves governed by the $φ^4$ equation. This connection enables analytical estimation of critical design parameters required for energy trapping and also the amount of energy trapped. Numerical simulations and experiments show that trapping energy in transition waves leads to enhanced damping performance compared to corresponding linear metamaterials. We further propose design variations to increase the amount of energy trapped in the transition wave. Additionally, we identify energy splitting as a damping mechanism that arises when there are repeated impulses or a single high-amplitude impulse that generates multiple transition waves. The transition waves interact to produce localized, fast-dissipating breathers, leading to a damped response. Furthermore, experiments demonstrate that multistable metamaterials can simultaneously achieve improved energy harvesting and better damping performance compared to their linear counterparts. Together, these results highlight the use of transition waves for creating multifunctional multistable metamaterials.

### [145] [EB-RANSAC: Random Sample Consensus based on Energy-Based Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12525)
*Muneki Yasuda,Nao Watanabe,Kaiji Sekimoto*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机抽样一致性（RANSAC）作为最流行的鲁棒估计方法之一，基于对数据集的重复采样。本研究旨在提出一种改进方法，避免RANSAC中繁琐的采样过程并减少超参数数量。

Method: 提出基于能量模型的RANSAC（EB-RANSAC），该方法采用与RANSAC相似的框架，但通过能量模型（energy-based model, EBM）实现，无需重复采样过程，且仅需一个超参数。

Result: EB-RANSAC在数值实验中展示了有效性，特别是在两个应用场景中：线性回归（linear regression）和最大似然估计（maximum likelihood estimation）。该方法适用于与RANSAC相似的广泛估计问题。

Conclusion: EB-RANSAC作为一种基于能量模型的鲁棒估计方法，保持了RANSAC的广泛适用性，同时避免了繁琐的采样过程并简化了超参数设置，在多种估计问题中表现出有效性。

Abstract: Random sample consensus (RANSAC), which is based on a repetitive sampling from a given dataset, is one of the most popular robust estimation methods. In this study, an energy-based model (EBM) for robust estimation that has a similar scheme to RANSAC, energy-based RANSAC (EB-RANSAC), is proposed. EB-RANSAC is applicable to a wide range of estimation problems similar to RANSAC. However, unlike RANSAC, EB-RANSAC does not require a troublesome sampling procedure and has only one hyperparameter. The effectiveness of EB-RANSAC is numerically demonstrated in two applications: a linear regression and maximum likelihood estimation.

### [146] [A theory of learning data statistics in diffusion models, from easy to hard](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12901)
*Lorenzo Bardone,Claudia Merger,Sebastian Goldt*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文揭示了扩散模型（diffusion models）在学习自然图像时表现出分布简单性偏差（distributional simplicity bias），即先学习简单的成对统计量（pair-wise statistics），再学习高阶相关性（higher-order correlations）。作者通过混合累积量模型（mixed cumulant model）精确控制输入统计量，并提出了扩散信息指数（diffusion information exponent）这一标量不变量来解释学习复杂度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管扩散模型已成为一类强大的生成模型，但其学习动态机制仍未被充分理解。本文旨在通过实证和理论分析揭示扩散模型学习复杂分布的具体机制，特别是其学习简单统计量与高阶相关性时的不同样本复杂度。

Method: 首先通过实证研究展示标准扩散模型在自然图像训练中表现出的分布简单性偏差。随后在混合累积量模型（mixed cumulant model）上训练简单去噪器（denoisers），该模型允许精确控制输入的成对统计量和高阶相关性。作者提出了扩散信息指数（diffusion information exponent）这一标量不变量来量化学习复杂度。

Result: 研究发现去噪器以线性样本复杂度学习输入的简单成对统计量，而更复杂的高阶统计量（如第四累积量）至少需要立方样本复杂度。然而，当成对统计量与高阶统计量共享相关潜在结构时，学习第四累积量的样本复杂度可降至线性。

Conclusion: 本文描述了扩散模型学习复杂度递增分布的关键机制，揭示了其先学习简单统计量再学习高阶相关性的学习动态。扩散信息指数为理解不同统计量的学习复杂度提供了理论框架，并解释了当统计量共享潜在结构时样本复杂度的降低现象。

Abstract: While diffusion models have emerged as a powerful class of generative models, their learning dynamics remain poorly understood. We address this issue first by empirically showing that standard diffusion models trained on natural images exhibit a distributional simplicity bias, learning simple, pair-wise input statistics before specializing to higher-order correlations. We reproduce this behaviour in simple denoisers trained on a minimal data model, the mixed cumulant model, where we precisely control both pair-wise and higher-order correlations of the inputs. We identify a scalar invariant of the model that governs the sample complexity of learning pair-wise and higher-order correlations that we call the diffusion information exponent, in analogy to related invariants in different learning paradigms. Using this invariant, we prove that the denoiser learns simple, pair-wise statistics of the inputs at linear sample complexity, while more complex higher-order statistics, such as the fourth cumulant, require at least cubic sample complexity. We also prove that the sample complexity of learning the fourth cumulant is linear if pair-wise and higher-order statistics share a correlated latent structure. Our work describes a key mechanism for how diffusion models can learn distributions of increasing complexity.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对于粉末样品，解释共振非弹性X射线散射（resonant inelastic X-ray scattering, RIXS）谱强度仍然具有挑战性，因为测量信号是所有取向的平均值。现有理论方法主要依赖球张量形式（spherical-tensor formalisms），通常涉及复杂推导和特定案例分析。

Method: 提出一个通用理论框架，将笛卡尔坐标（Cartesian coordinates）跃迁张量转换为粉末样品物理上有意义的取向平均强度。该形式体系允许从头计算（ab initio）预测X射线吸收谱（XAS）和RIXS的角度和偏振依赖性。

Result: 该框架的预测结果与Ce L₃边的RIXS实验数据表现出极好的一致性，证明其有效性。该形式体系还可扩展到其他光谱技术。

Conclusion: 本文发展的理论框架为粉末样品XAS和RIXS谱强度解释提供了通用解决方案，利用量子化学方法在笛卡尔坐标中准确计算跃迁张量，简化了取向平均强度的预测过程。

Abstract: X-ray absorption spectroscopy (XAS) and resonant inelastic X-ray scattering (RIXS) are powerful probes of electronic structure owing to their chemical and orbital selectivity. For powder samples, however, interpreting RIXS spectral intensities remains challenging as the measured signal is an average over all orientations. Existing theoretical treatments rely largely on spherical-tensor formalisms, which often involve complex derivations and case-specific analyses. Meanwhile, recent advances in quantum-chemistry methods have made the evaluation of transition tensors in Cartesian coordinates both accurate and straightforward. Here, we present a general theoretical framework that translates Cartesian transition tensors into physically meaningful, orientation-averaged intensities for powder samples. The formalism allows predicting angular and polarization dependences \textit{ab initio} for both XAS and RIXS and is extendable to other spectroscopies. The resulting predictions show excellent agreement with RIXS experimental data at the Ce L$_3$ edge.

### [148] [Optimal Experimental Design for Reliable Learning of History-Dependent Constitutive Laws](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12365)
*Kaushik Bhattacharya,Lianghao Cao,Andrew Stuart*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种贝叶斯最优实验设计框架，用于可靠学习历史依赖本构模型（history-dependent constitutive models）。通过量化、解释和最大化实验设计的效用，该框架能够显著提高参数可识别性，特别是在记忆效应相关参数方面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 历史依赖本构模型作为微观力学聚合效应的宏观闭合，其参数通常从实验数据中学习。然而，有限的实验预算使得获取完整响应范围来表征本构关系变得困难，导致参数估计存在不确定性或不可靠性。

Method: 提出了一个贝叶斯最优实验设计（Bayesian optimal experimental design）框架，将设计效用定义为参数不确定性的预期减少或预期信息增益。引入了两个关键近似：预期信息增益的高斯近似（Gaussian approximation）和费雪信息矩阵（Fisher information matrix）的代理近似，使得该框架适用于具有昂贵正向模型和高维数据的先进材料测试。

Result: 对粘弹性固体（viscoelastic solids）单轴试验的数值研究表明，优化的试样几何形状和加载路径产生的图像和力数据，相对于随机设计显著提高了参数可识别性，特别是与记忆效应相关的参数。

Conclusion: 该贝叶斯最优实验设计框架能够通过计算机模拟进行设计优化，降低物理实验成本，实现可靠参数识别，特别适用于历史依赖本构模型的学习。

Abstract: History-dependent constitutive models serve as macroscopic closures for the aggregated effects of micromechanics. Their parameters are typically learned from experimental data. With a limited experimental budget, eliciting the full range of responses needed to characterize the constitutive relation can be difficult. As a result, the data can be well explained by a range of parameter choices, leading to parameter estimates that are uncertain or unreliable. To address this issue, we propose a Bayesian optimal experimental design framework to quantify, interpret, and maximize the utility of experimental designs for reliable learning of history-dependent constitutive models. In this framework, the design utility is defined as the expected reduction in parametric uncertainty or the expected information gain. This enables in silico design optimization using simulated data and reduces the cost of physical experiments for reliable parameter identification.
  We introduce two approximations that make this framework practical for advanced material testing with expensive forward models and high-dimensional data: (i) a Gaussian approximation of the expected information gain, and (ii) a surrogate approximation of the Fisher information matrix. The former enables efficient design optimization and interpretation, while the latter extends this approach to batched design optimization by amortizing the cost of repeated utility evaluations. Our numerical studies of uniaxial tests for viscoelastic solids show that optimized specimen geometries and loading paths yield image and force data that significantly improve parameter identifiability relative to random designs, especially for parameters associated with memory effects.

</details>


### [149] [First-principles study of doping influence on twin formation in Ni-Mn-Ga nonmodulated martensite](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12413)
*Petr Šesták,Martin Heczko,Ladislav Straka,Alexei Sozinov,Martin Zelený*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过密度泛函理论计算了化学掺杂对Ni-Mn-Ga马氏体孪晶形成能垒的影响，揭示了掺杂位点依赖性效应：某些掺杂降低孪晶形核与扩展能垒，而另一些则提高能垒阻碍孪晶形成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究化学掺杂如何改变非调制（NM）Ni-Mn-Ga马氏体中孪晶形成的能量学，探索不同掺杂元素和位点对孪晶行为的影响机制。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory）计算化学计量比Ni₂MnGa及掺杂超胞的广义平面缺陷能（generalized planar fault energy, GPFE）曲线，分析(101)[10̄1]剪切系统中的孪晶形成能垒。

Result: 掺杂效应具有强烈的位点依赖性：Cu→Mn、Cu→Ni、Co→Ni和Zn→Mn掺杂降低形核能垒并软化GPFE曲线，有利于孪晶形成；而Cu→Ga、Co→Mn、Co→Ga、Fe→Ga和Zn→Ga掺杂则提高GPFE能垒阻碍孪晶形成。Fe→Mn对能垒影响较小，Fe→Ni产生异常GPFE响应。

Conclusion: 化学掺杂通过改变广义平面缺陷能景观和四方度c/a来调控孪晶行为，某些掺杂促进孪晶形成而另一些则阻碍孪晶形成，这与掺杂增强马氏体稳定性的传统目标存在权衡关系。

Abstract: We investigate how chemical substitution reshapes the energetics of twin formation in non-modulated (NM) Ni-Mn-Ga martensite. Using density functional theory, we compute generalized planar fault energy (GPFE) curves for the $(101)[10\bar{1}]$ shear system in stoichiometric Ni$_{2}$MnGa and in a set of doped supercells containing Cu, Co, Fe, or Zn on different sublattices. The GPFE landscape is used as a microscopic descriptor of twinning behavior: the first barrier reflects intrinsic stacking-fault formation (twin nucleation), whereas subsequent barriers govern twin thickening and boundary motion. We show that the impact of dopants is strongly site dependent. Substitutions Cu$\rightarrow$Mn, Cu$\rightarrow$Ni, Co$\rightarrow$Ni, and Zn$\rightarrow$Mn lower the nucleation barrier and generally soften the GPFE profile, indicating more favorable conditions for twin formation and propagation; these cases also correlate with a reduced tetragonality $c/a$, which implies a smaller twinning shear and a reduced energetic cost of twin formation. In contrast, Cu$\rightarrow$Ga, Co$\rightarrow$Mn, Co$\rightarrow$Ga, Fe$\rightarrow$Ga, and Zn$\rightarrow$Ga increase GPFE barriers and hinder twinning, even though such substitutions are often used to enhance martensite stability and raise $T_{m}$. Fe$\rightarrow$Mn leaves barrier heights largely unchanged, while Fe$\rightarrow$Ni produces an anomalous GPFE response indicative of unstable twin configurations. Finally, inspired by the nanotwinning characterisation of 10M/14M modulation, we link the depth of the two-layer nanotwin minimum to modulation stability. The substitutions Fe$\rightarrow$Mn, Cu$\rightarrow$Ni, and Zn$\rightarrow$Mn result in a lower energy minimum compared to the structure without the double-layered twin. The other substitutions favor the twin-free NM structure.

</details>


### [150] [Structural flexibility dictates reactivity of single-atom catalysts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12424)
*Jakub Planer,Dominik Hrůza,Tadeáš Lesovský,Ayesha Jabeen,Jan Čechal,Zdeněk Jakub*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单原子催化剂（single-atom catalyst）反应性来源是异相催化（heterogeneous catalysis）研究的核心挑战。关键问题在于活性是仅源于原子隔离，还是来自单原子独特的结构和电子构型。

Method: 在惰性载体上精确合成Fe-N₃和Fe-N₄模型催化剂位点，结合密度泛函理论（density functional theory）计算和原子分辨扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunneling microscopy）实验，量化配位几何结构对化学反应性的影响。

Result: 尽管Fe-N₃和Fe-N₄位点具有相同电子构型（高自旋Fe²⁺，S=2）且d轨道占据和费米能级位置几乎相同，但CO吸附能差异超过0.6 eV。这种反应性差异源于Fe-N₃位点的结构灵活性，通过铁原子从-N₃平面抬起增强了Fe 3dₓᵧ/ᵧᶻ-CO 2π*反键作用。

Conclusion: 配位几何结构在定义单原子催化剂反应性中起关键作用，仅通过位点电子结构分析无法预测这种效应。这为理解单原子催化剂反应性来源提供了新视角。

Abstract: Unravelling the origins of single-atom catalyst reactivity is a central challenge in heterogeneous catalysis research. A key question is whether the activity arises solely from atomic isolation or from distinct structural and electronic configurations of the single atoms. Here, we use precisely defined Fe-N$_3$ and Fe-N$_4$ model catalyst sites synthesized on an inert support to quantify the effect of coordination geometry on chemical reactivity. Both the Fe-N$_3$ and Fe-N$_4$ models have the same electronic configuration (high-spin Fe$^{2+}$ with S=2), and even their d-orbital occupancies and positions with respect to Fermi level are almost identical. Despite this electronic similarity, the adsorption energy of CO differs by more than 0.6 eV between the Fe-N$_3$ and Fe-N$_4$ sites, as indicated by density functional theory computations and confirmed by atomically-resolved scanning tunneling microscopy experiments. We trace this reactivity difference to the structural flexibility of the Fe-N$_3$ sites, which allows strengthening of the Fe 3d$_{xz/yz}$-CO 2$π$* back-bonding by lifting the Fe atom from the -N$_3$ plane. These results demonstrate that coordination geometry plays a crucial role in defining the reactivity of single-atom catalysts, and that such effects cannot be predicted by analysis of the sites' electronic structures alone.

</details>


### [151] [Xe gas bubble re-solution in U-10Mo nuclear fuel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12491)
*ATM Jahid Hasan,Linu Malakkal,Mathew Swisher,Benjamin Beeler*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过二元碰撞近似（BCA）和分子动力学（MD）模拟，量化了U-10Mo燃料中氙（Xe）气泡的再溶解（re-solution）速率，发现电子阻止（electronic stopping）产生的热峰（thermal spikes）对再溶解无贡献，而核阻止（nuclear stopping）是主要机制，再溶解速率与气泡压力呈反比关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 美国高性能研究堆（High-Performance Research Reactor）计划旨在将高功率研究堆从高浓铀（highly enriched uranium）转换为使用整体式U-10Mo燃料的低浓铀（low-enriched uranium）。裂变气体气泡行为是U-10Mo燃料性能的关键方面，其演化受气体原子捕获（trapping）和辐照诱导"再溶解"（re-solution）速率之间的相互作用控制，直接影响燃料性能和安全。

Method: 采用二元碰撞近似（BCA）和分子动力学（MD）模拟来量化U-10Mo燃料中的氙气泡再溶解速率。首先评估了裂变碎片（fission fragments, FFs）通过电子阻止和核阻止的能量损失，然后使用MD模拟结合双温模型（two-temperature model）分析电子阻止对再溶解的影响。通过BCA模拟获取裂变碎片的平均入射概率、能量和角度随距离的变化，并评估不同能量和气泡半径下的FF-气泡相互作用。

Result: 结果表明，电子阻止产生的热峰对U-10Mo中的气体气泡再溶解没有贡献。在平衡气泡压力下，单位裂变率密度的总体再溶解速率b值范围为：最大气泡的4.4×10⁻²⁶ m³/裂变到最小气泡的8.8×10⁻²⁵ m³/裂变。气泡压力对再溶解速率的影响分析显示两者呈反比关系。

Conclusion: 研究量化了U-10Mo燃料中氙气泡的再溶解速率，明确了核阻止是再溶解的主要机制，而电子阻止贡献可忽略。再溶解速率与气泡压力的反比关系为理解燃料性能提供了重要参数，对高性能研究堆的燃料设计和安全评估具有指导意义。

Abstract: The U.S. High-Performance Research Reactor program aims to convert high-power research reactors from highly enriched uranium to low-enriched uranium using a monolithic U-10Mo fuel design. A critical aspect of U-10Mo fuel performance is fission gas bubble behavior. These bubbles grow by trapping gas atoms (particularly Xe) but can disintegrate via irradiation-induced "re-solution". The interplay between the trapping and re-solution rates governs bubble evolution, impacting fuel performance and safety. In this study, binary collision approximation (BCA) and molecular dynamics (MD) simulations were performed to quantify the Xe gas bubble re-solution rate in U-10Mo fuel. First, the energy loss of fission fragments (FFs) through electronic and nuclear stopping was evaluated. The effect of electronic stopping on re-solution was then analyzed using MD simulations coupled with the two-temperature model. Results indicate that thermal spikes generated by electronic stopping do not contribute to gas bubble re-solution in U-10Mo. To quantify re-solution due to nuclear stopping, BCA simulations of FFs in U-10Mo were performed to obtain the average FF incidence probability, energy, and angle as a function of distance from the FF origin. Subsequent simulations assessed FF--bubble interactions in U-10Mo for different FF energies and bubble radii. From these analyses, an overall re-solution rate $b$ was calculated at equilibrium bubble pressure per unit fission rate density, yielding values ranging from $4.4 \times 10^{-26}$ m$^3$/fission for the largest bubbles to $8.8 \times 10^{-25}$ m$^3$/fission for the smallest. The effect of bubble pressure on the re-solution rate was also evaluated, revealing an inverse relationship between the two.

</details>


### [152] [Ferroaxial magnets: time-reversal-even mirror symmetry violation from spin order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12502)

Abstract: We investigate ferroaxial magnets, a new class of spin-order-driven multiferroic magnets in which magnetic ordering induces mirror-symmetry breaking while preserving both time-reversal and spatial-inversion symmetries. These systems exhibit a ferromagnet-like axial anisotropy that allows optical control of the ferroaxial polarization, while their macroscopic time-reversal symmetry makes them attractive for antiferromagnetic spintronics. Using spin crystallographic group analysis, we identify the candidate materials and the nonrelativistic ferroaxial nature stemming from the strong exchange splitting of magnets. Furthermore, a symmetry-based identification shows magnetic materials that host ferroaxial order and metallic conductivity, realizing the ferroaxial metal state that undergoes a ferroaxial phase transition while remaining metallic. As a direct probe for the ferroaxial metal, we propose a third-order nonlinear Hall effect originating from the transverse coupling between the electric field and Berry curvature dipole mediated by the ferroaxial anisotropy. Our results establish ferroaxial magnets as a platform for nonrelativistic multiferroicity and spintronic applications.

### [153] [Accelerating materials discovery using foundation model based In-context active learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12567)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 研究表明，预训练的基础模型可以作为高效的代理模型，显著加速基于主动学习的材料发现过程。TabPFN通过其原则性贝叶斯推断和良好校准的预测uncertainty，解决了传统代理模型在小数据材料发现场景中的关键局限。

Abstract: Active learning (AL) has emerged as a powerful paradigm for accelerating materials discovery by iteratively steering experiments toward the most promising candidates, reducing costly synthesis-and-characterization cycles. However, current AL relies predominantly on Gaussian Process (GP) and Random Forest (RF) surrogates with complementary limitations: GP underfits complex composition--property landscapes due to rigid kernel assumptions, while RF produces unreliable uncertainty estimates in small-data regimes, precisely where most materials datasets reside (with < 500 samples). Here we propose foudaiton model based In-Context Active Learning (ICAL), replacing conventional surrogates with TabPFN, a transformer-based foundation model pre-trained on millions of synthetic tasks to meta-learn a universal prior over tabular data. TabPFN performs principled Bayesian inference in a single forward pass without dataset-specific retraining, delivering well-calibrated predictive uncertainty where GP and RF fail most severely. Benchmarked against GP and RF across 10 materials datasets spanning copper alloy hardness and electrical conductivity, bulk metallic glass-forming ability, and crystal lattice thermal conductivity, TabPFN wins on 8 out of 10 datasets, achieving a mean saving of 52\% in extra experiments/evaluations relative to GP and 29.77% relative to RF. Cross-validation analysis confirms that TabPFN's advantage stems from superior uncertainty calibration,achieving the lowest Negative Log-Likelihood and Area Under the Sparsification Error curve among all surrogates. Our work demonstrates that a pre-trained foundation model can serve as a highly effective surrogate for accelerating active learning-based materials discovery.

Abstract: Alternating (AC) magnetic fields can induce not only an alternating magnetization in materials, but also an alternating temperature via the magnetocaloric effect. In order to address this, we have developed a method to measure the AC magnetocaloric effect that is compatible with AC susceptibility measurements, and also a framework to analyze these data in combination. We demonstrate the efficacy of this approach using YbVO4, a material for which strong single-ion anisotropy leads to slow spin-lattice relaxation at low temperatures via a phonon bottleneck effect. We analyze the data using a discretized thermal model, and extract the field-dependence of the intrinsic spin-lattice relaxation rate. This demonstration experiment illustrates a general approach to quantitatively address multiple measured quantities in driven systems using a unified thermal circuit analysis. The thermal analysis methods presented in this report can be extended to study other magnetic, dielectric, and elastic materials exhibiting a complex response to an external driving field in the presence of internal and external relaxation, particularly when an energy dissipation process is within an accessible frequency regime.

Abstract: Excitons in the weakly interacting regime can be well-described by many-body perturbation theories such as the Bethe-Salpeter equation formalism. However, for materials such as transition metal dichalcogenides moiré heterostructures under strong illumination, with the emergence of dense excitonic states, the strong correlation and entanglement between electrons and holes may cause the many-body perturbation method to fail, and excitons may not be treated in the bosonic picture, but exhibit fermionic behaviors. In our work, we investigate the phase space where excitons, and the electrons and holes which constitute them, are weakly or strongly entangled, as well as their binding for different interaction profiles and the degree of localization of the electrons and holes. We corroborate the validity of using many-body perturbation theory in the exciton with interactions. Our work provides a general way to analyze the correlation and entanglement of multi-particle excitations in many-body systems, and gives a more comprehensive understanding of different phases for exciton entanglement and interactions in 1D systems.

### [158] [Quantifying Perovskite Solar Cell Degradation via Machine Learning from Spatially Resolved Multimodal Luminescence Time Series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12857)
*Giulio Barletta,Simon Ternes,Saif Ali,Zohair Abbas,Chiara Ostendi,Marialucia D'Addio,Erica Magliano,Pietro Asinari,Eliodoro Chiavazzo,Aldo Di Carlo*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于深度学习框架LumPerNet的方法，通过多模态发光成像（电致发光和光致发光）直接评估钙钛矿太阳能电池的效率保持率，实现了非侵入式的器件健康监测和加速稳定性测试。

Abstract: Perovskite solar cells (PSCs) have experienced a remarkable rise in power conversion efficiency (PCE) over the past 15 years, positioning them as a promising alternative or complement to silicon for large-scale photovoltaic deployment. However, beyond scalable fabrication, operational stability remains a major bottleneck for commercialization. Reliable and rapid methods to assess device health and degradation mechanisms - ideally compatible with field applications - are therefore essential. We present a deep-learning framework to estimate efficiency retention, $R_\mathrm{PCE}=\mathrm{PCE}_t/\mathrm{PCE}_0$, directly from multimodal luminescence imaging acquired during device aging. Each training sample includes electroluminescence (EL), open-circuit photoluminescence (PLoc), and short-circuit photoluminescence (PLsc) images at an aged state, together with device-specific reference images at $t=0$. This design enables the model to learn spatially resolved degradation patterns relative to the pristine condition. The dataset was collected over 5-70 hours using an automated, in-house measurement platform. We introduce LumPerNet, a compact convolutional neural network that regresses $R_\mathrm{PCE}$ from stacked multimodal image tensors, and benchmark it against an intensity-only multilayer perceptron baseline. Using a leakage-aware protocol with device-level hold-out testing and four-fold cross-validation, restricted to $R_\mathrm{PCE}\in[0.8,1.2]$, LumPerNet achieves substantially improved and more robust performance (MAE -23.4%, RMSE -25.6%, $R^2$ +0.417). Ablation studies highlight the importance of complementary physical contrast across modalities for generalization. Overall, this work establishes a reproducible pipeline linking automated luminescence imaging to electrical labels, enabling accelerated stability testing and non-invasive degradation monitoring in PSCs.

Conclusion: 竞争性交换相互作用和基态（ground states）拓宽了同一范德华材料中通过外部参数变化产生不同类型磁振子激发的可能性，磁振子-磁振子耦合（magnon-magnon coupling）和面内各向异性（in-plane anisotropies）对激发特性有重要影响。

Abstract: Magnonic excitations are investigated in chromium oxychloride (CrOCl), a van der Waal (vdW) antiferromagnet prone to a multitude of magnetic phase transitions, with absorption experiments in a broad continuous energy range. At low magnetic fields, the magnon spectra show a strong bi-axial anisotropy and inform on the relative weights of the effective exchange coupling and the system anisotropies. As the magnetic field increases, magnons characteristic of a canted phase are first observed, with peculiarities attributed to in-plane anisotropies and magnon-magnon coupling. Subsequently, a hysteretic magnon spectrum appears as the system transitions to a ferrimagnetic state, with two new magnon branches partly coexisting with the lower energy canted phase branch, indicating the formation of spatially separated magnetic phases. Further changes in the magnon spectrum in higher magnetic fields accompany transitions to the different canted magnetic phases previously reported. Our experiments show that competing exchange interactions and ground states broaden the options to generate different kinds of magnonic excitations in the same vdW material upon the variation of external parameters.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Understanding how practical lithium storage capacity varies with charge-discharge rate is crucial for designing durable anode free lithium batteries. We examine the lithiation behavior of single element metal electrodes-Al (alloying), Mg (solid solution intercalation), Ag (solid solution then alloying), and Cu (surface Li plating)-to determine how their mechanisms influence reversibility, measured by coulombic efficiency. Using electrochemistry combined with depth resolved ion beam profiling, we map local coulombic efficiency across current densities and identify dominant lithium loss pathways. Ag uniquely sustains fast kinetics and high reversibility at elevated rates due to rapid formation of gamma brass-type alloy phases. In contrast, Mg and Al show increasing irreversibility from kinetically or structurally driven Li trapping, while Cu exhibits the largest losses through porous, highly reactive plated lithium. These results reveal fundamental limits of anode free systems that depend on reversible Li plating without excess lithium and underscore the importance of metal selection for stable, high rate performance.

### [164] [A Spatial Localizer for Electrons in Insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13206)
*Haylen Gerhard,Yifan Wang,Alexander Cerjan,Wladimir A. Benalcazar*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然一维绝缘体中存在确定电子局域态表示的方案，但在更高维度缺乏可比拟的通用理论。电子位置分布对从化学键合、电极化到能带绝缘体的拓扑分类及量子物质中关联态涌现等现象至关重要。

Method: 引入基于空间局域化算子（Spatial Localizers）谱特性的通用框架，用于寻找二维和三维绝缘体中电子的位置分布。该框架将Wannier中心概念自然扩展到具有边界、缺陷和杂乱的绝缘体系统。

Result: 该框架建立了电子电荷的体-缺陷对应（bulk-defect correspondence）的位置空间表述，并产生了最大局域化的电子态。在原子绝缘体中，这些态简化为最大局域化的Wannier函数；在陈绝缘体中，它们形成反映量子霍尔效应中朗道能级相干态结构的相干态。

Conclusion: 提出的空间局域化算子框架为确定高维绝缘体中电子位置提供了通用理论，统一处理了从原子绝缘体到拓扑绝缘体的各类系统，并建立了体-缺陷对应的位置空间表述。

Abstract: The location of electrons governs phenomena ranging from chemical bonding and electric polarization to the topological classification of band insulators and the emergence of correlated states in quantum matter. While a prescription exists for finding local state representations of electrons in one-dimensional insulators, no comparably general theory exists in higher dimensions. Here, we introduce a general framework for finding the location of electrons in insulators in two and three dimensions based on the spectral properties of quantum-mechanical operators that we term Spatial Localizers. This framework naturally extends the notion of Wannier centers to insulators with boundaries, defects, and disorder, which we use to establish a position-space formulation of the bulk-defect correspondence for electronic charge. This framework also yields maximally localized electronic states. As two representative examples, we show that these states reduce to maximally localized Wannier functions in atomic insulators, whereas in Chern insulators they form coherent states that mirror the coherent-state structure of Landau levels in the quantum Hall effect.

### [165] [Electromechanical Hysteresis in Phase Change Material Sb2S3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13221)
*Jack Kaman,Evan Musterman,Kyle P. Kelley,Neus Domingo-Marimon,Volkmar Dierolf,Himanshu Jain*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 锑硫化物（antimony sulfide, Sb2S3）作为一种新兴相变材料，在光学和电学存储与计算元件中具有应用潜力。先前研究报道其具有铁电性，但这一结论主要基于压电响应力显微镜（piezoresponse force microscopy, PFM）中的迟滞现象，而玻璃态Sb2S3理论上应禁止压电耦合。

Method: 研究对共晶结晶（congruently crystallized）的Sb2S3玻璃陶瓷进行了系统的压电响应力显微镜实验。通过对比玻璃态Sb2S3与晶态区域的响应，分离了压电信号与非压电贡献，并分析了施加电压引起的信号来源。

Result: 实验复现了先前观察到的迟滞行为，但发现该响应在玻璃态Sb2S3中不存在，主要源于施加电压引起的非压电贡献。这种迟滞行为与某些电化学活性非铁电氧化物相似，但具有独特的空间对比度，且与表面形貌解耦，表明电机械信号反映了体相性质。

Conclusion: 研究证实Sb2S3中观察到的压电响应力显微镜信号主要来自非压电机制，而非本征铁电性。这揭示了晶态与非晶态Sb2S3相在电学行为上的差异，对准确理解该材料的电学性质具有重要意义。

Abstract: Antimony sulfide is an emerging phase change material for optical and electrical memory and computation elements. It has additionally been reported as a ferroelectric, with recent evidence from hysteresis in piezoresponse force microscopy. Here, we complete a rigorous set of piezoresponse force microscopy experiments on a congruently crystallized Sb2S3 glass-ceramic, where piezoelectric coupling should be forbidden in glassy Sb2S3. We replicate previous results and reveal that the behavior is absent in glassy Sb2S3 but show that the response originates primarily from non-piezoelectric contributions to the signal caused by an applied voltage. This hysteretic behavior in piezoresponse force microscopy is quite similar to some electrochemically active non-ferroelectric oxides, but uniquely, it appears here with a very clear spatial contrast that is decoupled from surface topography. This shows that the electromechanical signal reflects bulk-like properties and reveals differences in electrical behavior of crystalline and amorphous phases of Sb2S3.

</details>
